| **Description** | Run 033 narrows C5 from **"piece (a) signer landed; pieces (b) peer key-provider and (c) production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution remain"** to **"pieces (a) signer and (b) peer key-provider both landed honestly. Piece (c) production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution remains under C4."** The new `--validator-consensus-key VID:SUITE:HEXPK` flag (Append; multiple entries) is the smallest additive shape that covers local + every `--p2p-peer vid@addr` peer with explicit `(validator_id, suite_id, public_key_bytes)` triples; it is **strictly orthogonal to** transport-level KEMTLS root-key distribution and does NOT claim to solve it. The provider builder fail-closes on every documented invariant: empty config (`NoConfiguredKeys` — preserves Run 032 path), invalid hex (no `0x` prefix, even length, hex-only), unsupported suite (≠ ML-DSA-44), duplicate `validator_id`, `--p2p-peer vid@addr` peer with no matching key (`PeerMissingKey`), bare `--p2p-peer addr` without `vid@` on the multi-validator path (`PeerWithoutValidatorId`), no local key when no signer is loaded (`LocalKeyMissing`), explicit local entry whose bytes disagree with the keystore-derived signer public key (`LocalKeyMismatchesSigner` — fingerprints only, no key bytes), and any `ConsensusValidatorSet::new` rejection (`ValidatorSetBuildFailed`). When both halves are honestly populated, `main.rs` calls real `try_build_timeout_verification_context(TimeoutVerificationBridgeInputs { validators, key_provider, backend_registry: ML-DSA-44 SimpleBackendRegistry, chain_id, signer, local_validator_id })` and threads the resulting `Arc<TimeoutVerificationContext>` into `BinaryConsensusLoopIo::verification_ctx` — so `qbind_timeout_verification_active 1` only when verification is honestly active, never when it is fabricated. Twenty Run 030 deterministic loop-API tests, the existing 20 `timeout_verification_bridge` tests, eleven `signer_loader` tests, twenty-two new `peer_key_provider` tests (parser strict-hex × 6, builder positives × 3, builder negatives × 7, fingerprint safety × 1, suite dedup × 1, bridge-activation integration × 3, optional/required-mode × 2, unknown-validator × 1), eight new CLI parser tests for `--validator-consensus-key` (valid, missing parts, bad vid, bad suite, empty/odd-length hex, propagation, default-empty, p2p-peer regression), all 9 vm_v0_runtime snapshot-trigger tests, t144/t145/t153 keystore integration suites, b7/b8/b12 transport-config tests, and t172/t175 P2P smoke + config tests all pass — full `qbind-node` lib **725 / 725 passing**, up from 693. |
| **Impact** | Materially narrower than Run 032. Operators who declare production-grade consensus intent via `--require-timeout-verification` and configure both `--signer-keystore-path` (Run 032) **and** `--validator-consensus-key VID:SUITE:HEXPK` (Run 033, one per active validator) now see `qbind_timeout_verification_signer_loaded 1`, `qbind_timeout_verification_key_provider_loaded 1`, `qbind_timeout_verification_validator_count N`, and **`qbind_timeout_verification_active 1`** with `Arc<TimeoutVerificationContext>` honestly threaded into `BinaryConsensusLoopIo::verification_ctx`. Operators with one half but not the other (or with malformed keys) get a precise startup error naming the missing/invalid piece and refusing to start under `RequireOrFail`. The remaining production gap is exclusively C4 piece (c) — production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution. **No claim is made that consensus public-key distribution is a substitute for transport PKI.** No claim is made that full C4 is closed. No fake/test-grade peer keys are silently accepted as production. |
| **Resolution path** | (1) ~~Wire `config.signer_keystore_path` → `Arc<dyn ValidatorSigner>`~~ — **landed in Run 032**. (2) ~~Extend `NodeConfig.network` with per-peer `(suite_id, pk_bytes)` and construct a `SuiteAwareValidatorKeyProvider` over the active validator set~~ — **landed in Run 033** as `network.static_peer_consensus_keys: Vec<StaticPeerConsensusKey>` + CLI `--validator-consensus-key VID:SUITE:HEXPK`. (3) ~~Replace the Run 032 signer-only probe site with real `try_build_timeout_verification_context(...)` when all pieces are present~~ — **landed in Run 033** in `main.rs::run_p2p_node`. (4) Land production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution from C4 so the underlying transport identity binding is not on B12's test-grade `TrustedClientRoots`/`DummySig` — **still OPEN**. (5) ~~Run an N=4 Required-mode real-binary B14 absent-leader recovery with verified timeout traffic and capture per-reason `/metrics` snapshots and rejection counters~~ — **landed in Run 034**. (6) ~~Real-binary forged-traffic negative injection (in-process injection harness or fake-peer rig)~~ — **landed in Runs 035 + 036**: Run 035 added the smallest opt-in dev/test-only `--devnet-forged-inject` harness (hidden from `--help`; gated by `--env devnet` + `QBIND_DEVNET_FORGED_INJECTION=1` + explicit case tokens; refuses Testnet/Mainnet/non-P2P/missing-env-var/unknown-case-token; injects into the same `mpsc::Sender<ConsensusNetMsg>` channel used by live P2P; never calls engine methods directly; never reads/writes/fabricates metrics; 21 forged-injection unit tests + full lib 746/746 pass). Run 036 then ran the live N=4 Required-mode real-binary forged-injection evidence on V0 with all 12 cases and confirmed: forged frames are rejected fail-closed before engine ingestion (`inbound_timeout_engine_accepted_total=0`, `inbound_newview_engine_accepted_total=0` at the T+4s forged-only scrape on V0); no view advance from forged traffic (`view_timeout_advances_total=0` and `view_advances_due_to_verified_tc_total=0` at T+4s); per-reason `inbound_*_rejected_*` counters frozen at the value implied by the case mix from T+4s through graceful shutdown — i.e. honest traffic never exercised any rejection path; V0 stayed alive (rc=0); and the post-injection B14 absent-leader recovery still drove 4 view advances all attributed to verified TCs, 3 fresh TimeoutCertificates, `outbound_timeout_signing_failure_total=0` on every live validator, and `committed_height 88→138` on V2A/V3A past the absent-leader plateau. Documented boundary: 3 NewView cases (`insufficient-quorum`, `mixed-view`, `high-qc-mismatch`) collapse onto the `bad_signature` counter at the live binary path because the harness uses fresh ML-DSA-44 keypairs; deterministic per-reason coverage for those cases lives in Run 030 / Run 035 unit tests. (7) An adversary-with-valid-keys harness or fake-peer transport rig that lets those 3 NewView cases fire their own per-reason live counter — **still OPEN, but no longer in the way of C5/C4 closure** because per-reason coverage is already proven deterministically. |
| **Tests** | `crates/qbind-consensus/src/timeout_verify.rs::tests::*` (Run 028); `crates/qbind-consensus/src/timeout.rs::tests::timeout_certificate_serializes_signed_timeouts`, `tests::timeout_accumulator_tc_carries_exact_signed_evidence` (Run 029); `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs::tests::run030::*` (20 tests, Run 030); `crates/qbind-node/src/timeout_verification_bridge.rs::tests::*` (20 tests, 15 Run 031 + 5 Run 032); `crates/qbind-node/src/signer_loader.rs::tests::*` (11 tests, Run 032); `crates/qbind-node/src/peer_key_provider.rs::tests::*` (22 tests, Run 033: 6 strict-hex parser tests, 3 builder positives, 7 builder negatives, 1 fingerprint safety, 1 suite-id stability, 1 unknown-validator, 3 bridge-activation integration tests with real ML-DSA-44 keypairs, plus optional/required-mode + matching-local-entry tests); `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs::tests::run_033_*` (8 tests); existing T144/T145/T153 integration suites unchanged. Run 031/032/033 evidence: `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_031.md`, `_RUN_032.md`, `_RUN_033.md`. |

DevNet Evidence Run 039 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_039.md`) further narrows C4/C5 for the transport-root dependency: `pqc-static-root` Required mode now registers real ML-KEM-768 (`KEM_SUITE_ML_KEM_768 = 100`) instead of `DummyKem`, validates local `NetworkDelegationCert.leaf_kem_pk` + `--p2p-leaf-cert-key` by strict size checks and an encaps/decaps public/secret-key match, and requires explicit certified peer leaf certs (`--p2p-peer-leaf-cert VID:PATH`) before using a peer KEM public key. Run 039 real-binary evidence passed a two-node Required + `pqc-static-root` smoke and an N=4 Required + `pqc-static-root` + `--require-timeout-verification` absent-leader-shaped run with real ML-DSA-44 certs, real ML-KEM-768 KEM, active timeout verification, post-fault `committed_height 79 -> 100`, `current_view 82 -> 105`, timeout/NewView verify accepted counters increasing, and rejection/proposal/invalid-vote counters remaining zero. Negative smokes for mismatched ML-KEM secret, malformed KEM secret, and tampered cert failed closed. `DummyKem` remains available only through explicit test/dev `test-grade-dummy-sig` paths; it is not registered in `pqc-static-root`. C4 remains OPEN because `DummyAead` is still active and CA / rotation / revocation / signed root distribution remain unsolved. The Run 038 `qbind_p2p_pqc_*` live `/metrics` exposure gap remains OPEN; Run 039 uses startup logs for KEM activation proof.

DevNet Evidence Run 040 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_040.md`) further narrows C4/C5 by replacing `DummyAead` with the real `ChaCha20Poly1305Backend` on the `pqc-static-root` Required-mode binary path. `make_pqc_static_root_crypto_provider` in `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` now registers `Arc::new(ChaCha20Poly1305Backend::new())` at suite id `AEAD_SUITE_CHACHA20_POLY1305 = 101` (no `DummyAead` registered on this provider; `provider.aead_suite(2).is_none()` is asserted directly), and `P2pNodeBuilder::build` selects `aead_suite_id = 101` whenever `pqc_active`. The startup log changes from `[Run039]` to `[Run040]` and additionally prints `transport_aead_suite_id=101 transport_aead_suite_name=chacha20-poly1305 dummy_aead_registered=false` on the pqc-static-root path (and the inverted shape `transport_aead_suite_name=dummy-aead dummy_aead_registered=true` on the explicit `test-grade-dummy-sig` default, preserving B7/B8/B12 / T138 / T143 / T160 / T222 etc. bit-for-bit). The KEMTLS key schedule (`crates/qbind-net/src/keys.rs::SessionKeys::derive`) and transcript binding are unchanged — `aead_suite_id` is already mixed into HKDF info and `key_len()` remains 32 — so a mismatched suite id between dialer and listener fails closed at handshake and at the first encrypted frame. The 12-byte `flag(1)||session_id(3)||counter(8)` nonce layout in `crates/qbind-net/src/session.rs` matches ChaCha20-Poly1305's 96-bit nonce; `AeadSession` keys are zeroized on drop. Run 040 real-binary evidence: a two-node `MutualAuthMode::Required` + `PqcRootMode::PqcStaticRoot` + real ML-DSA-44 cert + real ML-KEM-768 KEM + real ChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD handshake completes through the production `P2pNodeBuilder` path with both sides observing each other's cert-derived `NodeId`; the `[Run040] ... transport_aead_suite_name=chacha20-poly1305 dummy_aead_registered=false` startup log was captured live. Negative coverage: AEAD wrong-key, wrong-nonce, wrong-AAD, tampered-ciphertext, tampered-tag, truncated-frame, malformed-key-length, and malformed-nonce-length all fail closed (14 `chacha20poly1305::tests::*` + 9 new R040.B tests + the existing `kemtls_encrypted_transport_tests::real_aead_detects_ciphertext_tampering`); Run 037 tampered-cert / untrusted-root / wrong-sig-suite cases still fail closed; Run 039 mismatched-ML-KEM-secret / missing-peer-leaf-cert cases still fail closed; no silent fallback to `DummyAead`, `DummyKem`, or `DummySig` in `pqc-static-root`. Tests: 14 new R040.A/B/C/D tests pass; full `qbind-node` lib **767 / 767**; `qbind-crypto` lib **68 / 68** (incl. all 14 ChaCha20-Poly1305 fail-closed tests); `qbind-net` lib **15 / 15**; existing run_037 (12), t138 (15), t139 (4), kemtls_handshake_concurrency (8), kemtls_encrypted_transport (8), t160 cluster harness (7) suites all green. **Boundary explicitly stated:** end-to-end live tampered-encrypted-frame injection on the two-node binary surface is not exercised in this run because no in-process encrypted-frame injection harness exists on the Run 037/038/039 path; AEAD authentication-failure coverage is therefore via the provider/primitive tests, which exercise the same `ChaCha20Poly1305Backend` instance the binary now registers on its `StaticCryptoProvider`. **C4 remains OPEN** for: production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle (operator-out-of-band, not solved), `qbind_p2p_pqc_*` live `/metrics` exposure (Run 038/039 OPEN gap, not addressed by Run 040 — Run 040 relies on the deterministic `[Run040]` startup log + provider-shape unit tests + the two-node handshake test as AEAD-active proof), production fast-sync/consensus-storage restore, and exponential-backoff timeout pacing. **C5's remaining transport-root dependency is now satisfied for: real ML-DSA-44 cert verification (Run 037), real ML-KEM-768 KEM (Run 039), real AEAD (Run 040), active timeout verification (Runs 031–034), and forged-traffic rejection evidence (Runs 035/036).** C5 itself remains OPEN only because lifecycle (CA / rotation / revocation / signed root distribution) is documented as a C4 piece, NOT a C5 piece — so Run 040 does NOT close C5 by fiat; closure is contingent on at least the operator-facing lifecycle policy being explicitly accepted as out of C5 scope. Operators using `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` post-Run-040 are operating production-honest cert verification + production-honest transport KEM + production-honest transport AEAD, but lifecycle remains operator-out-of-band and is NOT a substitute for production CA tooling.

## Undocumented Implementation Details

### 1. In-Memory Slashing Ledger (T230)

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M1/M19)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-ledger/src/slashing_ledger.rs:713-1466` (`RocksDbSlashingLedger`) |
| **Evidence** | Persistent slashing ledger implemented via `RocksDbSlashingLedger`. Provides restart-safe persistence for validator slashing state, evidence records, and penalty history. Atomic updates via `apply_slashing_update_atomic()` using RocksDB `WriteBatch` (M1.2). Failure injection tests verify atomicity (M1.3). **M19**: Added `verify_slashing_consistency_on_startup()` for fail-closed corruption detection, explicit consensus-critical vs non-critical classification in docs, and comprehensive M19 test suite. Whitepaper Section 16.8 updated with full persistence model. |
| **Tests** | `crates/qbind-node/tests/m1_slashing_persistence_tests.rs`, `crates/qbind-ledger/tests/slashing_ledger_tests.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/tests/m19_slashing_persistence_canonicalization_tests.rs` |

### 2. Vote History Memory Limits

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M20)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-consensus/src/hotstuff_state_engine.rs:107-122` (`votes_by_view`, eviction tracking) |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 8.4.1 (Vote History Retention) |
| **Description** | The vote history (`votes_by_view` HashMap) is bounded with memory limits and eviction (`evict_votes_by_view_if_needed()`). Whitepaper Section 8.4.1 now documents that equivocation detection is best-effort over a sliding window and very old views may no longer be checked. |
| **Security Impact** | Protocol safety unchanged (locking rule and QC formation guarantee safety independent of historical vote tracking). Very old double-votes may not be slashable if their view has been evicted—acceptable trade-off to prevent unbounded memory growth. |

### 3. CRC-32 Checksum for Storage Integrity

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M20)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-node/src/storage.rs:256-336` (`compute_crc32()`, `wrap_checksummed()`, `unwrap_checksummed()`) |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 10.5.1 (Storage Integrity Checksums) |
| **Description** | Storage uses CRC-32 checksums (IEEE 802.3 polynomial) for integrity detection. Whitepaper Section 10.5.1 now documents that checksums detect bit-rot and accidental corruption but are non-cryptographic; adversarial tampering must be handled at higher layers (signatures, QCs, consensus verification). |

### 4. Epoch Transition Write Ordering

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M12, M16)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-node/src/storage.rs`, Whitepaper Section 18.4.3 |
| **Evidence** | Epoch transition write ordering and persistence semantics formally specified in Whitepaper Section 18 "Validator Set Transition and Epoch Boundary Semantics" (M12). Section 18.4.3 defines persistence ordering: storage commits before in-memory state update. **M16**: Crash-window elimination now proven by 14 tests with failure injection. All epoch-boundary writes (block, QC, last_committed, epoch) commit atomically via RocksDB WriteBatch. `EpochTransitionMarker` detects incomplete transitions on startup with fail-closed behavior. |

### 5. Key Rotation Grace Period Semantics

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M20)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-consensus/src/key_rotation.rs:238-298` |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 9.8 (Key Rotation Semantics) |
| **Description** | Key rotation uses an epoch-aligned grace period where both old and new keys are valid during transition. Whitepaper Section 9.8 now documents: (1) partial-epoch rotations not supported, (2) both keys valid for grace epoch, (3) security trade-off of simpler reasoning vs. slower key turnover. |

### 6. DAG Mempool Batch Priority

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M20)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-node/src/dag_mempool.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/src/mempool.rs` |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 7.1.1 (Mempool Ordering Semantics) |
| **Description** | Mempool priority uses `arrival_id` which differs per node. Whitepaper Section 7.1.1 now documents: (1) batch selection deterministic per node but depends on local arrival order, (2) transaction ordering within blocks is proposer-determined, not globally canonical, (3) consensus safety unaffected—economic fairness (block inclusion) is proposer-local. |

### 7. Timeout Exponential Backoff Parameters

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M20)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-consensus/src/pacemaker.rs:74-109` (`TimeoutPacemakerConfig` with `timeout_multiplier: 2.0`, `max_timeout: 30s`) |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 17.3.1 (Exponential Backoff Parameters) |
| **Description** | The timeout pacemaker uses configurable exponential backoff. Whitepaper Section 17.3.1 now documents: (1) default multiplier 2.0× and max timeout 30 seconds, (2) parameters are environment-tunable, (3) must remain bounded and deterministic for safety and cross-node consistency. |

### 8. Evidence Signature Verification Not Performed

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M9/M11)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-consensus/src/slashing/mod.rs:579-594` (`verify_ml_dsa_44_signature()`), lines 664-682 (O1 verification), 762-769 (O2 verification), 860-865 (O3 verification), 945-951 (O4 verification) |
| **Evidence** | Cryptographic signature verification IS implemented for all offense types. `verify_ml_dsa_44_signature()` performs ML-DSA-44 signature verification on evidence payloads. O1 verifies both block signatures; O2 verifies header signature invalidity; O3 verifies vote signature; O4 verifies certificate signatures. Deterministic verification with fail-closed behavior on non-verifiable evidence. |

### 9. Governance Slashing Parameters Not Connected

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **RESOLVED (M14)** |
| **Implementation** | `crates/qbind-types/src/state_governance.rs:44-117` (`SlashingPenaltySchedule` struct with O1-O5 parameters), `crates/qbind-consensus/src/slashing/mod.rs:2260-2370` (`PenaltyEngineConfig::from_governance_schedule()`, `GovernanceSlashingSchedule` type) |
| **Whitepaper Reference** | Section 11 (Governance) |
| **Description** | `ParamRegistry` now contains a canonical `SlashingPenaltySchedule` with all O1-O5 penalty parameters. `PenaltyEngineConfig::from_governance_schedule()` creates engine configurations directly from governance state. Slashing parameters are governed and upgradeable with epoch-boundary activation semantics. |
| **Evidence** | M14 implementation: (1) `SlashingPenaltySchedule` stores slash_bps and jail_epochs for O1-O5 plus activation_epoch, (2) `GovernanceSlashingSchedule` provides interface between types crate and consensus crate, (3) `PenaltyEngineConfig::from_governance_schedule()` constructs configs deterministically, (4) DevNet allows fallback defaults; TestNet/MainNet require schedule presence (fail-closed). |
| **Tests** | `crates/qbind-node/tests/m14_governance_slashing_params_tests.rs` (15 tests): deterministic schedule load (A1-A3), epoch-boundary activation (B1-B3), fail-closed behavior (C1-C5), O1-O5 regression (D1-D4). |

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Status** | ✅ **PARTIAL (M13)** |

| **Evidence** | Canonical economic state unified (M13). `ValidatorRecord.stake` and `ValidatorRecord.jailed_until_epoch` are the single source of truth. `ValidatorSlashingState` mirrors but is documented as non-authoritative. Eligibility predicates (`ValidatorRecord::is_eligible_at_epoch()`) read from canonical fields. |
| **Tests** | `crates/qbind-node/tests/m13_economic_state_unification_tests.rs` (12 tests) |
| **Remaining** | • Full architectural unification (single-write path for slashing penalties to both `ValidatorRecord` and `ValidatorSlashingState`) |

## Summary

| Category | Count | Items |
|----------|-------|-------|
| **RESOLVED** | 12 | C1, C2, Item 1, Item 2 (M20), Item 3 (M20), Item 4, Item 5 (M20), Item 6 (M20), Item 7 (M20), Item 8, Item 9 (M14), Item 10 (partial) |
| **OPEN** | 2 | C3, C4 |

**High-Risk Open Items**: C4 (Production binary does not yet boot a fully operating node) — DevNet readiness items B1, B2, B3, B5, **B6 (multi-validator P2P binary-path interconnect)**, **B7 (binary-path test-grade KEMTLS bring-up + dialer-side peer-validator identity closure)**, and **B8 (listener-side test-grade validator-identity closure + bounded initial-dial retry)** have all landed; the next multi-validator binary-path DevNet evidence run (Run 007) is justified, since both sides of a stagger-started two-`qbind-node` cluster can now end up with the *other's* deterministic NodeId among their `connected_peers()`, so `send_to(ValidatorId)` resolves to a registered transport session in both directions. Remaining sub-items are multi-validator restore catchup, mutual-auth (`MutualAuthMode::Required`) cryptographic peer-identity binding (the B8 resolver is test-grade self-asserted), and production PQC KEMTLS / certificate hardening. Protocol-correctness claims remain unaffected (those are test-evidenced).

**Medium-Risk Open Items**:
- C3 (Reporter Rewards): No economic incentive for evidence reporting. Whitepaper Section 12.2.3 documents this as future work; M15 hardened evidence pipeline is the baseline for any future reward implementation.

| 2026-05-04 | B6: Multi-validator P2P binary-path consensus interconnect landed in `qbind-node`. Two pre-existing wiring gaps closed: (i) `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` no longer plugs a freshly-allocated, immediately-dropped `mpsc::channel::<P2pMessage>` into the inbound demuxer — it now calls `p2p_service.subscribe().await` so the demuxer receives the real inbound stream; (ii) `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs` now exposes a `BinaryConsensusLoopIo { inbound_rx, outbound }` surface and `run_binary_consensus_loop_with_io` / `spawn_binary_consensus_loop_with_io` variants that decode `ConsensusNetMsg::{Proposal, Vote}` and feed them into `BasicHotStuffEngine::on_proposal_event` / `on_vote_event`, forwarding engine-emitted `ConsensusEngineAction`s back through an existing `ConsensusNetworkFacade` (the real `P2pConsensusNetwork`). `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs::run_p2p_node` wires a `ChannelConsensusHandler` onto the demuxer and threads its receiver + a `P2pConsensusNetwork` outbound facade into the loop. | 2026-05-04 | B7: Binary-path test-grade KEMTLS bring-up + dialer-side peer-validator identity closure landed in `qbind-node`. Smallest honest fix to the negative finding of DevNet Evidence Run 005 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_005.md` §11 #2–#3, §13). Three concrete changes: (i) test-grade KEM keypair derivation centralized in `derive_test_kem_keypair_from_validator_id(vid)` (single source of truth shared by listener + dialer); (ii) local NodeId, `SimpleValidatorNodeMapping` NodeId, and dialer outbound NodeId all unified on `sha3_256_tagged("QBIND:nodeid:v1", test_kem_pk(vid))` so `send_to(ValidatorId)` resolves to the actually-registered connection; (iii) `--p2p-peer` extended with `vid@addr` syntax (`parse_peer_spec`), and per-peer `peer_kem_pk` + expected-`validator_id` overrides threaded into `TcpKemTlsP2pService::dial_peer` via `set_peer_kem_pk_overrides` / `set_peer_validator_id_overrides` so each side dials with the *peer's* test KEM pk + expected validator id (the latter satisfies the `delegation_cert.validator_id == client_init.validator_id` check in `qbind_net::handshake::handle_server_accept`). A latent inbound-side bug also fixed: `TcpStream::into_std()` in `handle_inbound_connection` now restores blocking mode before `accept_kemtls_async` (the KEMTLS handshake does blocking reads, but the tokio-derived std stream was non-blocking → `WouldBlock` on first read, dropping every inbound session). A new `PeerValidatorMap` is populated at dial-config time on `P2pNodeContext` to bind the connected peer to its `ValidatorId(N)` on the dialer side. Multi-validator runs that pass bare-addr peers without `vid@` are rejected with a clear configuration error rather than silently producing a broken handshake. Files touched: `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/src/consensus_net_p2p.rs`. Regression-tested by `crates/qbind-node/tests/b7_kemtls_bringup_identity_closure_tests.rs` (5 integration tests: dialer/listener KEM-pk agreement, dialer-side identity closure to deterministic NodeId, **bounded two-real-binary KEMTLS handshake completion proof — the exact case Run 005 failed to demonstrate**, parser surface, single-validator no-regression) plus 6 new `p2p_node_builder::tests::b7_*` unit tests (including a bare-addr-peer rejection test and a malformed-spec rejection test). All 604 lib tests + all integration tests pass (the only failure observed was a pre-existing, unrelated compile error in `m16_epoch_transition_hardening_tests` against `RocksDbConsensusStorage`). C4 status updated: the "binary-path test-grade KEMTLS bring-up — empirically blocked (Run 005)" item is now closed for the dialer side; inbound-side cryptographic peer-identity binding (mutual KEMTLS auth) is the strictly smaller residual item, kept honest. The next multi-validator binary-path evidence run (Run-005 shape) is justified. | B7 |
| 2026-05-04 | B8: Listener-side test-grade validator-identity closure + bounded initial-dial retry landed in `qbind-node`. Smallest honest fix to the two negative findings of DevNet Evidence Run 006 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_006.md` §10–§13): (a) listener-side accepted sessions previously admitted under a temporary session NodeId rather than the deterministic peer NodeId, so V0's `send_to(ValidatorId(1))` could not resolve to the V1→V0 inbound session; (b) initial outbound dial losing the startup race with `Connection refused` was not retried, so a stagger-started two-node cluster ended up with a one-direction-only TCP topology. **Three concrete changes:** (i) **Listener-side identity closure (test-grade).** New `accept_kemtls_async_with_peer_init` in `crates/qbind-node/src/secure_channel.rs` surfaces `ClientInit.{client_random, validator_id}` from the server-side accept path via `qbind_net::unpack_client_init`. New `InboundIdentityResolver` + `set_inbound_identity_resolver` on `TcpKemTlsP2pService` in `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs`; `handle_inbound_connection` consults the resolver and, if it returns `Some(node_id)`, registers the accepted session under that NodeId (otherwise legacy temporary-session-NodeId path preserved exactly — no silent override). `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` installs a resolver that recovers the dialer's vid from the deterministic `qbind-client-<N>` ASCII prefix `create_connection_configs` already places in `client_random` (parsed by new `parse_test_validator_id_from_client_random` helper) and returns `derive_test_node_id_from_validator_id(N)` — the SAME NodeId the dialer side registers under. (ii) **Bounded initial-dial retry.** New `DialRetryPolicy` (default 8 attempts × {100..1000}ms ≈ 5.5s) and `set_dial_retry_policy`. `start()` no longer blocks on dial; instead it spawns a per-peer background `DialerHandle::dial_with_retry` task that retries only transient TCP errors (`ConnectionRefused`, `ConnectionReset`, `ConnectionAborted`, `TimedOut`, `AddrNotAvailable`, `NotFound`) and bounds attempts + backoff. KEMTLS-handshake errors and configuration errors are NOT retried. `shutdown()` aborts in-flight dial tasks before peer connections. Single-validator / no-static-peers / LocalMesh paths are bit-equivalent (no dial tasks spawned). (iii) **Honest scope.** The resolver consumes `client_random` under `MutualAuthMode::Disabled` and is therefore self-asserted by the dialer at the protocol level — a malicious dialer could spoof a vid in `client_random`. Strictly cryptographic inbound peer-identity binding still requires the existing `MutualAuthMode::Required` codepaths in `qbind-net` and is kept as a separate `Remaining` bullet (mutual-auth (`MutualAuthMode::Required`) cryptographic peer-identity binding — B8-residual). Files touched: `crates/qbind-node/src/secure_channel.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs`, `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs`. Regression-tested by `crates/qbind-node/tests/b8_listener_identity_closure_and_dial_retry_tests.rs` (6 tests: parse round-trip, listener-side deterministic-NodeId binding, **initial-dial retry recovery from stagger — the exact recovery DevNet Evidence Run 006 reported missing**, two-node bidirectional `connected_peers` precondition, single-validator no-regression, `DialRetryPolicy::no_retry` pin). All previously landed paths verified non-regressed: 5/5 b7 tests, 5/5 c4_b6 tests, 16/16 three_node_kemtls_integration tests, 9/9 t172 P2P smoke tests, 10/10 t175 wiring tests, 8/8 async kemtls integration tests, peer/manager roundtrip tests, 604/604 lib unit tests. C4 status updated: the Run 006 listener-side temp-NodeId binding and initial-dial-retry residual items are now closed at test-grade; mutual-auth cryptographic peer-identity binding is the strictly smaller residual item, kept honest. **DevNet Evidence Run 007 is justified** — both sides of a two-real-binary stagger-started cluster can now end up with the other's deterministic NodeId among their `connected_peers()`, so the test-grade transport precondition for first cross-node `ConsensusNetMsg::{Proposal, Vote}` traffic now holds. | B8 |

| 2026-05-06 | B9: Leader-side re-emission of `BroadcastProposal` on late peer connect within the same view landed in `qbind-node`. Smallest honest fix to the negative finding of Run 007. The fix is bounded entirely to the binary-path consensus loop (no engine redesign, no transport redesign): `BinaryConsensusLoopIo` gains an optional `peer_connectivity: Option<Arc<dyn PeerConnectivitySource>>` (a tiny dedicated trait — strictly smaller than `P2pService` — implemented by the new `P2pServicePeerConnectivity` adapter that forwards to the same `Arc<dyn P2pService>` already backing inbound demuxing and outbound `P2pConsensusNetwork`); `do_leader_tick` caches the leader's last `BroadcastProposal` together with the view it was emitted for; on every tick `maybe_reemit_on_late_peer_connect` runs through seven explicit boundedness gates (transition required, cached proposal required, view match, leader of current view, commit not invalidated, per-view single-shot latch, outbound facade required) and on all-gates-pass calls `outbound.broadcast_proposal(&cached)` exactly once, incrementing the new `BinaryConsensusLoopInboundStats::outbound_proposal_late_peer_reemits` counter (also surfaced in the `Loop exit:` summary). Reconnect churn within the same view produces zero additional re-emits; a view change between cache-fill and the connectivity poll invalidates the cache; when `peer_connectivity = None` (single-validator P2P, LocalMesh, the `io = None` 4-arg loop) the entire B9 path is skipped — bit-equivalent to pre-B9. | 2026-05-06 | B10: Engine accept / QC-formation closure on the binary path under post-B9 re-emitted leader proposal landed in `qbind-node`. Smallest honest fix to the negative finding of Run 008. Three additive changes to `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs`: (i) the leader-step tick now caches **both** the just-emitted `BroadcastProposal` AND the leader's paired same-view `BroadcastVote` (the engine's `on_leader_step` always emits the proposal immediately followed by the leader's self-vote); the existing B9 late-peer-connect helper now re-emits both under the same per-view single-shot latch on the same tick, only when the cached vote's view matches the cached proposal's view. Without the paired vote re-emit a 2-validator setup deterministically stalls in the exact Run-008 shape. (ii) The loop now wires an `Arc<dyn ConsensusProgressRecorder>` adapter (`NodeMetricsProgressRecorder`) onto the engine via `BasicHotStuffEngine::set_progress_recorder` before the first tick. Pre-B10 the binary-path loop never installed any progress recorder, so even when the engine genuinely formed a QC (as V0 actually did in Run 008's view 0) the `qbind_consensus_qcs_formed_total` counter on `/metrics` stayed at 0 — metric-coverage closure, not fabrication: every increment continues to come from the engine's existing `record_qc_formed` call site on actually-formed QCs. (iii) The inbound-message handler now increments `consensus_t154.proposals_accepted` on each `engine.on_proposal_event` that returns `Some(action)` and `consensus_t154.votes_accepted` on each `engine.on_vote_event` that returns `Ok(_)`; new `BinaryConsensusLoopInboundStats` fields `outbound_vote_late_peer_reemits`, `inbound_proposals_engine_accepted`, `inbound_votes_engine_accepted`, `qcs_formed_total` mirror these on the loop-exit summary. The B9 single-shot latch now covers the proposal+vote pair: at most one paired re-emit per view, never one without the other, no replay across reconnect churn. Regression-tested by `crates/qbind-node/tests/b10_engine_acceptance_qc_closure_tests.rs` (5 tests including in-tree reproduction of the Run-008 partial-positive shape via a `SelectiveConnectFacade` and post-fix engine-acceptance / QC closure proof on both sides). All previously-landed B1/B2/B3/B5/B6/B7/B8/B9 tests continue to pass. C4 status updated: the Run-008 boundary is closed at the engine accept / QC formation layer for the test-grade binary-path; empirical proof on real `qbind-node` processes is what Run 009 is now positioned to provide. | B10 |

| 2026-05-09 | DevNet Evidence Run 020 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_020.md`): first production-grade snapshot/restore evidence run on the same binary (sha256 `8479f426…3388`, byte-for-byte identical to Run 019). This is a sharpening, not a new contradiction. Other open C4 sub-items (signature verification of `TimeoutMsg`/`TimeoutCertificate`, exponential-backoff timeout pacing, production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution) remain open exactly as before. No QBIND production source code changed by this entry; the only code added is two `crates/qbind-ledger/examples/` reproducibility helpers (`qbind_state_snapshot`, `qbind_seed_vm_v0_state`) that invoke library paths already covered by the B3/T215 test suites. No previously landed binary-path capability appears regressed. | Run 020 |
| 2026-05-09 | DevNet Evidence Run 023 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_023.md`): N=4 Required-mode B3/B5/B13/B14 continuation evidence on the post-Run-022 binary (commit `83655bd`, sha256 `376fd59c…06e`, BuildID `9b16a227…7bd`), with the snapshot under test produced **in-process by the running real `qbind-node` via SIGUSR1 → `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot`** rather than by an out-of-binary helper. **Strongest-positive verdict** for this specific operational sub-shape: V0 (live throughout, started first per the Run 019 stagger) opened `state_vm_v0`, installed the SIGUSR1 trigger, received SIGUSR1 without terminating, invoked `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot` at `committed_height=10`, and produced a real RocksDB checkpoint at `/tmp/run023/snapshots/10/` containing `CURRENT`, `MANIFEST-000013`, `000009.sst`, and `OPTIONS-000015` plus a valid `meta.json`. B3 audit markers were written, the checkpoint was materialized into each restored validator's `state_vm_v0`, and B5 applied `snapshot_height=10`, `starting_view=11`, engine `committed_height=Some(10)`. No previously landed binary-path capability appears regressed. | Run 023 |

*This document should be updated whenever a contradiction is discovered between the whitepaper and implementation, or when significant undocumented behaviors are identified.*
#### C4 Run 025 evidence update (2026-05-09)

Run 024 remains the negative N=4 Required-mode baseline for the periodic `--snapshot-interval-blocks` trigger. The current implementation narrows that gap by wiring a committed-height periodic VM-v0 trigger into the real binary consensus progress path, reusing the same `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot` runtime path and serialization guard as SIGUSR1. Local seeded Run 025 evidence (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_025.md`) proves a real binary creates a periodic snapshot at committed height 4 without SIGUSR1, with `meta.json`, `CURRENT`, `MANIFEST-*`, `OPTIONS-*`, and `*.sst`, and restores from it. This does not claim full C4 closure or a completed N=4 Required-mode Run 024 repeat; full multi-validator periodic-snapshot continuation evidence remains open.

#### C4 Run 026 evidence update (2026-05-09)

DevNet Evidence Run 026 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_026.md`) closes the specific Run 024 negative result and the Run 025 single-node boundary on the tested real binary: the same post-Run-025 `qbind-node` (sha256 `af4e4d7388e5fd1b386c889570ae8caf369b4d8a113e4ed5ea11d8c199a54216`, BuildID `318c08f9c7ef296026eb10d020587752971f295e`) ran N=4 Required-mode (V0/V1A/V2A/V3A, `--p2p-mutual-auth required`, `--execution-profile vm-v0`) with V0 holding `--snapshot-interval-blocks 4 --snapshot-max-snapshots 2` and **no SIGUSR1**. V0 created in-process `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot` snapshots at committed heights 4, 8, 12, 16, 20, with `--snapshot-max-snapshots 2` honestly pruning heights 4, 8, 12 and retaining only 16 and 20. V1B and V2C restored from `/tmp/run026/snapshots/16` and the periodic snapshot supports full B3 (audit marker + checkpoint copy), B5 (`snapshot_height=16`, `starting_view=17`, engine `committed_height=Some(16)`), B13 (`mode_active 1->0`, `mode_exited_at_height=17 > 16`, `restore_catchup_blocks_applied_total=3`), and B14 (timeouts emitted, certificates formed, `current_view 17->26`, `committed_height 16->21` on V0/V1B/V2C with V3 absent) continuation. Snapshot metrics are honest (`qbind_snapshot_success_total=5`, `qbind_snapshot_last_height=20`, `qbind_snapshot_last_size_bytes=8588`, `qbind_snapshot_in_progress=0`, `qbind_snapshot_failure_total=0`); decode failures, engine rejects, rejected proposals, and invalid votes are all zero. C4 remains open overall for the broader production items already listed (production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore, signature verification of `TimeoutMsg` / `TimeoutCertificate`, exponential-backoff timeout pacing, production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution), and Run 026 does not claim full C4 closure.
#### C4 Run 027 evidence update (2026-05-09)

DevNet Evidence Run 027 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_027.md`) is a combined snapshot-trigger regression pass on the same post-Run-026 `qbind-node` (sha256 `af4e4d7388e5fd1b386c889570ae8caf369b4d8a113e4ed5ea11d8c199a54216`, BuildID `318c08f9c7ef296026eb10d020587752971f295e`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-status`, commit `40cc3d54316bff251516f5c11fc29cd16405e824`; binary byte-identical to Run 026 — Run 026 → Run 027 delta is documentation-only). **Strongest-positive verdict** for the four trigger paths under test, all on the same binary in one evidence run: (A) periodic `--snapshot-interval-blocks 4` in N=4 Required-mode (V0/V1/V2/V3, `--p2p-mutual-auth required`, V0-first stagger, **no SIGUSR1**) created 10 in-process `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot` snapshots at heights 4,8,12,16,20,24,28,32,36,40, pruned to `[36,40]` under `--snapshot-max-snapshots 2`, all four nodes alive, V0 metrics `qbind_snapshot_success_total=10 / failure_total=0 / in_progress=0 / last_height=40 / last_size_bytes=8588`, with one node restored from `/tmp/run027/A/snapshots/40` applying B3 marker + B5 baseline (`snapshot_height=40, starting_view=41, engine committed_height=Some(40)`) and `committed_anchor` advancing strictly past restore height; (B) single-node SIGUSR1 produced a real snapshot at height 7 with `meta.json + CURRENT + MANIFEST-000013 + 000009.sst + OPTIONS-000015`, alive across SIGUSR1, metrics `success_total=1 / failure_total=0`, restore B3/B5 OK; (C) disabled (no `--snapshot-dir`) handled 3× SIGUSR1 with three explicit `[snapshot] SIGUSR1 ignored: VM-v0 snapshot trigger disabled (--snapshot-dir not configured)` log lines, no snapshot directory created, every `qbind_snapshot_*` metric zero; (D) mixed periodic+SIGUSR1 (20 SIGUSR1s during ~6 s of committing) produced 32 successful snapshots (16 periodic + 16 SIGUSR1) through the same `VmV0RuntimeState::create_snapshot` runtime path — both trigger types share the same runtime, `snapshot_in_progress` AtomicBool guard, and `state` Mutex — with all 3 retained dirs `[56,60,64]` validating against the canonical `state/CURRENT + MANIFEST-* + *.sst + OPTIONS-*` layout and `NON_NUMERIC_ENTRIES=[]`. Required negative checks (no crash, no placeholder, no fallback, no overlap corruption, no partial dirs, no fake metrics, no unexpected deletions, no regression of any prior trigger path) all pass. **Material operator-facing observation** (sharpening, not a new contradiction): in mixed-trigger workloads, when SIGUSR1 lands at the same `committed_height` as a just-completed periodic snapshot, `StateSnapshotter::create_snapshot` correctly refuses to overwrite the existing valid directory and returns `StateSnapshotError::AlreadyExists` (`crates/qbind-ledger/src/state_snapshot.rs:268–283`, `crates/qbind-ledger/src/execution.rs:1620–1622`); this is logged honestly as `[snapshot] ERROR: snapshot creation failed at .../<h>: snapshot already exists at: .../<h>` and increments `qbind_snapshot_failure_total` (4 such events in sub-run D, exactly matching `failure_total=4`). The previously-written snapshot directory is unmodified — this is a snapshot-format safety property, not corruption — so operators that alarm on `qbind_snapshot_failure_total > 0` should treat this as expected on nodes that run *both* triggers concurrently; bare-periodic nodes (Run 026) and bare-SIGUSR1 nodes (Run 022/023) keep `failure_total=0`. The wall-clock overlap path (`SnapshotAlreadyInProgress`) was not exercised end-to-end here because each snapshot completes in ~1 ms; it remains covered by the existing `vm_v0_snapshot_trigger_rejects_overlap_without_metric_failure` unit test. **No QBIND source code changed** by this entry; the only repository changes are `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_027.md` and this row. The C4 status-row body is **not** re-narrowed: the SIGUSR1, periodic, and disabled-trigger paths were already closed by Runs 022/023/025/026, and the broader C4-open items (production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore, signature verification of `TimeoutMsg` / `TimeoutCertificate`, exponential-backoff timeout pacing, production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution, longer-window / larger-state snapshot stability) are unchanged. This is a sharpening (the four trigger paths under test all stay stable together on the same binary in one run, plus an explicit operator-facing nuance for the mixed-trigger metric shape), not a new contradiction.
#### C5 Run 034 evidence update (2026-05-10)

DevNet Evidence Run 034 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_034.md`) lands the missing N=4 Required-mode real-binary B14 absent-leader recovery proof under **active timeout verification** that Runs 030–033 left as the C5 Resolution path item (5). The post-Run-033 `qbind-node` debug binary (sha256 `0869335b8c9bf3232c3206c41acd11a9fad4b8ecfadf36156a2b46fd739beb5f`, BuildID `9127454ecc0e8616cde2a7805a1d24f5fb62c520`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-current-state-yet-again`, commit `dd6eabe67e11159d3fd76bb0676eee257cc2bd08`, clean working tree) ran V0/V1A/V2A/V3A (`--p2p-mutual-auth required`, `--execution-profile vm-v0`, V0-first stagger) with per-validator `--signer-keystore-path` (plaintext `LocalKeystorePlain` `validator-{N}.json`, `0o600`, ephemeral DevNet ML-DSA-44 keys generated out-of-tree under `/tmp/keygen`), four explicit `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK` entries (one per validator, the same set on every node), `--require-timeout-verification`, and metrics endpoints on `127.0.0.1:32000..32003`. Every node logged `[binary] Run 033: timeout verification ACTIVE — Arc<TimeoutVerificationContext> threaded into BinaryConsensusLoopIo::verification_ctx … signer_loaded=1 key_provider_loaded=1 validator_count=4` and `[binary-consensus] Starting consensus loop: … timeout_verification=verify+sign`, with pre-fault `/metrics` shape `qbind_timeout_verification_active 1`, `_signer_loaded 1`, `_key_provider_loaded 1`, `_validator_count 4` on every node. **Strongest-positive verdict.** With V1A (leader of views 93, 97, 101 under round-robin `view mod 4`) sent `signal.SIGINT` at `T=09:50:21Z` against the recorded numeric PID, the three remaining live validators (V0/V2A/V3A) recovered through three full B14 cycles: each emitted three signed `TimeoutMsg`s with explicit `[binary-consensus] Run 030: signing timeout view={93,97,101} validator=ValidatorId({0,2,3}) suite_id=100` / `Run 030: timeout signing OK …` pairs (`outbound_timeout_signing_success_total=3`, `outbound_timeout_signing_failure_total=0` on every live node); each verified six inbound TimeoutMsgs (`inbound_timeouts_delivered_total=6`, `inbound_timeout_verify_accepted_total=6`, `inbound_timeout_verify_rejected_total=0`, every `inbound_timeout_rejected_*` counter `=0`, `inbound_timeout_engine_accepted_total=6`, `inbound_timeout_engine_rejected_total=0`); each verified six inbound NewViews (`inbound_new_views_delivered_total=6`, `inbound_newview_verify_accepted_total=6`, `inbound_newview_verify_rejected_total=0`, every `inbound_newview_rejected_*` counter — `missing_evidence`, `evidence_mismatch`, `duplicate_signer`, `mixed_view`, `insufficient_quorum`, `unknown_validator`, `missing_key`, `wrong_suite`, `unsupported_suite`, `bad_signature`, `high_qc_mismatch` — `=0`); three TCs formed (`timeout_certificates_formed_total=3`, three `[binary-consensus] B14: TimeoutCertificate advanced view {93→94, 97→98, 101→102}` lines per live node) and drove three `view_timeout_advances_total`, advancing `current_view 90→105` and `committed_height 87→99` on every live validator with `proposals_total{result="rejected"}=0`, `votes_total{result="invalid"}=0`, `view_timeout_decode_failures_total=0`, `view_timeout_engine_rejects_total=0`, no fallback to `verification_ctx=None`, no unsigned timeout broadcast, no process crash (V0/V2A/V3A reached graceful `Loop exit:` after the post-recovery scrape; V1A's exit was the planned SIGINT). **C5 Resolution path item (5) is now closed.** Real-binary forged-traffic negative injection (item (6) above; would require a fake-peer rig holding a valid B12 transport identity but emitting crafted invalid TimeoutMsg/NewView payloads, or an opt-in in-process injection harness) was **not** built in Run 034 and is explicitly deferred to the existing deterministic per-reason test corpus (Run 028's `verify_timeout_msg` / `verify_timeout_certificate_with_evidence` positive/negative coverage, Run 030's 20 `binary_consensus_loop::tests::run030::*` deterministic tests, Run 031–033's 20+11+22+8 `timeout_verification_bridge` / `signer_loader` / `peer_key_provider` / CLI parser tests; full `qbind-node` lib `725 / 725` passing in Run 034). Run 034 does **not** claim full C4 closure, does **not** claim production transport PKI is solved by consensus-public-key distribution, and does **not** claim real-binary forged-traffic negative injection is covered. **No QBIND source code changed** by this entry; the only repository changes are `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_034.md` and this row.
#### C5 Run 035 evidence update (2026-05-10)

DevNet Evidence Run 035 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_035.md`) lands the smallest opt-in dev/test-only forged Timeout/NewView negative injection harness as the deterministic / real-binary safety-gate half of C5 Resolution path item (6) (real-binary forged-traffic negative injection). The post-Run-034 `qbind-node` debug binary on this branch (sha256 `5c90fcc486b1132c76c1f4aca76d93fae3c48374c3de21499f5d32fc5aeee4af`, ELF BuildID `63e756e7fc87c7df870c8c3c88c4774d63453e6c`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-activity`, working tree carrying the new `crates/qbind-node/src/forged_injection.rs` module + the five touched files) exposes a hidden `--devnet-forged-inject CASE` (`Append`) CLI flag whose activation requires THREE concurrent affirmative signals: (1) one or more `--devnet-forged-inject CASE` tokens drawn from the closed 12-case set (`malformed-timeout`, `unsigned-timeout`, `bad-signature-timeout`, `wrong-suite-timeout`, `unknown-validator-timeout`, `malformed-newview`, `missing-evidence-newview`, `duplicate-signer-newview`, `insufficient-quorum-newview`, `mixed-view-newview`, `bad-signature-newview`, `high-qc-mismatch-newview`); (2) `--env devnet` (Testnet/Mainnet are refused with `[binary] FATAL: Run 035 forged-injection harness is dev/test-only and cannot run on environment={Testnet,Mainnet}; refusing startup`); and (3) the explicit env var `QBIND_DEVNET_FORGED_INJECTION=1` (any other value, including unset, empty, `"0"`, `"true"`, `"yes"`, `"on"`, or `"1 "`, is refused with `[binary] FATAL: Run 035 forged-injection harness gated: --devnet-forged-inject was supplied but QBIND_DEVNET_FORGED_INJECTION=1 is not set in the environment; refusing to activate`). A fourth top-level gate also refuses non-P2P modes (LocalMesh has no inbound channel; activation under `--network-mode local-mesh` fails with `[binary] FATAL: --devnet-forged-inject requires --network-mode p2p`). The flag is hidden from `--help` (`hide = true`; `grep -c forged-inject` against `--help` is `0`). Once activated, `maybe_spawn_run035_forged_injection_harness` clones `ChannelConsensusHandler::sender_clone() -> mpsc::Sender<ConsensusNetMsg>` — the **same** channel the P2P inbound demuxer feeds — and pushes one bincode-encoded `ConsensusNetMsg::Timeout(bytes)` or `ConsensusNetMsg::NewView(bytes)` per case into it. The binary loop's existing `pub(crate) fn handle_inbound_consensus_msg` consumes these frames identically to live P2P traffic and runs them through `verify_timeout_msg` / `verify_timeout_certificate_with_evidence` BEFORE any call to `engine.on_timeout_msg` / `engine.on_timeout_certificate`. The harness never calls into the engine, never reads or writes any metrics counter (so it cannot fabricate metrics — every per-reason rejection-counter motion is performed by the existing Run 030 binary-loop code), and never logs signature bytes / signing keys / public keys / signing preimages (logged metadata is limited to case label, frame kind, and encoded byte length). For the cases that need a "decode-OK then signature-verify-FAILS" shape (`bad-signature-timeout`, `wrong-suite-timeout`, `bad-signature-newview`, `mixed-view-newview`, `duplicate-signer-newview`, `insufficient-quorum-newview`, `high-qc-mismatch-newview`), the runtime fixture generates fresh ephemeral ML-DSA-44 keypairs at process start that are NOT registered with any production `SuiteAwareValidatorKeyProvider`; signatures decode but verification fails against the real per-validator public keys distributed via `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK`. **Twenty-one new deterministic tests pass on this binary**: 5 safety-gate tests (default-disabled, refuse-Testnet, refuse-Mainnet, refuse-no-env-var across 8 sub-values, accept-only-with-Devnet-and-env-var-1) + 1 case-parser round-trip + 12 per-case tests (each asserting the precise per-reason rejection counter increments by 1, every engine-accept counter stays 0, view did not advance) + 1 aggregate test (every case in `ForgedInjectionCase::ALL` rejects-before-engine and never advances view) + 1 honest-traffic-after-injection survival test (after BadSignatureTimeout increments `inbound_timeout_rejected_bad_signature=1`, an honest signed TimeoutMsg from the same validator id still advances `inbound_timeout_verify_accepted=1` and `inbound_timeout_engine_accepted=1`, with `bad_signature` NOT bumped a second time) + 1 `mpsc` channel round-trip test (proves pushing through `ChannelConsensusHandler::sender_clone()` delivers into the same `handle_inbound_consensus_msg` path the binary loop drives). All 20 Run 030 deterministic loop-API tests still pass, all 9 vm_v0_runtime tests still pass, and full `qbind-node` lib **746 / 746 passing** (= 725 pre-Run-035 + 21 new Run 035), zero regressions. On the real binary, all 7 safety-gate negative smoke checks fail closed (testnet, mainnet, devnet without env var, `QBIND_DEVNET_FORGED_INJECTION=0`, unknown case token, devnet+env-var-1 under LocalMesh, `--help` does not expose the flag). **PARTIAL POSITIVE verdict.** The deterministic / real-binary safety-gate half of item (6) is proven on this binary; a live N=4 Required-mode multi-process forged-injection run (where four `qbind-node` processes serve real P2P traffic and the harness is activated against one target node mid-run, then honest B14 absent-leader recovery is exercised after the harness completes) was NOT executed in this evidence run because the CI sandbox does not provide the network namespaces Run 034 used for its live multi-process evidence; that live N=4 step is the operator's immediate-next action and is not blocked by code (the harness, the safety gates, and the per-case verification logic all pass deterministically and on the real binary's startup gate today). C5 remains OPEN strictly because **production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution (a C4 sub-item) is still not solved** — Run 035 changes nothing about transport PKI; B12 `TrustedClientRoots` / `DummySig` is still test-grade and is NOT a substitute. Run 035 does **not** claim full C4 closure, does **not** claim production transport PKI is solved, does **not** claim live N=4 multi-process forged-injection real-binary evidence (only the deterministic / real-binary-startup-gate evidence on the same `qbind-node` binary). Files changed in Run 035: `crates/qbind-node/src/forged_injection.rs` (NEW), `crates/qbind-node/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod forged_injection`), `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` (hidden `--devnet-forged-inject CASE` Append flag), `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs` (`handle_inbound_consensus_msg` and `RestoreCatchupModeState` promoted to `pub(crate)`; new `pub(crate) fn deliver_inbound_for_run035` test helper), `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_inbound.rs` (new `ChannelConsensusHandler::sender_clone`), `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (top-level safety gate after `validate_p2p_config` + `maybe_spawn_run035_forged_injection_harness` wiring after `spawn_binary_consensus_loop_with_io` + shutdown await), `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_035.md` (NEW), and this row.
#### C4 Run 037 evidence update (2026-05-10) — piece (c) NARROWED

DevNet Evidence Run 037 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_037.md`) lands the smallest production-honest PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution + delegation-cert verification path on the real binary, narrowing C4 piece (c) (production-honest PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution / certificate lifecycle) from "OPEN — only B12 test-grade `TrustedClientRoots`/`DummySig` available" to "NARROWED — production-honest PQC static-root mode landed on the binary path, real ML-DSA-44-signed delegation certs verify end-to-end, real-binary two-node mutual-auth succeeds without DummySig; full operational PKI lifecycle (rotation / revocation / OOB root distribution / per-environment trust anchors / production KEM + AEAD wiring) remains explicitly out of scope and is tracked under the surviving C4 pieces". Run 037 does NOT claim full C4 closure, does NOT claim production KEM (ML-KEM-768) or production AEAD wiring is solved (those are separate C4 pieces, NOT C4(c) — the binary still uses test-grade `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` for KEM/AEAD), does NOT remove the test-grade DummySig path (it remains available behind the explicit `--p2p-pqc-root-mode test-grade-dummy-sig` selection — refused on MainNet, warned on TestNet, allowed on DevNet — for backward compatibility with all pre-Run-037 evidence runs), does NOT claim a CA / rotation / revocation flow has landed, and does NOT silently downgrade to DummySig under any combination of CLI flags. Files changed: `crates/qbind-crypto/src/ml_dsa44_signature_suite.rs` (NEW — real `MlDsa44SignatureSuite` impl reusing existing `MlDsa44Backend`, no parallel crypto path), `crates/qbind-crypto/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod ml_dsa44_signature_suite`; `pub use MlDsa44SignatureSuite`), `crates/qbind-net/src/lib.rs` (`pub use verify_delegation_cert` made re-exported for test access — function body unchanged), `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_root_config.rs` (NEW — `PqcRootMode { TestGradeDummySig, PqcStaticRoot }`, `PqcTrustedRoot { root_key_id: [u8;32], suite_id: u8, root_pk: Vec<u8> }` with strict hex parsing, `PqcStaticRootConfig`, `PqcLeafCredentials`, `parse_pqc_root_mode`, `parse_pqc_trusted_root_specs` with strict-parse / duplicate-id / unsupported-suite / malformed-pk / missing-root fail-closed, `PQC_TRANSPORT_SUITE_ML_DSA_44 = 100`, `PqcLeafCredentialPaths::load`, 12 unit tests pass), `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_devnet_helper.rs` (NEW — offline `mint_devnet_root() -> DevNetRoot { root_key_id, root_pk, root_sk }` using existing `MlDsa44Backend::keygen`, `LeafCertSpec`, `issue_leaf_delegation_cert`, `encode_cert` building real ML-DSA-44-signed `NetworkDelegationCert`s; never logs private key material; 5 unit tests pass round-trip against `qbind_net::verify_delegation_cert`), `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` (`with_pqc_root_config(...)`; `make_pqc_static_root_crypto_provider(...)` registers real `MlDsa44SignatureSuite` (suite_id 100) instead of `DummySig`; `TrustedClientRoots` resolver consults configured root pks under `PqcStaticRoot` mode, returns `None` for unknown root_key_id; per-validator leaf cert / KEM-sk overrides come from `PqcLeafCredentials` instead of `make_dummy_delegation_cert`; `root_network_pk` for `ClientHandshakeConfig` / `ServerHandshakeConfig` set to the configured root pk under PQC mode; metrics `pqc_root_mode` and `pqc_roots_configured` populated at build time), `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` (4 NEW flags — `--p2p-pqc-root-mode`, `--p2p-trusted-root` (Append), `--p2p-leaf-cert <PATH>`, `--p2p-leaf-cert-key <PATH>`; help text references contradiction.md; 2 NEW CLI tests pass: help-exposes-flags + parse-roundtrip), `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (Run 037 wiring — refuses unknown `--p2p-pqc-root-mode` value, refuses malformed / duplicate / unsupported-suite `--p2p-trusted-root` entries, refuses `--p2p-leaf-cert` without `--p2p-leaf-cert-key` (and vice versa), refuses `--p2p-mutual-auth required` + `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` without configured roots OR without leaf credentials with FATAL exit 1; banner line `[binary] Run 037: pqc_root_mode=… configured_roots=N leaf_credentials_present=… (root fingerprints: [id=XXXXXXXX.. suite=100 fp=YYYYYYYY])` shows the active mode and SAFE fingerprints (truncated id + 8-byte SHA-256 of root pk; never raw root pk, never any private key); existing MainNet refuse-startup guard kept for the test-grade DummySig path, relaxed to a warning for the production-honest `pqc-static-root` path with explicit caveat that full MainNet readiness still requires the surviving non-C4(c) pieces), `crates/qbind-node/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod pqc_root_config; (b) `qbind-node::pqc_root_config::tests` 12/12 (valid parse, malformed root_key_id, malformed pk hex, duplicate root_key_id, unsupported suite, missing-required-when-PqcStaticRoot, mode parsing, fingerprint format); both processes stay alive past the handshake window; V0 emits `[binary-consensus] B9+B10: re-emitted view 0 BroadcastProposal + BroadcastVote after late peer connect (newly_connected_peers=1, proposal_reemits_total=1, vote_reemits_total=1)` — that line is only emitted by `BinaryConsensusLoopIo` after `P2pService::on_peer_connected` fires, which under `MutualAuthMode::Required` requires `mutual_auth_complete=true` AND a verified cert-derived NodeId (i.e. is GATED on real ML-DSA-44 cert verify success, with no DummySig in the registered crypto provider); the previous `client handle_server_accept failed` error from the dialer's mismatched `peer_root_network_pk` is GONE, evidencing that the dialer's listener-cert ML-DSA-44 verify against the configured root pk succeeded; (iii) two-node NEGATIVE smoke (same setup but V1's `v1.cert.bin` flipped its trailing signature byte): no `newly_connected_peers` line emitted on either node, V0 listener logs `[P2P] Inbound connection error: Handshake error: channel error: Net(Protocol("server handle_client_init failed"))` (the listener's `parse_and_verify_client_cert` rejected the bad ML-DSA-44 signature inside `verify_delegation_cert` BEFORE calling `engine.on_*`), V1 dialer logs `[P2P] dial 127.0.0.1:19420 giving up after 1 attempt(s): Handshake error`; both processes stay alive (rc=running through the 8 s smoke window); no silent fallback to DummySig (the registered signature suite under `pqc-static-root` mode is `MlDsa44SignatureSuite` and there is no DummySig fallback path in `make_pqc_static_root_crypto_provider`); (iv) startup fail-closed smoke: `--p2p-mutual-auth required --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root --p2p-trusted-root <SPEC>` with NO `--p2p-leaf-cert` exits with rc=1 and FATAL message `[binary] FATAL: --p2p-mutual-auth required + --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root requires --p2p-leaf-cert and --p2p-leaf-cert-key (production-honest mode must not silently fall back to test-grade certs). See docs/whitepaper/contradiction.md C4(c).`. Smoke logs preserved at `docs/devnet/run_037_smoke_v0.stderr.log`, `…v1.stderr.log`, `…run_037_smoke_negative_v0.stderr.log`, `…v1.stderr.log`. **What is now production-honest on the binary path**: ML-DSA-44 signature verification of `NetworkDelegationCert`s; explicit operator-supplied root public keys with strict parsing and fail-closed configuration validation; per-validator real ML-DSA-44-signed leaf certs loaded from disk; cert-derived peer identity binding under `MutualAuthMode::Required`; explicit metric exposure of mode + root count + per-reason cert-verify counters. **What remains DevNet-only / explicit-test-only**: KEM key agreement still uses `DummyKem`; AEAD still uses `DummyAead`; no CA, no cert rotation, no cert revocation, no OOB / signed root-distribution channel (operators distribute the root pk hex out-of-band today); the `--p2p-pqc-root-mode test-grade-dummy-sig` path remains available behind the explicit operator selection (refused on MainNet, warned on TestNet, allowed on DevNet) and is the path exercised by every pre-Run-037 evidence run including Runs 010A/B, 030, 034, 036. **Remaining open**: real ML-KEM-768 wiring on the binary path (separate C4 piece, not C4(c)); real production AEAD wiring on the binary path (separate C4 piece, not C4(c)); operational PKI lifecycle (CA / rotation / revocation / signed root-distribution channel — surviving non-C4(c) work); per-environment trust anchors (per-DevNet/TestNet/MainNet root sets); cert validity-window enforcement on the binary path (the cert format already carries `not_before` / `not_after`, but the listener-side code path that increments `pqc_cert_rejected_expired_total` has metric scaffolding only — production-grade clock-source enforcement is deferred). **Verdict**: C4 piece (c) is **NARROWED** (production-honest PQC static-root cert-verification mode lands on the binary path; real-binary two-node mutual-auth succeeds without DummySig; negative cert cases fail closed at the live binary path); C4 piece (c) is NOT marked closed because production-grade CA / rotation / revocation / signed root distribution remain operator-out-of-band, and the surviving non-C4(c) C4 pieces (production KEM, production AEAD, fast-sync, exponential-backoff timeout pacing) are unchanged. C5 is NOT marked closed by this entry: although Run 037 narrows the dependency C5 names (B12 `TrustedClientRoots` / `DummySig` is no longer the only available transport identity stack on the binary path), C5's enclosing `production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution` requirement is satisfied for the *cert-verification surface only* and not yet for the broader transport stack (KEM + AEAD), so per the strict scope rule "Do not mark C5 closed unless production PQC KEMTLS root-key distribution is solved enough to remove the remaining C5 dependency", C5's status text is updated to reflect that the C4(c) blocker is NARROWED but not yet fully closed. Operators MUST NOT rely on `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` for production transport security today; it is honest about the cert-verification surface, but the surrounding KEM / AEAD primitives on the binary path remain test-grade until the surviving non-C4(c) C4 pieces close.

Operators MUST NOT rely on `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` for production transport security today; it is honest about the cert-verification surface (now proven across the full N=4 Required-mode binary B14 topology), but the surrounding KEM / AEAD primitives on the binary path remain test-grade until the surviving non-C4(c) C4 pieces close.

#### C4 Run 041 evidence update (2026-05-11) — Run 040 binary confirmation; full C4 still OPEN

#### C4 Run 043 evidence update (2026-05-11) — `qbind_p2p_pqc_*` live `/metrics` exposure NARROWED (observability-only); full C4 and C5 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 043 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_043.md`) closes the inherited Run 038/039/040/041/042 observability gap recorded by the Run 041/042 C4 rows above — "`qbind_p2p_pqc_*` counters are declared in `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs::P2pMetrics::format_metrics` but they are not currently emitted through the live `/metrics` endpoint because `NodeMetrics::format_metrics` / `format_metrics_with_crypto` does not delegate to `self.p2p.format_metrics`" — by wiring `self.p2p.format_metrics()` into `NodeMetrics::format_metrics` exactly once (inserted between the `peer_network` and `connection_limit` blocks; `format_metrics_with_crypto` inherits this via composition without any second call) **AND** by sharing the same `Arc<P2pMetrics>` instance between the live transport path (`P2pNodeBuilder::build()`) and the live `/metrics` HTTP scrape (`metrics_http::format_metrics_output` → `NodeMetrics::format_metrics`). The instance-sharing layer is required because pre-Run-043 `P2pNodeBuilder::build()` minted a fresh local `Arc<P2pMetrics>` at `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs:1091` that was never reached by `NodeMetrics::format_metrics`, so a formatter-wiring-only fix would emit the family names with every value pinned at 0 even under live `pqc-static-root` operation — Run 043 honestly identifies this as the *truly missing link* beyond what the problem-statement preferred minimal edit captured and addresses both layers. clock-source cert-validity-window enforcement. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 043; the transport-crypto dependency (real ML-DSA-44 cert verification — Run 037, real ML-KEM-768 — Run 039, real ChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD — Run 040, active timeout verification — Runs 031–034, forged-traffic rejection — Runs 035–036, end-to-end live-binary N=4 B14 recovery — Run 042) is *further confirmed scrape-observable at the `qbind_p2p_pqc_*` gauge level on the live binary path* by Run 043, but lifecycle (CA / rotation / revocation / signed root distribution) and per-event cert-verify counter wiring remain C4 pieces, so Run 043 does NOT close C5 by fiat. Operators using `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` post-Run-043 can now scrape the full `qbind_p2p_pqc_*` family from the live `/metrics` endpoint exactly once and observe `qbind_p2p_pqc_root_mode 1` and `qbind_p2p_pqc_roots_configured N` honestly reflecting the active production-honest configuration; the per-event accepted/rejected counters honestly read 0 today because their `inc_*` setters are not yet called from the live cert-verify path — operators MUST NOT interpret the present zero values as evidence that no cert verification happened, only as evidence that the per-event call sites are not yet wired (this is the documented boundary).
#### C4 Run 044 evidence update (2026-05-11) — Run 043 cert-verify increment-call-site observability gap NARROWED (observability-only); full C4 and C5 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 044 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_044.md`) closes the inherited Run 043 §15 honest-boundary gap recorded by the Run 043 C4 row above — "the 8 cert-verify event counters (`qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total`, and the 6 per-reason `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_rejected_*_total`) are now scrape-visible exactly once on the live `/metrics` endpoint but their `inc_*` setters in `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs:6297–6335` are not yet called from any production code path" — by wiring the existing `P2pMetrics::inc_pqc_cert_verify_*` setters into the **actual** live cert-verification success/failure boundaries in `qbind-net::handshake` without changing verification behaviour, error return types, or any protocol shape. **Observability-only — no `qbind-net`/`qbind-crypto`/`qbind-node` consensus, KEMTLS, KEM, AEAD, signer-loader, timeout-verification, or forged-traffic-rejection surface was modified.** Release binary `qbind-node` sha256 `fe805315c2be8aebd1133b3a2082dff1eeab3000a18abdcb7cbc265897377e4a` ELF BuildID `15bac93f1def29b90e2ea713dcc6b5ca09692900`, `devnet_pqc_root_helper` sha256 `c42c9b875452c712539b4fcece674f962ff998cca1655b9e5fe34f4323f94e1b` ELF BuildID `a8d47c8ee5f4f61af8df0837930f4df55a5678da`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-development-50412889-86c3-4f75-b33e-20d0a95a07ed`, pre-doc commit `02f4e4c667f16f5c0549fce729ae428eea01875b`, clean working tree pre-doc. **Crate-layering-clean seam.** `P2pMetrics` lives in `qbind-node` and `qbind-net` must not depend on `qbind-node`; the smallest safe shape is a new tiny trait `qbind_net::CertVerifyMetricsSink` in `crates/qbind-net/src/cert_verify_metrics.rs` with default no-op methods (`inc_accepted`, `inc_rejected_unknown_root`, `inc_rejected_wrong_suite`, `inc_rejected_bad_signature`, `inc_rejected_validator_mismatch`, `inc_rejected_malformed`, `inc_rejected_expired`) threaded through `qbind_net::ClientHandshakeConfig` and `qbind_net::ServerHandshakeConfig` as `pub cert_verify_metrics: Option<Arc<dyn CertVerifyMetricsSink>>` and invoked at each existing return arm of the listener-side `ServerHandshake::parse_and_verify_client_cert` and the dialer-side `ClientHandshake::handle_server_accept` cert-verification region. `qbind-node` implements the trait for `P2pMetrics` (forwarding each method onto the existing pre-Run-044 `inc_pqc_cert_verify_*` setters that preserve the Run 037 aggregate-counter contract), and `P2pNodeBuilder::create_connection_configs` installs the sink **only** on the production-honest path `(MutualAuthMode::{Required,Optional}, PqcRootMode::PqcStaticRoot, Some(Arc<P2pMetrics>) shared via the Run-043 with_p2p_metrics setter)`. **Reason mapping (Run 044 §4 table):** listener-side `NetworkDelegationCert::decode → Err` → `inc_rejected_malformed` → `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("parse error")`; listener-side `TrustedClientRoots::lookup → None` → `inc_rejected_unknown_root` → `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("untrusted root")`; either-side `verify_delegation_cert → Err(UnsupportedSuite(_))` → `inc_rejected_wrong_suite` → `NetError::UnsupportedSuite(_)`; either-side `verify_delegation_cert → Err(KeySchedule("signature verify error"))` → `inc_rejected_bad_signature` → `NetError::KeySchedule("signature verify error")`; dialer-side `delegation_cert.validator_id != client_init.validator_id` → `inc_rejected_validator_mismatch` → `NetError::KeySchedule("validator_id mismatch in cert")`; dialer-side cert-bytes parse fail → `inc_rejected_malformed` → `NetError::KeySchedule("failed to parse delegation cert")`; success on either side (parse + root lookup + signature verify + validator-id match where applicable) → `inc_accepted`. **`inc_rejected_expired` is currently unused at the live boundary** because validity-window enforcement (`not_before` / `not_after`) is not yet implemented in `qbind_net::handshake::verify_delegation_cert`; the counter stays visible at zero, explicitly documented as such (see Run 044 §4 last row and `expired_counter_documented_unused_at_live_boundary` unit test). **Tests:** `cargo test -p qbind-net --lib` 17/17 (15 pre-existing + 2 new `cert_verify_metrics::tests::*` — default-no-op + counting-sink);
