DevNet Evidence Run 045 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_045.md`) closes the Run 044 §4-last-row "`inc_rejected_expired` is currently unused at the live boundary because validity-window enforcement is not yet implemented in `verify_delegation_cert`" gap by adding the smallest-possible `not_before` / `not_after` enforcement to `qbind_net::handshake::verify_delegation_cert`, routing the three resulting failure shapes — expired, not-yet-valid, and inverted-window — through the already-wired Run 044 `inc_rejected_expired` cert-verify metrics sink, without changing any other verification semantics. **Narrow validity-window enforcement only — no `qbind-net`/`qbind-crypto`/`qbind-node` consensus, KEMTLS, KEM, AEAD, signer-loader, timeout-verification, forged-traffic-rejection, mutual-auth, or trust-anchor surface was modified.** Release binary `qbind-node` sha256 `e9b79590ec9610d34fbec476bb0b94b425d9a50e8f696e075d1201b881b1ccee` ELF BuildID `c17f96cfcc88f1f0b5dd220988ff5eacdcd7bc9c`, `devnet_pqc_root_helper` sha256 `a86d96d1259ac6eeb200543f3c520a3213a8a8724c6485e731ce92d820d6dc4d` ELF BuildID `ee14b1b7be65bbf73b1639a76ace33a3a8721ab6`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-development-9b9570c8-3ffd-4012-b84f-c69dda0603a5`, pre-doc commit `942fc3b8915b0ad25c11657f98b203ba8f8fcff3`, working tree dirty only with Run 045 changes pre-doc-commit. **Format already had the fields.** `qbind_wire::net::NetworkDelegationCert` (and `qbind_hash::net::network_delegation_cert_digest`) already carried `not_before: u64` / `not_after: u64` Unix-seconds fields in the signed digest preimage from Run 037 onwards; Run 045 does NOT change the wire format, the digest preimage, or any test cert fixture (every pre-existing helper / test fixture uses `not_before: 0, not_after: u64::MAX` which is currently-valid under any realistic wall-clock and therefore unaffected). **Validity-window semantics.** Inclusive on both ends: a cert is valid iff `not_before <= validation_time <= not_after`. Validation runs **after** signature verification, so a tampered validity field surfaces as `NetError::KeySchedule("signature verify error")` (preserving the existing tampered-cert contract from Run 037 §10), and a malformed inverted window (`not_before > not_after`) is fail-closed *before* any time comparison so it can't accidentally be accepted on a clock-skew corner case. Fail-closed cases on `verify_delegation_cert` / `verify_delegation_cert_at`: `not_before > not_after` → `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert invalid validity window")`; `validation_time < not_before` → `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert not yet valid")`; `validation_time > not_after` → `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert expired")`. **Time-source model.** Two entry points: `verify_delegation_cert(crypto, cert, root_pk)` is the binary-path convenience wrapper that reads `SystemTime::now()` once per call and is **explicitly** scoped as a transport-layer operational freshness check, NOT a consensus time source — consensus safety remains entirely independent of wall-clock; `verify_delegation_cert_at(crypto, cert, root_pk, validation_time_secs)` is the deterministic seam for tests and for any future callers that need explicit clock injection. Smallest-injection-seam — no new field was added to `ClientHandshakeConfig` / `ServerHandshakeConfig` (which would have forced every one of the ~120 historical call sites under `crates/{qbind-net,qbind-node}/tests/*` to be edited, expanding the change-surface against the "smallest code change" requirement); the seam is the public `verify_delegation_cert_at` function itself, which is used by the focused `crates/qbind-net/tests/run_045_cert_validity_tests.rs` deterministic tests and by `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_devnet_helper.rs` tests. No dangerous operator bypass (no `--ignore-cert-validity` or equivalent) was added; the wall-clock wrapper is the only path the live binary uses. **Reason-mapping update.** The `cert_verify_metrics::rejection-reason` table is extended with one row (Run 045) folded into the existing `inc_rejected_expired` cell: dialer-side and listener-side `verify_delegation_cert → Err(NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert expired" | "cert not yet valid" | "cert invalid validity window"))` → `inc_rejected_expired` → bumps `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_rejected_expired_total` AND the aggregate `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total` exactly once via the Run 037 per-reason-bumps-aggregate contract. Every other Run 044 mapping row is preserved bit-identically. Critically, validity-window failures do NOT collapse into `bad_signature` — the dialer-side and listener-side `match &e { ... }` blocks in `handle_server_accept` and `parse_and_verify_client_cert` explicitly precede the `NetError::KeySchedule(_) => inc_rejected_bad_signature` arm with a `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert expired" | "cert not yet valid" | "cert invalid validity window") => inc_rejected_expired` arm; any other (hypothetical future) `ClientCertInvalid(_)` shape from `verify_delegation_cert` still falls back to `bad_signature` rather than mis-classify as expired. **Accepted-counter and expired-counter boundary.** `inc_accepted` is reached only after parse + (listener-side) trusted-root lookup + signature verify + validity-window check (Run 045) + (dialer-side) validator-id match all succeed. `inc_rejected_expired` is reached only on the three validity-window failure shapes above. Accepted and expired are mutually exclusive on the same handshake event (any validity-window failure short-circuits before `inc_accepted`), enforced both by the `return Err(e)` immediately after the `match`-on-`e` block and by the `dialer_valid_cert_still_increments_only_accepted` regression test (which asserts a currently-valid cert under wall-clock bumps only `accepted = 1` and zero rejection counters). **No duplicate increments.** Each `verify_delegation_cert` invocation produces at most one `inc_*` call by construction (the `match &e {...}` block runs once per `Err` and the success path bumps `inc_accepted` exactly once); the listener wrapper and dialer wrapper layers each invoke `verify_delegation_cert` once per handshake event, and the sink is `Option<Arc<dyn CertVerifyMetricsSink>>` with the same `Arc` cloned into both `ClientHandshakeConfig::cert_verify_metrics` and `ServerHandshakeConfig::cert_verify_metrics` via `P2pNodeBuilder::create_connection_configs` (Run 044 shape preserved), so no double-counting between listener/dialer wrapper layers is introduced. **Tests.** `cargo test -p qbind-net --lib` 17/17 (no count delta vs Run 044 — Run 045 adds no new lib unit-test module); Live `inc_rejected_expired` counter movement (and aggregate `inc_pqc_cert_verify_rejected` movement, and `inc_accepted` non-movement) on the real `qbind-net::handshake` boundary is therefore proven by the **qbind-net handshake-boundary unit tests** in `crates/qbind-net/tests/run_045_cert_validity_tests.rs::listener_expired_cert_increments_expired_once`, `listener_not_yet_valid_cert_increments_expired_once`, `listener_inverted_window_cert_increments_expired_once`, `dialer_expired_cert_increments_expired_once`, `dialer_not_yet_valid_cert_increments_expired_once`, and `dialer_inverted_window_cert_increments_expired_once`, each of which drives the real `parse_and_verify_client_cert` / `handle_server_accept` boundaries through the existing public `qbind-net` API and asserts (a) the bit-identical typed `NetError::ClientCertInvalid(...)` is returned AND (b) `expired_counter == 1` AND (c) `aggregate_rejected_counter` movement via the Run 037 per-reason-bumps-aggregate contract AND (d) every other counter == 0 AND (e) `accepted == 0` for the same event. This is exactly the "partial-positive: validity enforcement lands in qbind-net tests, but real-binary negative metric movement is not observable due to startup self-verification" boundary anticipated in the Run 045 task description, recorded honestly as such — Run 045 does NOT claim live-binary expired-counter movement on the *negative-cert* smoke because the binary, by design (Run 037 / Run 042 startup self-verification), exits before serving `/metrics`; this is the correct fail-closed behaviour and is *more* defensive than allowing the binary to come up with an unusable cert. **C4 piece "cert validity-window enforcement (`not_before` / `not_after` — not yet enforced by `verify_delegation_cert`, the only remaining wired-but-unused per-reason cell)" is now NARROWED on the live binary path** — `verify_delegation_cert` enforces `not_before` / `not_after`, the `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_rejected_expired_total` cell is no longer the "documented-unused" per-reason cell, and the only fail-mode previously wired-but-unreachable at the live boundary is now fully reachable through `qbind-net::handshake` (proven by unit tests on the real boundary, by startup self-verification on the live binary path, and indirectly by digest-preimage signature coverage of `not_before` / `not_after` from Run 037 onwards). **Full C4 remains OPEN** for: production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle (operator-out-of-band, not solved — Run 045 does NOT claim CA lifecycle); production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; exponential-backoff timeout pacing; per-environment trust anchors. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 045; the transport-crypto dependency is now further hardened on the cert-freshness axis but lifecycle (CA / rotation / revocation / signed root distribution) remains a C4 piece, so Run 045 does NOT close C5 by fiat. **No fabricated metrics.** **No silent regression.** **No protocol behavior change beyond validity-window rejection.** **No removed tests, no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened.** **No operator bypass.** Operators using `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` post-Run-045 now have actionable live `/metrics` observability of expired / not-yet-valid / inverted-window PQC delegation-cert verification failures through `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_rejected_expired_total` on the live binary path whenever a peer connecting to a healthy node presents such a cert (the local-cert-against-self failure path stops at startup self-verification by design); the live binary itself refuses to come up at all if its own leaf cert is outside its validity window — both surfaces are honest fail-closed behaviour.
#### C4 Run 046 evidence update (2026-05-11)

Run 045 left the documented C4 remaining-items list as: production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle; production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; **exponential-backoff timeout pacing**; per-environment trust anchors. Run 046 narrows the "exponential-backoff timeout pacing" cell on the binary B14 path by replacing the pre-Run-046 fixed-cadence view-timeout primitive (`view_timeout_ticks = 50` ticks, constant) with a bounded, tick-deterministic exponential-backoff pacer (`ViewTimeoutBackoffState` in `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs`, defaults `base = 50` ticks / `multiplier = 2` / `max = 800` ticks). The pacer threshold grows by an integer multiplier after each consecutive local `TimeoutMsg` emission for a view without committed-height progress, saturating at the cap; it resets to base on real committed-height progress only. View-only advances (including TC-driven view advances, which are themselves timeout-driven and therefore not a recovery signal) do **not** reset the pacer, matching the standard HotStuff pacemaker convention that only commits demonstrate liveness. The pacer is observable on `/metrics` through five new lines (`qbind_consensus_view_timeout_current_threshold_ticks`, `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_backoff_level`, `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_backoff_resets_total`, `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_backoff_increases_total`, `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_max_cap_hits_total`); all five are strict accounts of state transitions that actually occurred (no fabricated resets, no increase without an emitted timeout, no cap-hit unless the threshold actually saturated). Run 046 is proven by 11 new `run046_*` unit tests (default-base-equals-old-fixed-threshold, doubles-then-saturates, reset-counts-real-only, multiplier-1-preserves-fixed-cadence, invalid-config-rejected-fail-closed, disabled-primitive-inert, second-view-emits-at-doubled-threshold-after-self-fire, committed-height-progress-resets-pacer, view-only-progress-does-not-reset-pacer, metrics-export-reflects-pacer-state-exactly, metrics-export-disabled-primitive-reads-zero) which together pin the pacer state machine, the wiring into `maybe_emit_view_timeout`, and the metric exposition. All 791 pre-existing `qbind-node` lib tests, all 12 Run 037 PQC static-root mutual-auth tests, all Run 030 timeout-verification tests, and the B14 Run 015 absent-leader / self-quorum / restore-catchup-suppression / disabled-via-None tests pass unchanged — preserving B14 safety, active timeout verification, forged-traffic rejection, single-validator no-timeout behaviour, `--require-timeout-verification` semantics, restore-catchup gating, and Run 037–045 transport behaviour. **C4 piece "exponential-backoff timeout pacing" is now NARROWED on the binary B14 path** — the binary path no longer fires `TimeoutMsg`s at a constant aggressive cadence under sustained absent-leader conditions, the pacer is fully deterministic and integer-only, and the schedule is observable end-to-end on `/metrics`. **Full C4 remains OPEN** for: production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle (operator-out-of-band, not solved — Run 046 does NOT claim CA lifecycle); production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment trust anchors. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 046; Run 046 does not touch transport-root dependency, transport KEM, transport AEAD, forged-traffic rejection, or timeout-verification activation. **No fabricated metrics.** **No silent regression.** **No protocol behaviour change beyond the threshold value the pacer uses to decide whether to emit a local timeout.** **No removed tests, no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened.** **No new CLI flag introduced; no `--ignore-timeout-validation`-style bypass.** **Fail-closed on invalid backoff config** (`base = 0`, `max < base`, `multiplier < 1` all rejected): an operator who misconfigures the pacer gets the disabled primitive (no timeout emission) plus a warning, NOT a silent fallback to the pre-Run-046 fixed cadence. **A live-binary N=4 multi-validator backoff smoke proving multi-view backoff progression on a real binary at real `/metrics` was NOT performed in Run 046**; Run 046 proves the pacer state machine and wiring through unit tests and through the unconditional `/metrics` exposition (the five new lines render at any reachable `/metrics` scrape, with the in-process pacer state), and explicitly does NOT claim live-binary multi-view backoff smoke evidence — that is reasonable future work.
#### C4 Run 047 evidence update (2026-05-11) — live N=4 Run 046 backoff pacing evidence; full C4 and C5 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 047 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_047.md`) executes the Run 046 live-binary follow-up on the current release `qbind-node` (`sha256 561e9f83c0a1ed447fbf75fafd19f60767e396806f3fe32e9603a9b0947f8948`, ELF BuildID `42c6e7c7f6e6a23d49de2152984a77b2214d177a`, branch `copilot/continue-qbind-development-4d03ad79-e3b8-4cd8-85ed-8a80fe3bdfd9`, commit `b29dbca50f6e8b603b3a057b483b82be7298dd8b`) with N=4 `--p2p-mutual-auth required`, `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root`, real ML-DSA-44 transport delegation certs, real ML-KEM-768, real ChaCha20-Poly1305, `--require-timeout-verification`, four 0o600 ML-DSA-44 consensus signer keystores, four `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK` entries on every node, explicit data dirs, and live `/metrics` on every node via `QBIND_METRICS_HTTP_ADDR`. **No QBIND Rust source code changed.**

V1A was stopped with SIGINT under the V0-first N=4 topology. The three live validators recovered through repeated absent-V1A B14 cycles with active timeout signing/verifying: local `TimeoutMsg` logs showed emission after exactly `50` ticks of no progress and reported the Run 046 pacer moving to `level=1, next_threshold=100`; high-frequency live scrapes captured `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_current_threshold_ticks 100` and `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_backoff_level 1` after successful local timeout emission, followed by reset to `threshold=50`, `level=0` only after committed-height progress, with `backoff_increases_total` and `backoff_resets_total` moving truthfully and `qbind_consensus_view_timeout_max_cap_hits_total 0`.

B14 recovery remained live (`timeout_certificates_formed_total`, `view_timeout_advances_total`, `view_advances_due_to_verified_tc_total`, committed-height, QC and current-view progression all advanced), timeout verification stayed active (`qbind_timeout_verification_active 1`, signer/key-provider loaded, validator count 4), and the required regression set passed (`qbind-node --lib binary_consensus`, `metrics`, `forged_injection`, `run030`, full `qbind-node --lib` 791/791, `qbind-consensus --lib timeout`, `qbind-crypto --lib`, `qbind-net --lib`, Run 037/040/044 integration tests, and release builds).

**Partial-positive boundary:** normal B14 recovery committed between absent-V1A windows, so Run 047 does not prove a later local timeout emitted at the increased `100`-tick or `200`-tick threshold, and cap-hit remains deterministic-test-only evidence from Run 046. This further narrows the C4 exponential-backoff timeout-pacing item on the binary path but does NOT close full C4.

Full C4 remains OPEN for production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle, production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore, and per-environment trust anchors. C5 remains NOT closed; Run 047 does not change transport-root lifecycle policy, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, or timeout/NewView wire formats. No DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback, timeout/NewView verification rejection, duplicate local timeout emission, decode failure, engine reject, panic, FATAL, or private-key-material log was observed in the honest run.

#### C4 Run 080 implementation update (2026-05-15) — disabled-by-default peer-candidate wire send-side counterpart landed; full C4/C5 still OPEN

Run 080 lands the production-binary-facing **disabled-by-default** send-side counterpart for peer-candidate wire frames (`0x05`) without widening scope into peer-driven apply/propagation. The transport (`crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs`) now supports bounded out-of-band raw-frame enqueue per authenticated peer, and the wire module (`crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_wire.rs`) now provides `LivePeerCandidateWirePublisher` with fail-closed publish-once semantics (local envelope load → Run 078 encoder → bounded wait-for-peer → bounded per-peer enqueue report). Hidden flags were added in `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` and fail-closed required-together checks were added in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs`:

- `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-publish-enabled`
- `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-publish-path <PATH>`
- `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-publish-once`

Run 080 also adds send-side counters on `P2pMetrics` (no `_applied_total`, no `peer_candidate_wire_*` family): `peer_candidate_sent_total`, `peer_candidate_send_failure_total`, `peer_candidate_send_no_peer_total`, `peer_candidate_send_oversize_total`. Regression evidence currently shows unit/integration pass for sender-side encode/oversize/no-peer/failure accounting and preserves non-mutation boundaries (no local apply, no sequence write, no live trust mutation, no session eviction, no rebroadcast). **Boundary explicitly retained:** release-binary N=2 two-process `0x05` exchange artifacts are not yet recorded in this contradiction update; therefore C4 is only narrowed to “validation-only wire exchange plumbing present,” and full C4/C5 remain OPEN for peer-driven live apply/propagation, activation_epoch runtime source, in-binary/on-chain signing-key ratification, KMS/HSM custody, production fast-sync/consensus-storage restore, and per-environment production trust-anchor operations.

#### C4 Run 048 evidence update (2026-05-11) — live N=7 multi-step Run 046 backoff pacing evidence; full C4 and C5 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 048 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_048.md`) executes the smallest safe live-binary follow-up to Run 047 on the byte-identical release `qbind-node` (`sha256 561e9f83c0a1ed447fbf75fafd19f60767e396806f3fe32e9603a9b0947f8948`, ELF BuildID `42c6e7c7f6e6a23d49de2152984a77b2214d177a`) using an **N=7** topology with V1 and V2 simultaneously SIGINT-stopped after warmup (consecutive absent leaders under the round-robin `view % 7` schedule; f=2, quorum=5; five live validators V0/V3/V4/V5/V6 are *exactly* the quorum, so TC formation and proposal commits both remain quorum-safe under honest traffic). **Strongest positive verdict.** Live `qbind-node` binaries with `--p2p-mutual-auth required`, `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root`, real ML-DSA-44 transport delegation certs, real ML-KEM-768, real ChaCha20-Poly1305, `--require-timeout-verification`, seven 0o600 ML-DSA-44 consensus signer keystores, seven `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK` entries on every node, explicit data dirs, and live `/metrics` on every node prove on log lines AND on high-frequency `/metrics` scrapes:

3. **Third local `TimeoutMsg` at the further-increased 200-tick threshold** on V0 for view 64 — bonus evidence — with the pacer log `threshold=200 ticks, level=3, next_threshold=400 ticks` reproducing the deterministic Run 046 schedule `50 → 100 → 200 → 400` end-to-end on a real binary; V0's `committed_height` stayed at `31` throughout the captured 40-second window (V0 lagged on commit application), so V0's pacer never reset and continued doubling through `400` while V3/V4/V5/V6 each reset back to base `50` after B14 recovery committed heights `54 → 58/59` and then re-incremented to `100` on the next absent-leader window (view 64 for V1 absent), giving `view_timeouts_emitted_total = 3`, `backoff_increases_total = 3`, `backoff_resets_total = 1`, `max_cap_hits_total = 0` on V3/V4/V5/V6.

#### C4 Run 049 evidence update (2026-05-11) — live 800-tick timeout-backoff cap-hit evidence; full C4 and C5 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 049 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_049.md`) closes the Run 048 live cap-hit boundary on the byte-identical release `qbind-node` (`sha256 561e9f83c0a1ed447fbf75fafd19f60767e396806f3fe32e9603a9b0947f8948`, ELF BuildID `42c6e7c7f6e6a23d49de2152984a77b2214d177a`) using the same safe **N=7** topology with V1 and V2 simultaneously stopped after warmup (f=2, quorum=5, live validators V0/V3/V4/V5/V6 exactly preserve quorum). **Strongest positive verdict.** Live `qbind-node` binaries with `--p2p-mutual-auth required`, `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root`, real ML-DSA-44 transport delegation certs, real ML-KEM-768, real ChaCha20-Poly1305, `--require-timeout-verification`, seven 0o600 ML-DSA-44 consensus signer keystores, seven `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK` entries on every node, explicit data dirs, and live `/metrics` on every node prove the Run 046 binary-path pacer reaches and saturates at `800` ticks truthfully. V6 independently showed threshold `800`, level `4`, and cap hits `0 → 1 → 2`. Threshold never exceeded `800` in any captured scrape; no scrape showed cap hits while threshold was below `800`; `backoff_increases_total` did not increment for the already-at-cap attempt; and no duplicate local timeout for the same validator/view was found.

B14 safety and timeout verification remained preserved.
