The real PQC transport stack stayed active (`pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root`, `transport_kem_suite_name=ml-kem-768`, `transport_aead_suite_name=chacha20-poly1305`, `dummy_kem_registered=false`, `dummy_aead_registered=false`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total=0` and all per-reason cert-rejection counters `0`). Required regressions passed: `qbind-node --lib binary_consensus` 63/63, `metrics` 102/102, `forged_injection` 21/21, `run030` 20/20, `t146_timeout_view_change_tests` 15/15, Run 037/040/044 integration tests 12/12, 14/14, 10/10, full `qbind-node --lib` 791/791, `qbind-consensus --lib timeout` 54/54 selected, `qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68, `qbind-net --lib` 17/17, and release builds clean.

#### C4 Run 050 evidence update (2026-05-12) — production-honest PQC trust-anchor bundle foundation; root-level lifecycle NARROWED; signed-bundle verification and leaf-level revocation remain OPEN; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 050 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_050.md`) lands the smallest production-honest foundation layer for PQC transport trust-anchor lifecycle on top of the Run 037 / 039 / 040 / 045 / 049 stack, on the release `qbind-node` binary `sha256 d05c28e4c069117a74293b163f0d63f12d3460de4e50ae47769068473392bdb5` (ELF BuildID `3a42b69feba597ecbf8b0c0ed139ce80e0f05ecf`) and the matching helper `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` (`sha256 61e6c29dd1d83c0f7650efca05ee5b1daec86ce7e183955363912b091eaa4536`).

**Strongest positive verdict for the scoped layer; explicit partial for the full C4 piece.** A structured, environment-bound, canonically-hashable PQC trust-anchor bundle (`crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs`) is now wired into `qbind-node`'s `pqc-static-root` startup via the new `--p2p-trust-bundle <PATH>` flag. The bundle carries per-environment binding (`devnet`/`testnet`/`mainnet`), per-root validity windows and `active|retired|revoked` status, explicit `revocations[]` defence-in-depth entries, schema-versioned metadata (`bundle_version`, `generated_at`, `valid_from`, `valid_until`, `sequence`, optional `chain_id`), and a deterministic `SHA3-256` fingerprint over the canonical JSON encoding with the signature envelope stripped. Loading fails closed (the binary refuses to start) on any of: unsupported schema version, wrong environment, malformed JSON, malformed hex, wrong-length ML-DSA-44 public key, inverted bundle/root validity window, not-yet-valid or expired bundle, not-yet-valid or expired Active root, duplicate `root_id`, unsupported suite id (only `100` = ML-DSA-44 accepted), revocation referencing an unknown root, duplicate revocation entry, signing-key id colliding with any `root_id`, an unsigned bundle on TestNet or MainNet, or any non-null `signature` field on any environment. Live `qbind-node` proved seven negative fixtures (`wrong-environment`, `expired-bundle`, `expired-root`, `duplicate-root`, `unsupported-suite`, `root-status-revoked`, `root-revocation-listed`) each exit `1` with the precise `FATAL` reason in `[binary]` logs, AND the positive `valid` fixture loaded the bundle, brought the transport up with `pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root`, surfaced `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_loaded=1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_environment=0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_active_roots=1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revoked_roots=0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence=1` on `/metrics`, kept `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total=0` and all per-reason cert-rejection counters at `0`, did NOT register `DummySig`/`DummyKem`/`DummyAead`, did NOT silently fall back to `--p2p-trusted-root` on bundle failure, and never wrote `root_sk` or any private-key bytes to any log or artefact file. Unit tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 27/27; integration tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 13/13; metrics suite 102/102; full `qbind-node --lib` 818/818 (was 791 before Run 050; +27 from the new module); `run_037_*` 12/12, `run_040_*` 14/14, `run_044_*` 10/10 unchanged; `qbind-net --lib` 17/17; `qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; release builds clean.

**C4 root-level trust-anchor lifecycle is NARROWED for DevNet.** Loading + canonical validation + environment binding + status filtering + validity-window filtering + root-level revocation enforcement + deterministic fingerprint + fail-closed startup are now proven on a real `qbind-node` release binary with real ML-DSA-44 + real ML-KEM-768 + real ChaCha20-Poly1305 + no Dummy fallback.

**Signed-bundle (ML-DSA-44) verification is explicitly NOT IMPLEMENTED in Run 050 and remains OPEN under C4.** The schema includes a `TrustBundleSignature { signing_key_id, suite_id, sig_bytes }` envelope so that operators can already author signed bundles, but `TrustBundle::validate_at` rejects any non-null `signature` with `SignedBundleVerificationNotImplemented`, refusing to silently treat an unverified signature as verified. Because of this, TestNet and MainNet bundle distribution is also explicitly NOT operational in Run 050: the validator refuses unsigned bundles on TestNet/MainNet (`UnsignedBundleNotAllowed(env)`) AND refuses signed bundles on TestNet/MainNet (`SignedBundleVerificationNotImplemented`), so any TestNet/MainNet deployment must keep using the pre-Run-050 CLI `--p2p-trusted-root` path until the signed-bundle-verification piece lands. DevNet retains the unsigned-bundle scaffolding to keep operator iteration cheap.

**Leaf-level revocation enforcement remains OPEN.** The schema records `revocations[i].leaf_cert_fingerprint` and integration tests exercise the field, but the live `NetworkDelegationCert` verify path does not yet consult it. Recorded as remaining.

**Activation epoch / activation height gating remains OPEN.** `roots[i].activation_epoch` and `roots[i].activation_height` are accepted by the schema but the runtime does NOT yet gate a root's acceptance on a consensus epoch or height; only wall-clock `not_before`/`not_after` is enforced today. Recorded as remaining.

**Sequence-number monotonicity persistence remains OPEN.** `sequence` is recorded in the bundle and surfaced on `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence`, but the validator does not yet persist a "highest sequence ever loaded" pin to refuse rollback to an older bundle. Recorded as remaining.

**`chain_id` crosscheck remains OPEN.** `bundle.chain_id` is parsed but not yet matched against `NodeConfig.chain_id` at load time. Recorded as remaining.

**Static-roots vs bundle conflict policy is defined and enforced.** DevNet allows both `--p2p-trust-bundle` and `--p2p-trusted-root` (the bundle's active roots are merged into the CLI roots, deduplicated by `root_key_id`). TestNet and MainNet refuse the combination with a FATAL `cannot be combined on environment={} (only DevNet allows the operator override)` message — no silent precedence, no silent fallback. The Run 037 invariant "Required + pqc-static-root demands ≥ 1 trusted root" is preserved end-to-end: a bundle whose every root is retired/revoked/expired (yielding `active_roots = 0`) is loaded by the schema validator (so operators can still inspect the parsed result via logs and metrics) but then fails closed at the existing Required-mode guard in `main.rs`. This is observable in the `root-status-revoked` and `root-revocation-listed` smokes.

**Trust-separation policy is encoded in the schema.** Even when signed-bundle verification lands, `TrustBundleSignature.signing_key_id` MUST NOT collide with any `roots[i].root_id`; collision is rejected by the validator (`SigningKeyCollidesWithRootId`). This prevents a compromised transport root from being retroactively elevated to a bundle-distribution authority.

**Full C4 remains OPEN** for: signed-bundle (ML-DSA-44) verification; production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle; production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment trust anchors for TestNet and MainNet specifically (DevNet binding is now proven end-to-end on a live binary; TestNet/MainNet binding is proven only by unit + integration tests, not by a live-binary TestNet/MainNet startup); leaf-level cert revocation enforcement; activation epoch/height gating; sequence-number monotonicity persistence; `chain_id` crosscheck. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 050; Run 050 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the bundle layer. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no operator bypass on TestNet/MainNet**, **no leak of `root_sk` or any private-key bytes to any log or artefact file** were observed in the honest run. Specifically there is no path on which a bundle failure silently degrades to the pre-Run-050 `--p2p-trusted-root` CLI path: bundle failure produces `[binary] FATAL: --p2p-trust-bundle load/validate failed for path=…: <reason>. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade).` and `std::process::exit(1)`.


**C4 piece "exponential-backoff timeout pacing" is now LIVE-EVIDENCE COMPLETE on the binary path** for the Run 046 schedule and cap semantics: `50 → 100 → 200 → 400 → 800 → 800`, committed-height-only reset, no view-only reset, one local timeout per view, truthful `max_cap_hits_total`, threshold capped at `800`, and no fabricated metrics. **Full C4 remains OPEN** for: production CA / cert rotation / cert revocation / signed root distribution lifecycle; production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment trust anchors. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 049; Run 049 does not change transport-root lifecycle policy, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, timeout/NewView wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics. No QBIND production/library/protocol source code changed; only the Run 049 evidence document and this C4 tracking update were added.

#### C4 Run 051 evidence update (2026-05-12) — signed PQC trust-bundle ML-DSA-44 verification LIVE; signed root distribution NARROWED for DevNet + TestNet (positive live-binary smoke); leaf-level revocation, activation gating, sequence persistence, chain_id crosscheck, full production CA/rotation playbook remain OPEN; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 051 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_051.md`) replaces the Run 050 `SignedBundleVerificationNotImplemented` boundary with a real, fail-closed ML-DSA-44 signed-bundle verification path, on the release `qbind-node` binary `sha256 5f081df0f97db1ceb99e5461a61af273fb12484fc2da2091f29fb88a77c89533` (ELF BuildID `8206eade49aa80f0dcd22aa21dd52c4e8933e1c7`) and the matching helper `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` (`sha256 da2f476ded67f41d926f4af8a389bea8b53431b973c79e35aad61c3bdbda3ebf`, ELF BuildID `4c87d078d9f78bee7af5594abca4386541225cbc`).

**Strongest positive verdict for the scoped signed-root-distribution layer.** `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs` now exposes `BundleSigningKey` / `BundleSigningKeySet` with a strict `KEYID:SUITE:PK` parser (32-byte hex KEYID, suite `100` = ML-DSA-44 only, exact ML-DSA-44 public-key length, duplicate-KEYID rejected, malformed-hex rejected, trailing/empty fields rejected), a `canonical_signing_bytes(bundle)` preimage prefixed by the dedicated domain separator `QBIND:pqc-trust-bundle-signature:v1` (distinct from the `QBIND:pqc-trust-bundle-fp:v1` fingerprint separator) over the canonical JSON encoding of the bundle with the `signature` envelope stripped, a `TrustBundle::validate_at_with_signing_keys` and matching `load_from_path_with_signing_keys` / `load_from_bytes_with_signing_keys` entry points that actually verify the ML-DSA-44 signature, and the explicit fail-closed variants `MissingSigningKey`, `UnsupportedSignatureSuite`, `SignatureSuiteMismatch`, `MalformedSignatureBytes`, `BadSignature`. The legacy `SignedBundleVerificationNotImplemented` variant is retained as `#[doc(hidden)]` for source-level back-compat but is never produced by the new verify path. CLI surface: the new repeatable `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key KEYID:SUITE:PK` flag is wired into `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` and `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs`. `main.rs` parses the flag once up front, refuses startup on a parse error, enforces trust-separation between the configured bundle-signing key list and the configured `--p2p-trusted-root` set (collision in either direction fails closed), refuses startup on TestNet/MainNet whenever `--p2p-trust-bundle` is supplied without at least one signing key, and warns (but does not abort) when signing keys are supplied without a bundle. On a successful verified-signed-bundle startup, `main.rs` bumps `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_verified_total` by exactly one; on any signed-bundle envelope rejection (`MissingSigningKey`, `UnsupportedSignatureSuite`, `SignatureSuiteMismatch`, `MalformedSignatureBytes`, `BadSignature`) it bumps `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_rejected_total` by exactly one before the fail-closed `std::process::exit(1)`. The trust-bundle log line now reports `signature=verified(signing_key_id=XXXXXXXX..)` or `signature=unsigned`, never `signed=false` as a blanket claim.

**Live-binary evidence (release `qbind-node`).** Positive DevNet signed-bundle smoke: `qbind-node --env devnet --p2p-mutual-auth required --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root --p2p-trust-bundle /tmp/run051/signed-devnet/trust-bundle.json --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key 53453d8f…:100:ac4397f6… --p2p-leaf-cert … --p2p-leaf-cert-key …` logs `[binary] Run 050/051: trust bundle loaded path=… env=devnet fp=49d28006… active_roots=1 revoked_roots=0 sequence=1 signature=verified(signing_key_id=53453d8f..) signing_keys_configured=1`, registers `pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root sig_suite_id=100 transport_kem_suite_id=100 transport_kem_suite_name=ml-kem-768 dummy_kem_registered=false transport_aead_suite_id=101 transport_aead_suite_name=chacha20-poly1305 dummy_aead_registered=false configured_roots=1`, stays up healthily through the 6-second smoke window (exit 124), commits binary-consensus anchors heights 28…57+, and on `/metrics` surfaces `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_loaded 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_environment 0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_active_roots 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revoked_roots 0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_verified_total 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_rejected_total 0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_keys_configured 1`, with `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total 0` and no `DummySig`/`DummyKem`/`DummyAead` fallback. Positive TestNet signed-bundle smoke (`--env testnet`, signed TestNet bundle, signing-key flag): `[binary] Run 050/051: trust bundle loaded path=… env=testnet fp=81b21565… active_roots=1 revoked_roots=0 sequence=1 signature=verified(signing_key_id=560a2082..)`, same `pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root` + `dummy_*=false` shape, process stays up through the 6-second smoke window. Negative live-binary smokes: `signed-tampered` exits `1` with `trust bundle ML-DSA-44 signature verification failed for signing_key_id b3398073… (tampered bundle or forged envelope — fail closed)`; `signed-wrong-key` exits `1` with `trust bundle signature references signing_key_id f203bf76… but no matching --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key was configured (fail closed)`; `signed-unsupported-suite` exits `1` with `trust bundle signature for signing_key_id 720ceede… uses unsupported suite_id 99 (only 100 = ML-DSA-44 accepted)`; `signed-malformed` exits `1` with `trust bundle signature for signing_key_id 9a5f55d3… has malformed sig_bytes: expected 2420 bytes, got 1`; `signed-key-root-collision` exits `1` with `trust bundle signing_key_id fe4ef9b8… collides with a transport root_id (trust-separation policy fails closed)`; `unsigned-testnet` exits `1` (with signing-key supplied, via the loader): `trust bundle is unsigned but environment testnet requires a signed bundle`; `unsigned-mainnet` exits `1` (without signing-key supplied, via the new TestNet/MainNet+bundle pre-check): `--p2p-trust-bundle … on environment=MainNet requires at least one --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`. **No fallback to `--p2p-trusted-root`** on any bundle-signature failure: every FATAL line ends with `No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade)`.

**Tests.** Unit tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 56/56 (was 27/27 in Run 050; +29 from the new Run 051 signing-key parser, canonical-signing-bytes, and signature-verification tests). Integration tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 13/13 (unchanged; the back-compat 3-arg `load_from_bytes` shim routes through the new verify path with an empty signing-key set); metrics suite 102/102 + 2 new (`pqc_trust_bundle_signature_metrics_start_at_zero_and_increment_atomically`, `pqc_trust_bundle_signature_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`); full `qbind-node --lib` 847/847 (was 818/818 before Run 051; +29 from new tests); `run_037_*` 12/12, `run_040_*` 14/14, `run_044_*` 10/10 unchanged; `qbind-net --lib` 17/17; `qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; release builds clean.

**Trust-separation policy is now both schema-encoded and CLI-encoded.** `signature.signing_key_id` MUST NOT collide with any `roots[i].root_id` in the bundle (`SigningKeyCollidesWithRootId` — Run 050 invariant, preserved); additionally, a `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key KEYID:…` MUST NOT collide with any `--p2p-trusted-root` KEYID configured on the same CLI invocation (`main.rs` fails closed before bundle load with `FATAL: --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key <id> collides with a configured --p2p-trusted-root id`). Both directions of the trust-separation invariant are enforced, so a compromised transport root cannot be retroactively elevated to a bundle-distribution authority and a compromised bundle-signing key cannot be retroactively elevated to a transport root.

**Environment policy (Run 051 final).** DevNet — unsigned bundle accepted (Run 050 scaffolding preserved); signed bundle verified against the configured signing-key set; missing key / bad signature / malformed sig_bytes / unsupported suite / suite mismatch fail closed. TestNet — unsigned bundle refused (`UnsignedBundleNotAllowed(Testnet)`); signed bundle verified or fails closed; `--p2p-trust-bundle` without `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key` fails closed before load. MainNet — same as TestNet. `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key` without `--p2p-trust-bundle` is a documented warning-only no-op (the live trust set is unchanged), not a fail-closed condition; this is the only intentional non-fail-closed branch on the Run 051 surface and is recorded here explicitly.

**Full C4 remains OPEN** for: leaf-level certificate revocation enforcement (no leaf-cert revocation introduced in Run 051; bundle-level `revocations[]` still only revokes whole roots); activation `epoch`/`height` gating (still recorded, not enforced); sequence-number monotonicity persistence (still recorded, not persisted across reboots / not cross-checked at load against any on-disk lower-bound); `chain_id` crosscheck against the runtime chain id (still recorded, not crosschecked); production CA / certificate rotation operator playbook (the helper still generates ephemeral DevNet bundle-signing keys in process; production signing remains an out-of-process KMS task); production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment production trust anchors for MainNet specifically (DevNet + TestNet are now proven end-to-end on the live release binary in Run 051; MainNet signed-bundle startup is proven by unit + integration tests + the same `validate_at_with_signing_keys` codepath, but a real-binary MainNet startup with a production-grade signing key was not performed and remains a separate evidence run). **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 051; Run 051 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle layer. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no operator bypass on TestNet/MainNet** (unsigned bundle refused; signed bundle without signing-key refused at the binary boundary; signed bundle with a bad/wrong/malformed/unsupported-suite signature fails closed at the validator boundary), **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority** (both directions of trust-separation enforced), **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only), and **no leak of `root_sk` or `signing_sk` or any private-key bytes to any log or artefact file** (the helper holds both secret keys in memory only and the live binary never receives a secret-key flag) were observed in the honest run.
#### C4 Run 052 evidence update (2026-05-12) — leaf-level certificate revocation enforcement; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 052 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_052.md`) wires the existing trust-bundle `revocations[].leaf_cert_fingerprint` surface into the `pqc-static-root` PQC delegation cert verification path on both the listener and dialer side. A new `LeafCertRevocationList` Arc-backed lookup is plumbed through `qbind_net::ServerHandshakeConfig.leaf_cert_revocations` and `qbind_net::ClientHandshakeConfig.leaf_cert_revocations` (default `None` is a zero-cost no-op preserving Run 044 behaviour bit-for-bit). The listener-side `parse_and_verify_client_cert` and the dialer-side `ClientHandshake::handle_server_accept` both compute the verified cert's canonical 32-byte leaf fingerprint AFTER all signature + validity-window + (dialer) validator-id checks pass, look it up in the configured revocation list, and on hit fail closed with `NetError::ClientCertInvalid("cert revoked")` while bumping `inc_rejected_revoked` exactly once and skipping `inc_accepted`. The qbind-node `P2pMetrics` adapter forwards `inc_rejected_revoked` onto the new `inc_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked` setter, which moves both the new `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total` counter and the aggregate `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total` (Run 037 contract preserved). The trust bundle now interprets `revocations[].leaf_cert_fingerprint = Some(fp)` as a leaf-only revocation that does NOT exclude the corresponding root from `active_roots` (the `None` shape is preserved as the Run 050 root-level revocation); a malformed `leaf_cert_fingerprint` (not 64 lowercase hex chars) fails the bundle load closed with `MalformedLeafFingerprint { root_id, reason }`; `effective_from` is honored so future-dated leaf entries are not yet active. The `qbind-node` builder gains a new `with_pqc_leaf_revocations(Arc<HashSet<[u8;32]>>)` setter and `main.rs` derives the active set from `loaded.revoked_leaf_fingerprints` and emits `[binary] Run 052: revoked_leaf_fingerprints=N (from trust bundle env=… sequence=…)` on every startup. The wiring is gated on `MutualAuthMode::Required | Optional` AND `cfg.mode == PqcRootMode::PqcStaticRoot` AND `!revoked_set.is_empty()`; the test-grade DummySig path and the empty-active-set path both take the zero-cost no-op path with no `LeafCertRevocationList` installed, mirroring the Run 044 cert-verify-metrics-sink discipline.

**Tests.** Unit tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 65/65 (was 56/56 in Run 051; +9 from the new Run 052 `cert_leaf_fingerprint` determinism, distinct domain separator, surfaced-lookup, future-dated-not-yet-active, malformed-fp-fail-closed, root+leaf coexistence, and unsigned-DevNet regression tests; minus 2 from the Run 050 root-level revocation tests retired in favour of the new explicit shape). Integration tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12, `--test run_044_pqc_cert_verify_metrics_adapter_tests` 10/10, `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 13/13, `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13 — all unchanged. `cargo test -p qbind-net` 175/175 (was 166/166 before Run 052; +9 from the new handshake-boundary tests; the +157 mechanical struct-update for `leaf_cert_revocations: None` adds no new test cases). `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib metrics` 104/104 (was 102/102; +2 from the new revoked-counter zero/non-zero rendering tests; the existing `run_043_*` non-zero propagation test was updated from aggregate=6 to aggregate=7 to account for the new sub-counter that also bumps the aggregate). `cargo test -p qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; release `qbind-node` library + binary builds clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to this run).

**No-fallback proof (Run 052).** The leaf-revocation surface is wired ONLY on the production-honest PQC path. The `PqcStaticRootConfig::trusted_roots` vector surfaced from a Run-052-revoked signed bundle still carries only `PQC_TRANSPORT_SUITE_ML_DSA_44` roots and `PqcRootMode::PqcStaticRoot` is preserved on the wire — both discriminators that would change if a future regression silently fell back to a test-grade `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` primitive. The `--p2p-trusted-root` legacy CLI list is not a fallback target — Run 052 wiring keys off the LOADED TRUST BUNDLE (`loaded.revoked_leaf_fingerprints`), not the `--p2p-trusted-root` list. The `no_fallback_to_test_grade_dummy_primitives_for_pqc_path` integration test pins this assertion. Cross-crate fingerprint determinism (qbind-node `cert_leaf_fingerprint` ≡ qbind-net `leaf_cert_fingerprint`) is asserted by an integration test, plus a separate test pins `TRUST_BUNDLE_LEAF_FINGERPRINT_DOMAIN_SEPARATOR == LEAF_CERT_FINGERPRINT_DOMAIN_SEPARATOR` so that a future drift would fail at compile + test time, not silently allow a revoked leaf onto the network.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 052).** Activation epoch / height gating for revocation entries (only `effective_from` UNIX seconds is honored today). Sequence-number monotonicity persistence across restarts. `chain_id` crosscheck. Operator-facing CA + rotation playbook. Live-binary release-build smoke artifacts for revoked-leaf fixtures (the smoke shape is identical to Run 051; the artifact set was not produced in this session and is recorded as the explicit remaining boundary). These are explicitly out of scope for Run 052 and remain as later C4 items so future runs can pick them up without ambiguity.
#### C4 Run 053 evidence update (2026-05-12)

DevNet Evidence Run 053 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_053.md`) closes the narrow trust-bundle `chain_id` crosscheck item left open by Runs 050–052. `TrustBundle` now accepts legacy `chain_id: null` bundles for compatibility, but when `chain_id` is present it must parse as a 64-bit lowercase hex chain id and match the runtime `NodeConfig.chain_id()` passed by `qbind-node`'s live `--p2p-trust-bundle` path. Malformed or mismatched chain ids fail closed before roots are merged into the PQC trust set. This does not close full C4: activation epoch/height gating, sequence persistence, operator CA/rotation playbook, and the broader production-operability items remain open.

#### C4 Run 054 evidence update (2026-05-12) — live-binary release-build smoke for Run 052 leaf-level certificate revocation enforcement; explicit boundary from Run 052 NARROWED on DevNet; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 054 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_054.md`) closes the explicit "live-binary release-build smoke artifacts for revoked-leaf fixtures" boundary that Run 052 recorded as remaining-open, on the live release `qbind-node` binary `sha256 2b68a090f131c38306d8e8b47d0e28719a0804c6e19f1f251e9470364e61facf` (ELF BuildID `379f2260cf3835b59eb8710c4c7e3f41b28be5de`) and the matching Run-054 helper `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` `sha256 9166626a31b0ed37547dd525de454a45602bd1abf810321bf41e6e33842d04fc` (ELF BuildID `e53080be76c9f6bb56fd5ea06f9f41cbcd51759a`). Run 054 is **evidence-only** — the only source-tree edit is an additive extension to the existing DevNet helper `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs` adding three new fixture modes (`signed-devnet-revoked-v0`, `signed-devnet-revoked-v1`, `signed-devnet-revoked-unknown`) that mirror the Run 051 signed-bundle helper flow and inject one active `TrustBundleRevocation { leaf_cert_fingerprint: Some(fp), … }` entry into the bundle BEFORE signing, plus an additional helper output `v<N>.leaf-fp.hex` that captures the canonical 32-byte leaf fingerprint of each issued cert (verbatim what the live binary computes via Run 052's `cert_leaf_fingerprint`). No `crates/**/src/**` core library source, no protocol source, no test source, and no `Cargo.toml` was touched; Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, Run 050, Run 051, Run 052, and Run 053 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit.

**Live-binary smoke evidence (Run 054).** Four release-binary smokes were run with `--p2p-mutual-auth required --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root --p2p-trust-bundle … --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key …` and no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback: (1) Positive non-revoked signed-bundle two-node smoke (`signed-devnet` bundle, V0+V1 on `127.0.0.1:19410/19411`) — both nodes connect and verify peer leaf certs, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total = 2`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total = 0` on each side, `signature=verified(signing_key_id=dad1b167..)`. (2) Negative revoked-local-leaf single-node startup (`signed-devnet-revoked-v0` bundle) — node starts; `[binary] Run 052: revoked_leaf_fingerprints=1 (from trust bundle env=devnet sequence=1)` surfaces at boot; the node does NOT exit non-zero on its own because Run 052's wiring is wire-level only (no startup self-check exists today); the task's conditional language ("**if** local self-check sees the revocation") is honored — this absence is recorded as a small, well-scoped remaining-open C4 item rather than fabricated. (3) **Strongest positive — negative revoked-peer-leaf two-node mutual-auth smoke** (`signed-devnet-revoked-v1` bundle, V0+V1 on `127.0.0.1:19430/19431`) — V0 stderr shows BOTH `[P2P] Inbound connection error: Handshake error: channel error: Net(Protocol("server handle_client_init failed"))` (listener path: V0's `parse_and_verify_client_cert` refused V1's revoked cert) AND `[P2P] dial 127.0.0.1:19431 giving up after 1 attempt(s): Handshake error: channel error: Net(Protocol("client handle_server_accept failed"))` (dialer path: V0's `ClientHandshake::handle_server_accept` refused V1's revoked cert); V0 `/metrics` shows `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total 2` AND `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total 2` AND `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total 0` — the Run 052 metric contract (`inc_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked` bumps both the sub-counter and the aggregate; `inc_accepted` is skipped) is now proven on the live release binary, not just in handshake-boundary unit tests. (4) Negative unknown-leaf-fingerprint two-node smoke (`signed-devnet-revoked-unknown` bundle revokes the all-zeros 64-hex fingerprint that no real cert can produce; V0+V1 on `127.0.0.1:19440/19441`) — both nodes connect and verify normally, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total = 2`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total = 0` on each side — proving the Run 052 zero-cost-no-op invariant on a non-empty revocation set where the actual cert fingerprints do not collide.

**Tests.** All required regression suites rerun on the release profile and remain green: `cargo test --release -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 68/68; `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `--test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test --release -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `--test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12; `--test run_040_pqc_static_root_real_aead_tests` 14/14; `--test run_044_pqc_cert_verify_metrics_adapter_tests` 10/10; `--lib metrics` 104/104; `--lib p2p` 138/138; full `cargo test --release -p qbind-node --lib` 859/859; `cargo test --release -p qbind-net --lib` 17/17; `cargo test --release -p qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; `cargo check --release -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 054). `binary_consensus`, `forged_injection`, `run030`, and `qbind-consensus --lib timeout` were intentionally not rerun because Run 054 did not modify any source on those paths (only a DevNet example helper was extended).

**No-fallback proof (Run 054).** Every Run-054 smoke emitted `[Run040] P2pNodeBuilder: pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root sig_suite_id=100 transport_kem_suite_id=100 transport_kem_suite_name=ml-kem-768 dummy_kem_registered=false transport_aead_suite_id=101 transport_aead_suite_name=chacha20-poly1305 dummy_aead_registered=false configured_roots=1 leaf_credentials_present=true` verbatim, proving real ML-DSA-44 + real ML-KEM-768 + real ChaCha20-Poly1305 on the active cert-verify path and the absence of `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead`. No `--p2p-trusted-root` was supplied on any smoke; the trust set was sourced exclusively from the signed `--p2p-trust-bundle`. The Run 052 wiring keys off `LoadedTrustBundle::revoked_leaf_fingerprints`, not off `--p2p-trusted-root` — confirmed by the integration test `no_fallback_to_test_grade_dummy_primitives_for_pqc_path` (still 12/12 pass). The Run 054 helper still mints all root and signing keys ephemerally in memory and never writes `root_sk` or `signing_sk` to disk; no private-key bytes appear in any Run-054 log artefact. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only), and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 054).** Activation epoch / height gating for revocation entries (only `effective_from` UNIX seconds is honored). Sequence-number monotonicity persistence across restarts. Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook (the helper still mints ephemeral DevNet bundle-signing keys in process; production signing remains an out-of-process KMS task). Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore. Live MainNet signed-bundle release-binary smoke with a production-grade signing key (Run 054 ran DevNet only; MainNet signed-bundle startup is proven by unit + integration tests + the same `validate_at_with_signing_keys` codepath that powers DevNet, but a real-binary MainNet smoke was deliberately not performed). A startup self-check in `qbind-node/src/main.rs` that fails the binary closed when `--p2p-leaf-cert` matches an active entry in the loaded bundle's `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` (Run 052 deliberately did not ship one; Run 054 records this as a small, well-scoped future C4 item — documented honestly rather than fabricated). **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 054; Run 054 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle leaf-revocation evidence surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**

#### C4 Run 055 evidence update (2026-05-12) — trust-bundle sequence-number monotonicity persistence across restarts; explicit Run-050/051/052/054 boundary NARROWED; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 055 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_055.md`) closes the explicit "sequence-number monotonicity persistence across restarts" boundary that Runs 050, 051, 052, and 054 each recorded as remaining-open. A new pure-Rust module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_sequence.rs` adds a persistent, atomically written JSON record under `<data_dir>/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` that captures the highest signed-bundle `sequence` accepted on this node for the runtime `(environment, chain_id)` trust domain, together with the corresponding canonical bundle fingerprint. On every subsequent startup the just-validated bundle's sequence is compared against the persisted record before any bundle root is merged into the live PQC trust set: a strictly lower sequence is rejected as a rollback attempt (`SequenceRollback`); an equal sequence with a different canonical fingerprint is rejected as equivocation (`EqualSequenceFingerprintMismatch`); an equal sequence with the same canonical fingerprint is accepted as a no-op restart (no record rewrite); a strictly higher sequence is accepted and the record is updated via a tmp-file + rename atomic write that `sync_all`s the tmp file before rename so a mid-write crash leaves either the old record or a harmless `.tmp` sibling but never a corrupt destination. A persisted record carrying a different `environment` or `chain_id` than the runtime trust domain fails closed (`WrongEnvironment` / `WrongChainId`) — a stray DevNet record cannot leak into a MainNet startup, or vice versa. A malformed / unsupported-`record_version` / non-hex-`chain_id` / non-hex-fingerprint persistence file fails closed (`Malformed` / `UnsupportedRecordVersion`); the module never silently truncates, resets, or rewrites a corrupted file. A persistence write failure fails closed (`PersistFailure`) — the bundle is NOT accepted if its new highest sequence cannot be recorded, otherwise a subsequent restart could re-accept the same or an older bundle without record. Wiring lives in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` after the Run 051 ML-DSA-44 signature verification and the Run 053 chain-id crosscheck but BEFORE the bundle's `active_roots` are merged into `trusted_roots`, so any of the failure modes above prevents new trust anchors from entering the live PQC trust set on a rejected restart.

**Strict scope (NOT covered by Run 055).** Run 055 is anti-rollback persistence ONLY. It does NOT implement activation `epoch` / `height` gating for revocation or root-status entries (still recorded as a separate remaining-open C4 item). It does NOT implement an operator-facing CA / certificate-rotation / signing-key-rotation playbook (still remaining-open). It does NOT implement live MainNet signed-bundle release-binary smokes with production-grade signing keys (still remaining-open). It does NOT touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, fast-sync, consensus-storage restore, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle persistence layer.

**`--data-dir` policy.** Sequence persistence requires `--data-dir` because the record must live on disk. Run 055 wires this fail-closed on TestNet/MainNet: a `--p2p-trust-bundle` run without `--data-dir` on TestNet or MainNet now exits non-zero with `FATAL: --p2p-trust-bundle … on environment={} requires --data-dir so the bundle's sequence number can be persisted across restarts. Without persistence, an older signed bundle could be replayed after a restart (anti-rollback regression).` On DevNet a `--p2p-trust-bundle` without `--data-dir` emits `[binary] Run 055 WARNING: --p2p-trust-bundle supplied without --data-dir on environment=devnet; trust-bundle sequence anti-rollback persistence is NOT active for this run (DevNet convenience; TestNet/MainNet would fail closed).` and proceeds — this is the same DevNet-convenience shape used elsewhere in the binary and is explicitly documented rather than silently weakened.

**Trust-domain key.** The persisted record is keyed by the `(environment, chain_id)` tuple. The persistence file path is supplied by the caller (today always `<data_dir>/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json`), so two independent nodes operating on different `data_dir`s have independent records. The in-file `(environment, chain_id)` pair defence-in-depths against a stray file under a freshly configured `data_dir` whose environment or chain id does not match.

**Metrics.** Four new metrics are surfaced through the `qbind-node` `/metrics` HTTP scrape path on the shared `P2pMetrics` Arc: `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_highest` (gauge, mirrors the persisted highest sequence after a successful startup; 0 when no bundle was loaded or no persistence file exists yet), `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_rollback_rejected_total` (counter, bumped on every rejected rollback), `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_equal_fingerprint_mismatch_total` (counter, bumped on every rejected equivocation attempt), and `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_persist_failures_total` (counter, bumped on any I/O / serialise / rename failure writing the sequence record). The Run 050/051/052/053/054 metrics are preserved bit-for-bit; the new families render exactly once per metrics body (asserted by `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`). In the binary's fail-closed startup path the process exits before `/metrics` is scraped, so the rollback/equivocation/persist-failure counters are primarily observed today through unit + integration tests; they are still exposed so a future hot-reload of the trust bundle (out of scope for Run 055) can report rejected reloads without a metric-schema change.

**Tests.** Unit tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21 (new module: first-load + upgrade + rollback + equal-same-fp + equal-diff-fp + wrong-env + wrong-chain + malformed JSON + missing field + malformed chain_id hex + malformed fingerprint hex + unsupported record_version + missing-file = None + atomic-write-then-load round trip + creates missing parent dir + two-step upgrade + rollback after two-step + persist-failure when path is a directory + equivocation detail carries both fingerprints + Display messages are operator-actionable + fingerprint_hex shape + chain_id_hex shape). Integration tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12 (first-load signed DevNet + upgrade + rollback + restart-with-identical-bundle no write + equal-sequence different-fingerprint equivocation + wrong-chain-id bundle fails BEFORE sequence update + tampered-signature fails BEFORE sequence update + revoked-root only bundle still loads + corrupt persistence file fails closed no silent reset + stray MainNet record blocks DevNet load fail-closed + null-chain-id bundle persists under runtime chain id + TrustBundleSignature re-export still present). Metrics tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib metrics` 106/106 (was 104/104; +2 from `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_metrics_start_at_zero_and_increment_atomically` and `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`). All Run 050/051/052/053/054 regression suites remain green: `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 70/70 (preserves all earlier assertions); `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `--test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `--test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12. `cargo check -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 055).

**No-fallback proof (Run 055).** The sequence persistence wiring in `main.rs` keys off the LOADED TRUST BUNDLE's `sequence` and canonical `fingerprint`, NOT off `--p2p-trusted-root`. On any error path (`SequenceRollback`, `EqualSequenceFingerprintMismatch`, `PersistFailure`, `WrongEnvironment`, `WrongChainId`, `Malformed`, `UnsupportedRecordVersion`, `Io`, `TestNet/MainNet without --data-dir`) the binary emits a precise FATAL message and calls `std::process::exit(1)` — it does NOT fall back to `--p2p-trusted-root`, does NOT install bundle roots, does NOT install `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead`, and does NOT silently delete or reset the persistence file. The persisted record is written via tmp + `sync_all` + rename; on a mid-write crash the destination file is left intact and the `.tmp` sibling is harmless. The persisted record carries no secret-key material, no validator-signer key bytes, and no signing-key public bytes — only `(record_version, environment, chain_id, highest_sequence, bundle_fingerprint, updated_at_unix_secs)`. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer), **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed.

#### C4 Run 056 evidence update (2026-05-12) — live-binary release-build smoke for Run 055 trust-bundle sequence-number monotonicity persistence; explicit Run-055 boundary NARROWED on DevNet; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 056 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_056.md`) closes the explicit "live release-binary smoke artefact set for the Run 055 anti-rollback path itself" boundary that Run 055 recorded as remaining-open, on the live release `qbind-node` binary `sha256 69013d1eb30e9c9c5e7bbd5083f2fe8103c94118182002cf779f50b967ef4bce` (ELF BuildID `9b27c3be718768bda7dcfa1e23c7446b264e105d`) driven from the live release helper `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` `sha256 e4359904c159aaae61bad9e38a17ba8d43a7fc5de12493702010801c412b4ab9` (ELF BuildID `5e8eb5a99b12ba7efe740d2128af3ba5c818abdd`). Run 056 is **evidence-only** — the only source-tree edit is an additive extension to the existing DevNet helper `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs` adding an optional 4th positional `[sequence_override]` u64 argument that sets the bundle's `sequence` field BEFORE signing (so the signed preimage covers the requested sequence) for the existing `signed-devnet`/`signed-testnet`/`signed-mainnet`/Run-054 leaf-revocation modes; an `eprintln` summary update to report `bundle_sequence=<N>`. No `crates/**/src/**` core library source, no protocol source, no test source, no `Cargo.toml`, and no `main.rs` / `pqc_trust_sequence.rs` was touched; Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, Run 050, Run 051, Run 052, Run 053, Run 054, and Run 055 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit.

**Live-binary smoke evidence (Run 056).** Six release-binary smokes were run with `--env devnet --validator-id 0 --network-mode p2p --enable-p2p --p2p-listen-addr 127.0.0.1:0 --p2p-mutual-auth required --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root --p2p-trust-bundle … --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key … --p2p-leaf-cert … --p2p-leaf-cert-key … --data-dir /tmp/run056/data` and no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback: (1) Positive first-load `sequence=1` smoke on a fresh `--data-dir` — node started, emitted `[binary] Run 055: trust-bundle sequence persistence env=devnet chain_id=51424e4444455600 path=/tmp/run056/data/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json first-load persisted_sequence=1 fp=fddb8e40` and `[binary] Run 050/051: trust bundle loaded … sequence=1 … signature=verified(signing_key_id=722e5f80..) signing_keys_configured=1`; the persistence file `/tmp/run056/data/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` appeared with `{"record_version":1,"environment":"devnet","chain_id":"51424e4444455600","highest_sequence":1,"bundle_fingerprint":"fddb8e40…1494",…}`; `/metrics` reported `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_highest 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_verified_total 1`, all three failure counters at `0`. (2) Positive upgrade `sequence=2` smoke on the same `--data-dir` with a freshly-minted second signed bundle (`fp=951df85c…92a9`) — node started, emitted `… upgraded previous_sequence=1 -> new_sequence=2 fp=951df85c`; the persistence file's `highest_sequence` updated from `1` to `2` and the `bundle_fingerprint` flipped to `951df85c…92a9`; `/metrics` reported `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_highest 2`. (3) Negative rollback smoke (reload the original `sequence=1` bundle on the same `--data-dir`) — `exit_code=1` BEFORE any bundle root was merged, FATAL `pqc trust-bundle sequence rollback rejected: attempted_sequence=1 is lower than persisted highest_sequence=2 (fail closed; this node has already accepted a newer signed bundle for the same trust domain). No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade or silently reset persistence state).`; the persistence file was byte-for-byte unchanged. (4) Positive equal-sequence same-fingerprint smoke (reload the `sequence=2` bundle) — node started, emitted `… equal-sequence same-fingerprint (no write) sequence=2 fp=951df85c`; the persistence file's `updated_at_unix_secs` was byte-for-byte unchanged (no rewrite), proving the no-op-restart steady-state semantics; `/metrics` reported `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_highest 2`, all failure counters at `0`. (5) **Strongest negative — equal-sequence different-fingerprint equivocation smoke** (load a *second* validly-signed DevNet bundle at `sequence=2`, different ephemeral root + signing key + `generated_at`, distinct canonical fingerprint `9a699845…f441`) — `exit_code=1` BEFORE any bundle root was merged, FATAL `pqc trust-bundle equal-sequence equivocation rejected: sequence=2 persisted_fingerprint=951df85c…92a9 attempted_fingerprint=9a699845…f441 (fail closed; two distinct bundles cannot share the same sequence). No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure …`; the FATAL names BOTH the persisted and the attempted fingerprints (operator forensics, as Run 055 unit `equivocation_detail_carries_both_fingerprints` pins); the persistence file was byte-for-byte unchanged. (6) Negative corrupted-persistence-file smoke (overwrite the JSON record with 35 bytes of garbage `this is not valid json {{{\x00\xff broken` and restart) — `exit_code=1`, FATAL `pqc trust-bundle sequence malformed: expected ident at line 1 column 2. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure …`; the corrupted file's byte contents were verified IDENTICAL after exit (Run 055's "never silently delete, truncate, or reset a corrupted file" guarantee honoured by the live binary). On every positive smoke, `dummy_kem_registered = false`, `dummy_aead_registered = false`, `pqc_root_mode = pqc-static-root`, `sig_suite_id = 100` (ML-DSA-44), `transport_kem_suite_id = 100` (ML-KEM-768), `transport_aead_suite_id = 101` (ChaCha20-Poly1305) — proving no fallback to test-grade primitives. The three negative smokes exit BEFORE the `[Run040] P2pNodeBuilder` line is reached, so no `Dummy*` primitive can be installed even hypothetically; `/metrics` is not reachable on those paths (fail-closed startup before the metrics HTTP server is bound) and the counter movement remains pinned by Run 055's 21 unit + 12 integration tests, documented honestly rather than fabricated.

**Tests.** All required regression suites rerun on the release profile and remain green: `cargo test --release -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21; `--lib pqc_trust_bundle` 70/70; `--lib metrics` 106/106; `--lib p2p` 138/138; full `--lib` 882/882; `--test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `--test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `--test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12; `--test run_040_pqc_static_root_real_aead_tests` 14/14; `--test run_044_pqc_cert_verify_metrics_adapter_tests` 10/10; `cargo test --release -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `--lib` 17/17; `cargo test --release -p qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; `cargo check --release -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 056). `binary_consensus`, `forged_injection`, `run030`, and `qbind-consensus --lib timeout` were intentionally not rerun because Run 056 did not modify any source on those paths (only a DevNet example helper was extended). The pre-existing `m16_epoch_transition_hardening_tests` `cargo build --tests` failure (`set_inject_write_failure` / `clear_epoch_transition_marker` methods missing on `RocksDbConsensusStorage`) is unrelated to Run 056 and was present on `d5a6056` before Run 056's edits.

**No-fallback proof (Run 056).** No `--p2p-trusted-root` was supplied on any Run 056 smoke. The Run 055 wiring in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` keys the sequence check off the LOADED TRUST BUNDLE's `sequence` and canonical `fingerprint`, NOT off `--p2p-trusted-root` (Run 055 invariant, preserved by Run 056 — no `main.rs` edits). On all three negative paths (rollback, equivocation, corrupt persistence) the FATAL line explicitly ends with `No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade or silently reset persistence state).` and `exit_code = 1`; the three negative smokes exit BEFORE the `[Run040] P2pNodeBuilder` line, so the live PQC trust set was never populated from any source on those paths. The Run 056 helper still mints all root and signing keys ephemerally in memory and never writes `root_sk` or `signing_sk` to disk; no private-key bytes appear in any Run-056 log artefact. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer), and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 056).** Activation epoch / height gating for revocation entries and root-status windows (only `effective_from` UNIX seconds is honoured). Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook (the helper still mints ephemeral DevNet bundle-signing keys in process; production signing remains an out-of-process KMS task). Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore. Live MainNet signed-bundle release-binary smoke with a production-grade signing key (Run 056 ran DevNet only; MainNet signed-bundle startup is proven by unit + integration tests and the same `validate_at_with_signing_keys` + `check_and_update_sequence` codepaths that power DevNet, but a real-binary MainNet smoke was deliberately not performed). A startup self-check in `qbind-node/src/main.rs` that fails the binary closed when `--p2p-leaf-cert` matches an active entry in the loaded bundle's `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` (Run 052 / Run 054 boundary; still open). An optional "wrong-domain persistence" smoke that manually alters the persisted record's `environment` or `chain_id` and restarts (already pinned by two Run 055 unit tests and one Run 055 integration test; Run 056 task explicitly permitted skipping it given that coverage). **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 056; Run 056 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle sequence-persistence evidence surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**

#### C4 Run 057 evidence update (2026-05-13) — PQC trust-bundle activation epoch/height gating NARROWED on DevNet (height path closed; epoch path explicitly deferred); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 057 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_057.md`) closes the narrow trust-bundle `activation_height` gating item left open by Runs 050–056 ("Activation epoch / height gating remains OPEN. `roots[i].activation_epoch` and `roots[i].activation_height` are accepted by the schema but the runtime does NOT yet gate a root's acceptance on a consensus epoch or height; only wall-clock `not_before`/`not_after` is enforced today.") on the **height path** end-to-end on the DevNet binary surface, and records the **epoch path** as explicitly deferred behind a documented "no safe pre-consensus epoch source today" boundary. The bundle layer's signature and canonical fingerprint already cover both `activation_epoch` and `activation_height` (proved by the Run 057 tests `tampering_activation_height_after_signing_invalidates_signature` and `canonical_fingerprint_covers_activation_height`); when a real runtime epoch source lands, no schema or signing change will be needed.

**What changed (Run 057).** New module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_activation.rs` introduces `ActivationContext { current_height, current_epoch }`, `TrustBundleActivationError`, and `check_bundle_activation(...)` — an inclusive `current >= required` gate evaluated independently on bundle-level and per-root activation fields. `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs` adds optional bundle-level `activation_epoch` / `activation_height` fields (`#[serde(default)]`, covered by `canonical_signing_bytes` and `canonical_fingerprint`), adds `TrustBundleError::Activation(_)`, and adds the activation-aware loader `load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation(...)` which runs the activation check AFTER signature/env/chain_id/window/revocation validation. `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` wires the activation context (`current_height = restore_baseline.snapshot_height` when `--restore-from-snapshot` was supplied, else `0`; `current_epoch = None`) and calls the activation-aware loader, so the gate runs **BEFORE** the Run 055 sequence-persistence step and **BEFORE** the Run 050 root-merge step — i.e. a future-activation bundle does NOT advance the persisted highest sequence and does NOT inject roots into the live trust set. Five new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_*` metrics are surfaced through `P2pMetrics::format_metrics` (`_height_required`, `_height_current`, `_epoch_required`, `_epoch_current`, `_rejected_total`); each new family renders exactly once per `/metrics` body (asserted by `pqc_trust_bundle_activation_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`). The DevNet helper `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs` gains an optional 5th positional `[activation_height_override]` u64 argument (additive; identical pattern to the Run 056 sequence_override knob); no other helper edits.

**Tests.** Run 057 unit tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_activation` 14/14 (missing-fields-accepted with-and-without runtime source; bundle-level height satisfied / inclusive-equal / future / runtime-source-unavailable; bundle-level epoch future-when-source-present / runtime-source-unavailable; both-gates satisfied / one-future; root-level future-rejected; root-level activation field is advisory-only on non-Active status; required_height is `max` across bundle + Active roots; Display message ends in fail-closed phrase). Run 057 integration tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_057_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_tests` 12/12 — including the central invariant `future_activation_does_not_advance_sequence_persistence` (signed DevNet bundle at `sequence=5` with `activation_height=1_000` at `current_height=0` is rejected with `TrustBundleError::Activation(ActivationHeightNotYetReached{..})`, no persistence record is written, and a subsequent satisfied bundle at the same `sequence=5` then advances the record cleanly — proving the future-activation rejection path does NOT burn a higher sequence) and the cross-coverage proofs `future_activation_bundle_is_structurally_valid_and_signed` (same bundle passes the non-activation loader, so the gate is its own boundary), `tampering_activation_height_after_signing_invalidates_signature` (`activation_height` is in the canonical signing preimage), `canonical_fingerprint_covers_activation_height` (Run 055's equivocation guard cannot be bypassed by re-publishing "same sequence, different activation_height"), `per_root_activation_height_future_refuses_bundle`, and `legacy_bundle_json_without_activation_fields_parses_clean` (hand-crafted JSON missing the new fields parses via `serde(default)` so existing bundles still load). Metrics tests `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib metrics` 108/108 (was 106; +2 from `pqc_trust_bundle_activation_metrics_start_at_zero_and_increment_atomically` and `pqc_trust_bundle_activation_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`). All required prior suites green on the same workspace: `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 72/72; `--lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21; full `--lib` 898/898; `--test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12; `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `--test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `--test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-net --lib` 17/17; `--test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `cargo check -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 057); `cargo build -p qbind-node --example devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` clean.

**No-fallback proof (Run 057).** On the activation-rejection path the binary surface in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` returns `Err(TrustBundleError::Activation(_))` from `TrustBundle::load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` **BEFORE** the trust-bundle's roots are merged into `trusted_roots` and **BEFORE** `check_and_update_sequence` is invoked (pinned end-to-end by the integration test `future_activation_does_not_advance_sequence_persistence`), increments `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_rejected_total` by exactly one, surfaces the runtime height on the `_height_current` gauge for forensic completeness, emits FATAL `... No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade). See docs/whitepaper/contradiction.md C4 (signed root distribution).` and exits `std::process::exit(1)`. The activation error's own `Display` impl additionally ends with `No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root.` (asserted by `display_error_messages_carry_fail_closed_phrase`). The binary exits before `P2pNodeBuilder` is constructed, exactly as in Run 055/056, so no `Dummy*` primitive can be installed even hypothetically. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer), and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 057, with Run 058 update inline below).** (a) **Epoch gating runtime source.** Bundles that declare `activation_epoch` are rejected at load with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable` today, because no safe pre-consensus epoch source exists in this binary — epoch transitions only happen AFTER consensus begins committing blocks, and the trust bundle is required BEFORE consensus can establish peer transport. Epoch gating is therefore deferred behind a future change that plumbs a persisted "last committed epoch" into the pre-consensus startup context, exactly as Run 057 plumbs `restore_baseline.snapshot_height` for height gating. The bundle layer's signature and fingerprint ALREADY cover `activation_epoch`, so no schema or signing change will be needed when that future change lands. (b) **Live release-binary smoke artefact set for the Run 057 activation gate.** Run 057 ships unit + integration tests covering the exact codepaths the release binary runs, but does NOT include the matched Run-056-style release-binary smoke artefacts (positive `activation_height` satisfied + negative `activation_height` future + identity). Recorded explicitly as remaining-open. (c) **Activation gate on revocation entries.** `TrustBundleRevocation` carries `effective_from` (UNIX seconds) and is honoured at the validity-window layer; an equivalent activation-height / activation-epoch field on revocation entries is NOT introduced by Run 057 — only bundle-level + root-level gating. (d) **Per-environment minimum-activation-height policy** (e.g. "MainNet bundles MUST declare `activation_height >= last_finalized_height + N`") is not introduced and remains an open production-operability item under C4. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 057; Run 057 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle activation surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 055).** Activation epoch / height gating for revocation entries and root-status windows (still only `effective_from` UNIX seconds is honored). Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook. Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore. Live MainNet signed-bundle release-binary smoke with a production-grade signing key. Live release-binary smoke artefact set for the Run-055 anti-rollback path (the unit + integration test coverage is complete; the release-binary smoke artefact set was deliberately not produced in this session to keep the scope minimal and is explicitly recorded as a future evidence run). A startup self-check that fails the binary closed when `--p2p-leaf-cert` matches an active entry in the loaded bundle's `revoked_leaf_fingerprints`. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 055; Run 055 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle persistence layer. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**
