On the positive smoke, `dummy_kem_registered = false`, `dummy_aead_registered = false`, `pqc_root_mode = pqc-static-root`, `sig_suite_id = 100` (ML-DSA-44), `transport_kem_suite_id = 100` (ML-KEM-768), `transport_aead_suite_id = 101` (ChaCha20-Poly1305) — proving no fallback to test-grade primitives. All four negative smokes exit BEFORE the `[Run040] P2pNodeBuilder` line is reached, so no `Dummy*` primitive can be installed even hypothetically; `/metrics` is not reachable on those paths (fail-closed startup before the metrics HTTP server is bound) and the counter movement remains pinned by Run 050/051/055/057 unit tests, documented honestly rather than fabricated.

**Tests.** All required regression suites rerun on the release profile and remain green: `cargo test --release -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 72/72; `--lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21; `--lib pqc_trust_activation` 14/14; `--lib metrics` 108/108; `--lib p2p` 138/138; full `--lib` 898/898; `--test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `--test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `--test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `--test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `--test run_057_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_tests` 12/12; `--test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12; `--test run_040_pqc_static_root_real_aead_tests` 14/14; `--test run_044_pqc_cert_verify_metrics_adapter_tests` 10/10; `cargo test --release -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `--lib` 17/17; `cargo test --release -p qbind-crypto --lib` 68/68; `cargo check --release -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 059). The pre-existing `m16_epoch_transition_hardening_tests` `cargo build --tests` failure (`set_inject_write_failure` / `clear_epoch_transition_marker` methods missing on `RocksDbConsensusStorage`) is unrelated to Run 059 and was present on `cc2f33e` before Run 059's edits.

**No-fallback proof (Run 059).** No `--p2p-trusted-root` was supplied on any Run 059 smoke. The Run 050/051/053/055/057 wiring in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` runs the environment + chain_id + activation + signature + sequence-persistence checks inside `TrustBundle::load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` and (for sequence) `check_and_update_sequence`, returning `Err(TrustBundleError::*)` BEFORE the bundle's roots are merged into `trusted_roots` (Run 050 invariant, preserved by Run 059 — no `main.rs` edits). On all four negative paths (unsigned, tampered, wrong-signing-key, wrong-chain_id) the FATAL line explicitly ends with `No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle failure (production-honest lifecycle must not silently downgrade). See docs/whitepaper/contradiction.md C4 (signed root distribution).` and `exit_code = 1`. All four negative smokes exit BEFORE the `[Run040] P2pNodeBuilder` line, so the live PQC trust set was never populated from any source on those paths. The Run 059 helper still mints all root and signing keys ephemerally in memory and never writes `root_sk` or `signing_sk` to disk; no private-key bytes appear in any Run-059 log artefact. **No fabricated metrics**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer), and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 059).** (a) **MainNet two-node release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Run 059's single-validator MainNet smoke DOES start consensus and DOES commit blocks past height 1 on the live binary, exercising the full MainNet trust-bundle load path end-to-end; a two-node MainNet peer-connection artefact set was deliberately not produced because it is blocked by **unrelated production config** (validator keystore loading — `config.signer_keystore_path` is not read on startup, per the binary's own `[binary] Run 032` / `Run 033` disclosures emitted on Smoke 1 — plus per-peer consensus-key distribution and production-grade KEM/AEAD primitives on the binary path, per the binary's own `[binary] Run 037` disclosure that "KEM/AEAD primitives on the binary path are still test-grade and remain a separate C4 piece (not C4(c)); MainNet readiness is therefore not yet implied"). The trust-bundle verification path itself is exhaustively pinned for MainNet by the five Run 059 smokes plus the 898-lib + integration regression suite plus the two-node DevNet smokes from Run 054. Recorded explicitly as remaining-open. (b) **Production-grade signing-key custody.** Run 059's MainNet signing key is an ephemeral ML-DSA-44 keypair minted in memory by the DevNet helper for this run only. A production-grade HSM/KMS signing-key custody / rotation flow remains out of scope under (c) below. (c) **Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook** unchanged from Run 056/057/058. (d) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore** unchanged. (e) **Epoch gating runtime source** unchanged from the Run 057/058 boundary — bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`. (f) **Activation gate on revocation entries** unchanged. (g) **Per-environment minimum-activation-height policy** (e.g. "MainNet bundles MUST declare `activation_height >= last_finalized_height + N`") is not introduced and remains an open production-operability item under C4. (h) **`--restore-from-snapshot` satisfied-height live release-binary smoke** unchanged from the Run 058 boundary. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 059; Run 059 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle MainNet startup-evidence surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 058).** (a) **`--restore-from-snapshot` satisfied-height live release-binary smoke.** Run 058 did NOT produce a live-binary smoke that drives `current_height > 0` via `--restore-from-snapshot`. Producing it on the release binary requires a pre-existing valid VM-v0 RocksDB state-store + matching `StateSnapshotMeta` snapshot artefact set (helper `crates/qbind-ledger/examples/qbind_state_snapshot.rs` requires a populated `RocksDbAccountState` — itself the output of an earlier consensus-running release-binary run), which is a separate cross-domain operational artefact outside the Run 058 activation-height evidence scope. The activation-height restore path itself is already pinned end-to-end by Run 057 unit + integration tests (`bundle_activation_height_satisfied_accepted`, `bundle_activation_height_equal_accepted_inclusive`, `activation_height_satisfied_accepts_bundle`, `activation_height_inclusive_equal_accepts`, and the central invariant `future_activation_does_not_advance_sequence_persistence` — exactly the Smoke 5 → Smoke 6 transition observed live on the binary). No fake snapshot was created or used. Recorded explicitly as remaining-open. (b) **Epoch declaration live release-binary negative smoke.** The Run 057 helper does not currently expose an `[activation_epoch_override]` argument (only the height override). Underlying fail-closed code path is pinned by Run 057 unit (`bundle_activation_epoch_requires_runtime_source_today`, `bundle_activation_epoch_future_rejected_when_epoch_source_present`) and integration (`activation_epoch_present_without_current_epoch_refuses`); since the binary wires `current_epoch = None` unconditionally, the `CurrentEpochUnavailable` fail-closed path is what a real-binary smoke would observe and it is already pinned by those tests. Recorded explicitly as remaining-open. (c) **Epoch gating runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057 boundary — bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`. Epoch gating is deferred behind a future change that plumbs a persisted "last committed epoch" into the pre-consensus startup context, exactly as Run 057 plumbs `restore_baseline.snapshot_height` for height gating; bundle signature and fingerprint already cover `activation_epoch`. (d) **Activation gate on revocation entries.** Unchanged from the Run 057 boundary — `TrustBundleRevocation` still carries only `effective_from` (UNIX seconds) at the validity-window layer; an equivalent activation-height / activation-epoch field on revocation entries is NOT introduced by Run 058. (e) **Per-environment minimum-activation-height policy** (e.g. "MainNet bundles MUST declare `activation_height >= last_finalized_height + N`") is not introduced and remains an open production-operability item under C4. (f) **Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook** unchanged from Run 056/Run 057. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore** unchanged. (h) **Live MainNet signed-bundle release-binary smoke with a production-grade signing key**: Run 058 ran DevNet only; activation-gate semantics are environment-independent at the bundle envelope layer (the same `check_bundle_activation` executes on every environment), but a real-binary MainNet smoke was deliberately not performed. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 058; Run 058 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle activation-height evidence surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**
#### C4 Run 060 evidence update (2026-05-13) — operator-facing PQC trust lifecycle playbook + DevNet rehearsal scripts NARROWED; full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 060 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_060.md`) lands the smallest production-honest operator playbook for the PQC trust-anchor and bundle-signing lifecycle proven by Runs 050–059 (Run 056 item "Operator-facing CA + certificate rotation + signing-key rotation playbook", carried forward unchanged by Runs 057/058/059). Run 060 is **evidence- and documentation-only** — no `crates/**/src/**` core library source, no protocol source, no test source, no `Cargo.toml`, no `main.rs`, no `pqc_trust_bundle.rs` / `pqc_trust_sequence.rs` / `pqc_trust_activation.rs` / `pqc_root_config.rs` / `cli.rs` / `metrics.rs` / `p2p_node_builder.rs`, and no helper source was touched; Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, Run 050, Run 051, Run 052, Run 053, Run 054, Run 055, Run 056, Run 057, Run 058, and Run 059 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit.

**What changed (Run 060).** Three documents and two DevNet-only rehearsal scripts: (1) NEW `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` — 12-section operator playbook covering scope & non-goals, trust model + role separation (transport-root / bundle-signing / validator / publisher / incident-responder / auditor), artifact inventory (12 artifact classes: transport root pk/sk, bundle-signing pk/sk, validator leaf cert + KEM secret, trust-bundle JSON, sequence-persistence file, revocation entries, activation height/epoch fields, chain_id, environment), key generation & custody, per-environment policy (DevNet / TestNet / MainNet), §6.A normal transport-root rotation workflow (mint R_new offline → issue new leaf certs → overlap bundle sequence=N+1 with both roots active and `activation_height = current_finalised_height + margin` → roll validators to new leaves → retire bundle sequence=N+2 with R_old retired → optional revoke bundle sequence=N+3 for compromise rotations), §6.B emergency root revocation workflow (mint revocation bundle sequence=N+1 with `roots=[R_bad(revoked), R_new(active)]` and `revocations[]` entry, `activation_height = current_finalised_height` no margin, honest liveness-vs-revocation tradeoff documented), §6.C leaf rotation workflow (scheduled and emergency variants, the emergency variant adds `revoked_leaf_fingerprints[]` per Run 052/054), §6.D bundle-signing-key rotation workflow (out-of-band CLI overlap procedure since the binary does not ratify a new signing key on-chain — operator distributes BSK_new alongside BSK_old, mints bundle N+1 under BSK_new, removes BSK_old line after rollout), §7 promotion checklist (17 items per bundle change), §8 incident checklist (8 items per compromise event), §9 evidence checklist (12 artifacts per production bundle change), §10 residual risks (9 items NOT solved by the runbook, all carried-forward from existing C4 boundaries), §11 mapping to Runs 050–059, §12 operator-facing flag glossary; (2) NEW `scripts/devnet/trust_bundle_rotation_demo.sh` — DevNet-only rehearsal of §6.A that drives the existing `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` example with documented arguments to mint three signed DevNet bundles at sequences 1, 2, 3, fails fast (`set -euo pipefail` + a `find … -name 'root.sk.*' -o -name 'signing-key.sk.*' -o -name 'bundle-signing.sk.*'` self-check) if any private-key file is unexpectedly persisted, emits a summary.txt with canonical artifact paths; (3) NEW `scripts/devnet/trust_bundle_revocation_demo.sh` — DevNet-only rehearsal of §6.C variant 2 (leaf revocation) using helper modes `signed-devnet`, `signed-devnet-revoked-v0`, `signed-devnet-revoked-v1` at sequences 1, 2, 3 with the same private-key self-check; (4) NEW `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_060.md` — this evidence document; (5) this row.

**Anchoring (Run 060).** Every fail-closed invariant cited by the runbook §1.3 is anchored in the implementation file and the prior evidence run that proved it on the live release binary: signature verification + signing-key/root-id trust separation + environment + chain_id + validity windows + root status + revocations are pinned by `pqc_trust_bundle::TrustBundle::validate_at_with_signing_keys_and_chain_id` (Runs 050/051/053; live-binary evidence Runs 056/059); monotonic sequence ordering + equal-sequence equivocation rejection + corrupt-file fail-closed (never silently truncates) are pinned by `pqc_trust_sequence::check_and_update_sequence` (Run 055; live-binary evidence Run 056 Smokes 3/5/6); inclusive `current >= required` activation semantics + `CurrentEpochUnavailable` fail-closed + the central `future_activation_does_not_advance_sequence_persistence` invariant are pinned by `pqc_trust_activation::check_bundle_activation` (Run 057; live-binary evidence Run 058 Smokes 2/3/4); the no-`Dummy*` invariant under `--p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` is pinned by `p2p_node_builder::make_pqc_static_root_crypto_provider` (Runs 037/039/040/041); per-environment chain ids are pinned by `crates/qbind-types/src/primitives.rs` (`QBIND_DEVNET_CHAIN_ID = 0x51424E4444455600`, `QBIND_TESTNET_CHAIN_ID = 0x51424E4454535400`, `QBIND_MAINNET_CHAIN_ID = 0x51424E444D41494E`); the MainNet signed-bundle unsigned/tampered/wrong-key/wrong-chain fail-closed paths are pinned by Run 059 Smokes 2/3/4/5.

The two DevNet rehearsal scripts pass `bash -n` syntax validation and are marked executable; end-to-end execution requires `cargo run --example devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper`, which is the supported DevNet helper invocation.

**No-fallback proof (Run 060).** Run 060 introduces no code path. It documents the existing fail-closed paths. The runbook §1.3 invariants table forbids any operator procedure that would attempt to bypass any fail-closed boundary; §10 enumerates the residual risks Run 060 does NOT close. The DevNet rehearsal scripts never call `qbind-node` with `--p2p-trusted-root` on TestNet/MainNet (they target DevNet only), never reach for any `Dummy*` primitive (they do not invoke the binary at all; they only mint bundle artifacts via the documented helper), never edit a persistence file, and self-check that NO private-key file appears under their output directory (failing non-zero if one does — using a `find` filter for `root.sk.*` / `signing-key.sk.*` / `bundle-signing.sk.*` patterns). **Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 060).** (a) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059 boundary — bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`. The runbook §5.2 / §5.3 / §7 forbid operators from setting this field on production bundles, but the binary-side runtime source remains an open production-operability item. (b) **Validator self-check on local leaf in `revoked_leaf_fingerprints`.** Unchanged from the Run 052/054/056/057/058 boundary — the binary does NOT fail closed at startup if the operator's own `--p2p-leaf-cert` matches an active entry in the loaded bundle's `revoked_leaf_fingerprints`. The runbook §6.C variant 2 requires operators to verify out-of-band; the binary-side self-check remains open. (c) **Per-environment minimum activation-height policy.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059 boundary — the binary does NOT enforce a minimum margin between `activation_height` and the current finalised height. The runbook §5.3 RECOMMENDS at least one finality block (suggested ≥ 100 on MainNet) but enforcement is operator policy, not binary policy. (d) **In-binary bundle-signing-key ratification.** There is no on-chain ratification of a new bundle-signing key. The runbook §6.D is an out-of-band CLI overlap procedure; if a future runtime adds on-chain ratification, both this row and the runbook MUST be updated. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Run 060 treats the signing-key custody surface in §3.2 / §3.4 as a runbook boundary; operators MAY back it with HSM in production but full KMS integration is not in scope. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke** unchanged from the Run 059 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore** unchanged. (h) **DevNet rehearsal scripts are evidence rehearsal, not production tooling.** A production CA / KMS-backed rotation pipeline is out of scope. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 060; Run 060 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the operator-documentation surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN.**

#### C4 Run 061 evidence update (2026-05-13) — local revoked-leaf startup self-check CLOSES Run 060 §10 item (b); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 061 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_061.md`) implements, exercises on the live release binary, and proves the smallest production-honest startup self-check that closes exactly one Run 060 §10 remaining boundary: **§10 item (b) "Validator self-check on local leaf in `revoked_leaf_fingerprints`"**. After Run 061, an operator who starts `qbind-node` under `--p2p-mutual-auth required --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root` with a `--p2p-leaf-cert` whose canonical Run 052 leaf fingerprint appears in the loaded trust bundle's currently-active `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` set sees the binary fail closed at startup (exit 1) BEFORE any P2P state is constructed, BEFORE `pqc_config` is built, BEFORE `P2pNodeBuilder::with_pqc_leaf_revocations(...)` is called, BEFORE `builder.build(...)` constructs any live listener / dialer / peer manager, and BEFORE any peer-handshake metric could move. The check runs strictly AFTER the full Run 050/051/053/055/057 trust-bundle validation pipeline accepts the bundle, so existing fail-closed boundaries are preserved bit-for-bit. The startup-time fingerprint is byte-identical to the Run 052 peer-handshake fingerprint (proven by cross-crate unit + integration tests plus live-binary log-prefix byte-match against the helper's `v0.leaf-fp.hex` artifact). No new metric family is introduced (the node exits before `/metrics` binds; a startup-time counter would be unscrapeable and misleading); the Run 052 peer-handshake metric family `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total` is preserved bit-for-bit. No private-key material crosses the helper boundary (helper signature accepts only public cert bytes, the public revocation set, and the public bundle fingerprint — pinned by two dedicated tests). No fallback to `--p2p-trusted-root`, `DummySig`, `DummyKem`, or `DummyAead` is introduced or strengthened. Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, Run 050, Run 051, Run 052, Run 053, Run 054, Run 055, Run 056, Run 057, Run 058, Run 059, and Run 060 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit (regression suites all green; see "Tests").

**What changed (Run 061).** Three source surfaces + one evidence document + this row: (1) `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs` — adds `pub enum LocalLeafSelfCheckError { DecodeFailed, Revoked { leaf_fingerprint_prefix, bundle_fingerprint_prefix } }` (Display emits only 8-hex prefixes — never the full fingerprint, never private material) and `pub fn check_local_leaf_not_revoked(local_leaf_cert_bytes, revoked_leaf_fingerprints, bundle_fingerprint) -> Result<[u8;32], LocalLeafSelfCheckError>` (decodes via `NetworkDelegationCert::decode`, hashes via the existing Run 052 `cert_leaf_fingerprint`, checks the active revocation set; pure function); (2) `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` — wires the helper into startup between the Run 050/051 trust-bundle observability gauge surfacing and the `let pqc_config = PqcStaticRootConfig {...}` construction; on rejection emits exactly one FATAL line `[binary] FATAL: Run 061 local leaf certificate revoked: the local --p2p-leaf-cert fingerprint (<8hex>..) appears in the active revoked_leaf_fingerprints set of the loaded trust bundle (bundle fp <8hex>..). Refusing to start P2P. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle-revoked local leaf.` and exits via `std::process::exit(1)`; on acceptance emits one info line `[binary] Run 061: local-leaf startup self-check passed (local_leaf_fp=<8hex>.. bundle_fp=<8hex>.. active_revoked_leaf_fingerprints=<N>)`; the check is a strict no-op when the loaded bundle has no revoked leaf fingerprints OR no bundle is configured OR no `--p2p-leaf-cert` is configured (preserving pre-Run-061 behaviour bit-for-bit); (3) `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_061_pqc_local_leaf_self_check_tests.rs` — NEW integration-test file with 9 tests covering the positive non-revoked path, the negative revoked-local-leaf fail-closed path, the unknown-revoked-fingerprint positive path, Run 052 fingerprint cross-crate parity, the leaf-vs-root axis orthogonality, the empty-set short-circuit, the malformed-cert decode-failure defence-in-depth path, the "startup self-check does NOT touch the Run 052 peer-handshake metric family" invariant, and the "no private-key material crosses the helper boundary" API contract; (4) NEW `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_061.md` — the evidence document; (5) this row.

**Anchoring (Run 061).** The local-leaf startup self-check is anchored in the implementation as: helper `pqc_trust_bundle::check_local_leaf_not_revoked` (lines added between the existing `cert_leaf_fingerprint_hex` and the hex-parsing helpers, immediately after Run 052's `cert_leaf_fingerprint`), wired into `main.rs` between Run 050/051 observability surfacing and `PqcStaticRootConfig` construction. Fingerprint semantics are byte-identical to qbind-net's `leaf_cert_fingerprint` (proven by `run_061_self_check_fingerprint_equals_run_052_handshake_fingerprint` lib-test and `run_061_self_check_fingerprint_matches_run_052_peer_handshake_fingerprint` integration test; the cross-crate domain-separator equality `TRUST_BUNDLE_LEAF_FINGERPRINT_DOMAIN_SEPARATOR == LEAF_CERT_FINGERPRINT_DOMAIN_SEPARATOR` was already pinned by Run 052 and is reused here). On the live release binary Smoke 2 reports `leaf_fp=6015416d..` which byte-matches the helper's `v0.leaf-fp.hex` artifact `6015416dda89fdfcc91824ba0695d69eee62dad68360024065d8a0447c46606d` — a third anchor proving the startup-time fingerprint computation is the same one Run 052 publishes. Ordering ("after bundle validation, before P2P start") is anchored by the source-file placement plus the live-binary Smoke 2 stderr (the FATAL line appears AFTER Run 050/051/055/057 log lines and BEFORE any `[binary] Run 052: revoked_leaf_fingerprints=` line, any `Failed to build P2P node` line, and any `newly_connected_peers` line — proving the builder is not entered). The "no peer-handshake metric movement" invariant is pinned by the dedicated integration test `run_061_self_check_does_not_touch_peer_handshake_metric_family` plus by the live-binary metric scrape on Smoke 1 (`qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total 0` after a clean restart). The "no private-key dependency" invariant is pinned by the helper's signature shape (which references only `&[u8]`, `&HashSet<[u8;32]>`, `&[u8;32]`) plus by two dedicated tests (`run_061_self_check_does_not_require_private_key_material`, `run_061_helper_signature_pins_no_private_key_dependency`).

**Tests.** All required regression suites pass on the Run 061 working tree: `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust` 115/115 (= 80 `pqc_trust_bundle` [+8 new Run 061 unit tests vs the Run 060 baseline of 72] + 21 `pqc_trust_sequence` + 14 `pqc_trust_activation`); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_061_pqc_local_leaf_self_check_tests` 9/9 (NEW); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_057_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_040_pqc_static_root_real_aead_tests` 14/14; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_044_pqc_cert_verify_metrics_adapter_tests` 10/10; `cargo test -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib metrics` 108/108; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib p2p` 138/138; full `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib` 906/906. `cargo check -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings unrelated to Run 061). Three release-binary live smokes recorded in the evidence doc: Smoke 1 positive non-revoked (exit 124 = timeout-after-clean-startup, no Run 061 line emitted because the bundle's revocation set is empty so the helper short-circuits — pre-Run-061 behaviour preserved bit-for-bit, with `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total = 0`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_loaded = 1`, `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_signature_verified_total = 1`); Smoke 2 negative revoked-local leaf (exit 1, exactly one FATAL line emitted with `leaf_fp=6015416d.. bundle_fp=b34d4c16..` — both prefixes byte-match the helper-emitted artifacts; zero `[binary] Run 052: revoked_leaf_fingerprints=` log lines, zero `Failed to build P2P node` log lines, zero `newly_connected_peers` log lines, zero `Dummy*` registration lines — proving the builder is not entered and no peer-handshake counter could move); Smoke 3 positive unknown-revoked-fingerprint (exit 124, exactly one `[binary] Run 061: local-leaf startup self-check passed (local_leaf_fp=b75600e7.. bundle_fp=85786421.. active_revoked_leaf_fingerprints=1)` line; the local v0 leaf fingerprint prefix `b75600e7` byte-matches the helper's `v0.leaf-fp.hex` artifact `b75600e7c880b06c42f5c363518f147f4ff9c9d49031a6a9ddcac941d3652bfa`). Binary identity recorded in the evidence doc: `qbind-node` sha256 `f851ef91…`, build-id `2749978a…`; `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` sha256 `d2796da0…`; `devnet_pqc_root_helper` sha256 `11a6ff45…`.

**No-fallback proof (Run 061).** Source diff is +1425 lines / -0 lines across 4 files; no existing test was modified or removed; no `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced; no classical signature surface was introduced (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only); no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority; no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change; the helper signature accepts only public bytes and cannot read `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes; the FATAL log line carries only 8-hex public prefixes and the static marker phrase plus the explicit non-fallback claim "Refusing to start P2P. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle-revoked local leaf"; on the live release binary Smoke 2 stderr contains zero `Dummy*` registration lines and zero non-FATAL "fallback" occurrences; the Run 055 sequence persistence file is written by the Run 050/051/055/057 pipeline BEFORE Run 061 runs and is not reset on rejection (mirroring Run 055's "no silent reset" discipline); no `/metrics` scrape was fabricated to claim a behaviour the binary does not produce. **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of the helper API surface to accept private-key material**, and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 061).** (a) **Root-level local revocation self-check.** Unchanged. A bundle that root-revokes the issuing root of the local leaf cert but does NOT list the leaf fingerprint on `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` does not by itself trigger a startup-time fail-closed; the Run 050 root-revocation axis remains enforced at cert verify time under `--p2p-mutual-auth required`. Adding a startup-time root-revocation self-check is a separate narrower follow-up. (b) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060 boundary. (c) **Per-environment minimum activation-height policy.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060 boundary. (d) **In-binary bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060 boundary; out-of-band CLI overlap (Run 060 §6.D) remains the supported rotation path. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke** unchanged from the Run 059/060 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore** unchanged. (h) **Operator playbook prose update.** Run 060's `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` §6.C variant 2 still reads "operators must verify out-of-band"; with Run 061 the binary now refuses to start with a bundle-revoked local leaf, so the operator-side verification step is now a defence-in-depth recommendation rather than the only guard. The runbook is intentionally NOT updated in Run 061 (Run 061 is source-and-evidence, not operator-doc); a future evidence/documentation-only run may align the runbook prose. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 061; Run 061 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle startup self-check surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 061 closes only Run 060 §10 item (b); all other Run 060 §10 remaining items persist unchanged.

#### C4 Run 062 evidence update (2026-05-13) — per-entry revocation activation gates on the PQC trust-bundle (NARROW C4 sub-piece); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 062 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_062.md`) implements, exercises on the live release binary, and proves the smallest production-honest activation-gate surface for **per-entry** PQC trust-bundle revocations. Before Run 062, every entry on `TrustBundleRevocation` (root-scope or leaf-scope) became fully active the moment the bundle parsed (subject only to wall-clock `effective_from`); operators had no way to publish a *scheduled* revocation that takes effect at a known future block height. Run 062 introduces an optional, ML-DSA-44-signature-covered, canonical-fingerprint-covered `activation_height: Option<u64>` field on each revocation entry. Resolution rule (mirroring the Run 057 bundle-level activation gate): an entry is **ACTIVE** iff `effective_from <= validation_time` AND (`activation_height` is `None` OR `current_height >= activation_height`); otherwise, when the entry is signature-valid but its height gate is unsatisfied (or no runtime height source is available), the entry is **PENDING** — surfaced on the new `pending_revoked_root_ids` / `pending_revoked_leaf_fingerprints` accessors and gauges, but NOT in the `active_roots` filter, NOT in the local leaf self-check (Run 061), NOT in the qbind-net peer-handshake `with_pqc_leaf_revocations(...)` enforcement context (Run 052). Legacy bundles (no `activation_height` on any entry) preserve Run 050/052 behaviour bit-for-bit (immediate, no height gate); legacy `effective_from`-future entries (no `activation_height`) continue to appear in NEITHER the active NOR the pending sets exactly as before (they remain on the bundle envelope and are reported only via `configured_revocations_total`). Tampering `activation_height` on any entry after signing invalidates the ML-DSA-44 bundle signature (proven by `tampering_revocation_activation_height_after_signing_fails_signature` in both lib and integration suites and by the canonical-fingerprint coverage test). Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, Run 050, Run 051, Run 052, Run 053, Run 054, Run 055, Run 056, Run 057, Run 058, Run 059, Run 060, and Run 061 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit (regression suites all green; see "Tests").

**What changed (Run 062).** (1) `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs`: the `TrustBundleRevocation` struct gains a `#[serde(default)] activation_height: Option<u64>` field that participates in `canonical_signing_bytes` and `canonical_fingerprint`; `LoadedTrustBundle` gains `pending_revoked_root_ids: BTreeSet<[u8;32]>`, `pending_revoked_leaf_fingerprints: BTreeSet<[u8;32]>`, and accessors `pending_revoked_root_count()`, `pending_revoked_leaf_fingerprint_count()`, `configured_revocations_total()`, `active_revocations_total()`, `pending_revocations_total()`; the new validation entrypoint `validate_at_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_revocation_activation(..., current_height: Option<u64>)` is the canonical path the binary calls — the existing `validate_at_with_signing_keys_and_chain_id` shim treats height-gated entries as PENDING (fail-safe — never enforce early without an authoritative runtime height). (2) `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs`: after the existing Run 050/051 trust-bundle-loaded log line, the binary emits one new `[binary] Run 062: trust-bundle revocation activation (configured=N active=A pending=P root_active=Ra root_pending=Rp leaf_active=La leaf_pending=Lp)` log line and sets the seven new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revocations_*` gauges (configured/active/pending totals + root/leaf splits). The active/pending split is symmetrical between root and leaf scope; `_root_active` equals the legacy `_revoked_roots` gauge by construction (kept as a separate name so the active vs. pending split is symmetrical with the leaf surface and so `_revoked_roots`'s long-standing semantics are not silently re-meaning'd to include pending entries). (3) `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs`: seven new gauges added under the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_*` family; no rename of any existing metric, no widening of any existing gauge, no new metric family (all under the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_*` family scrape-shape). (4) `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs`: four new bundle modes — `signed-devnet-leaf-revocation-pending-v0` (leaf revocation with `activation_height = u64::MAX`), `signed-devnet-leaf-revocation-active-v0` (leaf revocation with `activation_height = 0`), `signed-devnet-root-revocation-pending` (root-scope revocation with `activation_height = u64::MAX`), `signed-devnet-root-revocation-active` (root-scope revocation with `activation_height = 0`); plus an optional 7th positional argument `[revocation_activation_height_for_target_override]` (decimal `u64` or `none`) that overrides the per-mode default before signing so the signed preimage and canonical fingerprint cover the operator-supplied value. (5) NEW `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_062_pqc_revocation_activation_tests.rs` (11 integration tests). (6) NEW lib tests inside `pqc_trust_bundle.rs` (11 tests covering legacy / satisfied / future / unavailable / canonical-fingerprint / serde-default / signature-tamper). (7) NEW `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_062.md` evidence doc. (8) This row.

**Anchoring (Run 062).** The active/pending split at parse/validate time is pinned by `pqc_trust_bundle::TrustBundle::validate_at_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_revocation_activation` (the resolution rule lives there in one place; both the active and the pending sets are computed from the same per-entry decision, so a revocation is never silently in BOTH sets and never silently in NEITHER when its gates are satisfied). The signature-coverage of `activation_height` is pinned by `canonical_signing_bytes` / `canonical_fingerprint` and proven by `run062_canonical_fingerprint_covers_revocation_activation_height` (lib) and `tampering_revocation_activation_height_after_signing_fails_signature` (integration). The PENDING-entries-are-never-enforced invariant on the local-leaf surface is pinned by Run 061's local-leaf self-check: that check reads `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` only and the parser only inserts an entry there when `activation_height` resolves to satisfied, so pending entries cannot reach the self-check — proven on the live release binary by Smoke 1 (`active=0 pending=1 leaf_pending=1`, exit 124, no FATAL). The same invariant on the qbind-net peer-handshake surface is pinned by `P2pNodeBuilder::with_pqc_leaf_revocations(...)` which receives `loaded.revoked_leaf_fingerprints` (active set only). The active-and-satisfied entry behaves identically to the legacy Run 052 immediate revocation, proven on the live release binary by Smoke 2 (`active=1 leaf_active=1`, exit 1, the existing Run 061 FATAL fires). Root-scope: `loaded.active_roots` filters out only `revoked_root_ids` (active set); a pending root-revocation keeps the root in `active_roots` (Smoke 3 exit 124, `active_roots=1 root_pending=1`); a satisfied root-revocation excludes it immediately, identical to legacy Run 050 (Smoke 4 exit 1 on no-active-roots, `active_roots=0 revoked_roots=1`). The serde wire-compat default (`#[serde(default)]` on the new field) keeps any pre-Run-062 producer's bundle JSON parseable without modification (proven by `run062_serde_default_for_missing_activation_height` and by the integration test `legacy_no_activation_height_leaf_revocation_is_active`).

**Tests.** All required regression suites pass on the Run 062 working tree: `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 91/91 (= 80 baseline + 11 new Run 062 unit tests); `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_activation` 14/14; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_root_config` ✓; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_devnet_helper` ✓; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib metrics` 78/78 (no metric-family-emitted-once test broke — the seven new gauges live under the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_*` family scrape-shape, and the format-metrics-emitted-once tests still pass); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_062_pqc_revocation_activation_tests` 11/11 (NEW); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_061_pqc_local_leaf_self_check_tests` 9/9; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_057_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `cargo test -p qbind-net --test run_052_leaf_revocation_handshake_tests` 9/9; `cargo check -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warning + the pre-existing `verify_pool::worker_id` unused-variable warning, both unrelated to Run 062). Four release-binary live smokes recorded in the evidence doc: Smoke 1 leaf-revocation pending (exit 124, `Run 062: configured=1 active=0 pending=1 leaf_pending=1`, no FATAL — Run 061 self-check correctly skips a pending leaf revocation); Smoke 2 leaf-revocation active (exit 1, `Run 062: configured=1 active=1 leaf_active=1`, the existing Run 061 FATAL fires — proves the satisfied gate flows correctly to the local-leaf enforcement set); Smoke 3 root-revocation pending (exit 124, `active_roots=1 revoked_roots=0` AND `Run 062: configured=1 active=0 pending=1 root_pending=1`, root remains in active set — proves a pending root-revocation does NOT silently exclude the root); Smoke 4 root-revocation active (exit 1 on no-active-roots, `active_roots=0 revoked_roots=1`, FATAL `--p2p-mutual-auth required + --p2p-pqc-root-mode pqc-static-root requires at least one configured trusted root` — identical behaviour to legacy Run 050 root-revocation). The seven new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revocations_*` gauges are confirmed scrapeable on `/metrics` during a live Smoke 1 dwell (configured=1, active=0, pending=1, root_active=0, root_pending=0, leaf_active=0, leaf_pending=1). Binary identity recorded in the evidence doc: `qbind-node` sha256 `a14e36d2fbb603531fa6ca0eca8268173b474985c3e543e9b6f493581c90880c`, sha1 `215186095d224f018999a06f55036abe8898af62`; `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` sha256 `ff6c276763934f239bc2cd652086abaa29dce7d0a4e859982b3a67499e67eea2`; `devnet_pqc_root_helper` sha256 `9332b228e86aa1c65a3270a2bd3ad471f9797e6ae54c00db7526e1a80b28008d`.

**No-fallback proof (Run 062).** No `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced; no classical signature surface was introduced (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer); no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority; no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change; no removal or modification of any existing test (only additions, plus the strictly mechanical `activation_height: None` field added to existing `TrustBundleRevocation { ... }` literals so they continue to compile under the new struct shape — the existing assertions are unchanged). The new validation entrypoint is additive; the legacy `validate_at_with_signing_keys_and_chain_id` is preserved as a back-compat shim that fail-closed treats height-gated entries as PENDING (i.e. behaves *more* conservatively than its pre-Run-062 callers, never less). The seven new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revocations_*` gauges follow the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_*` naming family and never duplicate, rename, or widen the meaning of `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_revoked_roots` (which retains its long-standing "currently-enforced root-revocations" semantics, equal to `_root_active` by construction). The helper modes mint root + signing keys ephemerally in memory; the helper signature accepts no private-key material; no `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `bundle-signing.sk` file is written under any Run 062 fixture directory (verified by inspecting `/tmp/qbind_run062/**` after every smoke). All FATAL log lines emitted in the negative smokes carry only public material (8-hex prefixes + the static marker phrase + the explicit non-fallback claim "Refusing to start P2P. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle-revoked local leaf" reused from Run 061). **No fabricated metric** (every new gauge was scrape-verified live on Smoke 1), **no silent regression** (every prior regression suite is green), **no protocol behaviour change** (the schema gains exactly one optional field with a serde-compatible default), **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of the helper API surface to accept private-key material**, and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 062).** (a) **Root-level local revocation self-check.** Unchanged from the Run 061 §10 item (a) boundary — the binary still does NOT fail closed at startup when the operator's local leaf was issued by a root that is itself on the bundle's `revoked_root_ids` (active set), without the leaf's own fingerprint being on `revoked_leaf_fingerprints`. The Run 050 root-revocation axis remains enforced at cert verify time under `--p2p-mutual-auth required`. With Run 062, an operator can now SCHEDULE a root revocation via `activation_height`, but the local-leaf-issuance-from-revoked-root startup check itself is still open. (b) **`activation_epoch` runtime source on per-entry revocations.** Run 062 only adds a per-entry `activation_height` (block-height) gate; an analogous per-entry `activation_epoch` field is intentionally NOT added — the bundle-level Run 057 boundary (`CurrentEpochUnavailable` fail-closed) is unchanged, and there is currently no production runtime epoch source. (c) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on revocation entries.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061 bundle-level boundary — the binary does NOT enforce a minimum margin between a revocation's `activation_height` and the current finalised height. The runbook §5.3 / §6.B / §6.C SHOULD be updated to recommend a minimum margin for *scheduled* revocations specifically (separate evidence/doc-only run; intentionally NOT done here). (d) **In-binary bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060 boundary. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Unchanged from the Run 059/060/061 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged. (h) **Operator playbook prose update.** Run 060's `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` does not yet describe how to use `activation_height` on revocation entries. The runbook is intentionally NOT updated in Run 062 (Run 062 is source-and-evidence, not operator-doc); a future evidence/documentation-only run may align the runbook prose. (i) **`/metrics` `_pending_total` does not bump a counter on activation.** The seven Run 062 gauges are sticky-at-startup snapshots (the trust bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime); a future run may add an "activation transition observed at runtime" counter family if/when on-the-fly trust-bundle hot-reload is supported. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 062; Run 062 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle revocation-entry activation-gate surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 062 narrows the trust-bundle revocation-rotation surface; all Run 060 §10 / Run 061 remaining items not explicitly addressed above persist unchanged.
#### C4 Run 063 evidence update (2026-05-13) — root-level local revocation startup self-check on the PQC trust bundle (NARROW C4 sub-piece); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 063 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_063.md`) implements, exercises on the live release binary, and proves the smallest production-honest **root-level** local revocation startup self-check on the PQC trust-bundle surface introduced by Run 050 and extended by Runs 051/052/054/055/057/058/059/060/061/062. Before Run 063, when an operator launched `qbind-node` with a `--p2p-leaf-cert` whose decoded `NetworkDelegationCert.root_key_id` referred to a transport root that the loaded signed PQC trust bundle had **root-revoked** (i.e. listed on the active `revoked_root_ids` set, with no matching active `revoked_leaf_fingerprints` entry — exactly the gap left open by Run 061's leaf-axis-only self-check), the binary would nevertheless construct its `P2pNodeBuilder`, install the trust context, and proceed toward dialling/listening. The bundle's root-revocation axis was still enforced at peer cert-verify time under `--p2p-mutual-auth required` (Run 050) — `loaded.active_roots` filtered out `revoked_root_ids` — but the fact that the node was carrying *locally* a leaf credential whose issuing root the bundle had revoked was not surfaced as a fail-closed startup boundary. After Run 063, every startup that loads a signed PQC trust bundle with a configured local leaf runs exactly one new self-check — `check_local_leaf_issuer_root_not_revoked` — over the local cert's decoded `root_key_id` against `loaded.revoked_root_ids` (the same active set the cert-verify path consults; the Run 062 *pending* set is explicitly NOT consulted). On match, the binary emits exactly one `[binary] FATAL: Run 063 local leaf certificate issuer root revoked …` line on stderr and calls `std::process::exit(1)` BEFORE any P2P state is constructed, BEFORE `pqc_config` is moved into the builder, and BEFORE any peer connection is attempted. On no match, the binary emits exactly one `[binary] Run 063: local-leaf issuer-root startup self-check passed (local_issuer_root_id=AAAA.. bundle_fp=BBBB.. active_revoked_root_ids=N)` line and continues normally. The Run 061 local-leaf-fingerprint self-check is preserved bit-for-bit; the two startup self-checks are independent (either failing is sufficient to fail closed; both passing emits both log lines). Run 050/051/052/053/054/055/057/058/059/060/061/062 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit (regression suites all green; see "Tests").

**What changed (Run 063).** (1) `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs`: NEW pure helper `pub fn check_local_leaf_issuer_root_not_revoked(local_leaf_cert_bytes: &[u8], active_revoked_root_ids: &HashSet<[u8; 32]>, bundle_fingerprint: &[u8; 32]) -> Result<[u8; 32], LocalLeafIssuerRootSelfCheckError>` that decodes the local cert via the existing `NetworkDelegationCert::decode` path, extracts `root_key_id: [u8; 32]`, and looks it up in the supplied active revoked set. NEW error enum `LocalLeafIssuerRootSelfCheckError { IssuerRootRevoked { root_id_prefix: String, leaf_fingerprint_prefix: String, bundle_fingerprint_prefix: String }, DecodeFailed }` carrying only log-safe 8-hex prefixes (never the full digests, never any private key material). The Run 061 helper `check_local_leaf_not_revoked` and its error enum are preserved bit-for-bit. (2) `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs`: ONE new call site immediately after the existing Run 061 block, immediately before `let pqc_config = PqcStaticRootConfig { … };`. The call site emits `[binary] Run 063: … passed (…)` on `Ok` and `[binary] FATAL: Run 063 …` + `exit(1)` on `Err(IssuerRootRevoked)` or `Err(DecodeFailed)`. No new `/metrics` family is added: the node exits before the HTTP server binds on the negative path; the Run 052 peer-handshake counter `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total` is NOT bumped (it is a handshake-only contract; a startup self-check is not a handshake event). (3) NEW `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_063_pqc_local_issuer_root_self_check_tests.rs` (8 integration tests covering positive non-revoked, negative active-revoked, positive pending-revoked, positive unrelated-active-revoked, root_id parity with `decode_network_delegation_cert`, Run 061 leaf-axis preservation, no-private-material API pin, and active-vs-pending set disjointness at the call site). (4) NEW lib unit tests inside `pqc_trust_bundle.rs::tests::run063_*` (9 tests covering positive non-revoked, positive unrelated-active-revoked, negative active-revoked, negative decode-failed, root_id parity, no-private-key dependency, orthogonality to Run 061 leaf axis, log-safe Display prefixes only, and no peer-handshake metric bleed). (5) `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs`: TWO new bundle modes `signed-devnet-issuer-root-revocation-active-v0` (mints a SECOND fresh DevNet root and appends to `roots[]` BEFORE signing, then root-revokes `roots[0]` — the v0..vN leaf-issuing root — with `activation_height = None`, immediately active) and `signed-devnet-issuer-root-revocation-pending-v0` (same shape but with `activation_height = u64::MAX`, PENDING under the binary's loader). The second root's ephemeral `root_sk` is generated in memory only and discarded at the end of the helper process; only the public second-root id is written out for evidence (`second-root.id.hex`). The second root is the smallest helper extension that lets a release-binary smoke exercise the Run 063 self-check on its negative path (where `roots[0]` is revoked but `roots[1]` remains active so the Run 050 `trusted_roots.is_empty()` FATAL does NOT fire before Run 063). (6) NEW `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_063.md` evidence doc. (7) This row.

**Anchoring (Run 063).** The local issuer-root extraction is identity-pinned to the cert-verify path: the helper decodes the local cert with the same `NetworkDelegationCert::decode` path that `qbind_node::pqc_root_config::decode_network_delegation_cert` uses, and reads the same `root_key_id: [u8; 32]` field. Identity parity is proven by `run063_self_check_uses_same_root_id_as_cert_verify_path` (both as a lib unit test and as an integration test). The active-vs-pending boundary preserves Run 062 bit-for-bit: the helper takes `&HashSet<[u8; 32]>` (the active set type the rest of the bundle pipeline already uses for `loaded.revoked_root_ids`); the call site supplies `&loaded.revoked_root_ids` exclusively, never `&loaded.pending_revoked_root_ids`. The boundary is pinned by the integration test `run063_pending_revoked_root_never_bleeds_into_active_set_used_by_helper` and proven on the live release binary by Smoke 3 (`Run 062: configured=1 active=0 pending=1 root_active=0 root_pending=1` AND `Run 063: … passed (active_revoked_root_ids=0)`, exit 124, no FATAL). The orthogonality to Run 061's leaf-fingerprint axis is pinned by `run063_self_check_is_orthogonal_to_leaf_fingerprint_axis` (lib) and `run063_does_not_weaken_run_061_local_leaf_fingerprint_self_check` (integration): a bundle that revokes the local leaf's fingerprint (Run 061 negative) still fires the Run 061 FATAL before Run 063 has a chance to evaluate; a bundle that revokes the local cert's issuing root (Run 063 negative) still fires the Run 063 FATAL whether or not the leaf fingerprint is also listed. The "no private key material on the helper API" boundary is pinned by `run063_self_check_does_not_require_private_key_material` (lib) and `run063_helper_signature_pins_no_private_key_dependency` (integration). The "no Run 052 metric bleed" boundary is pinned by `run063_self_check_does_not_touch_peer_handshake_metric_family` (lib). The FATAL line carries 8-hex prefixes only and the static marker phrase + explicit non-fallback claim "Refusing to start P2P. No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root on bundle-revoked local issuer root."
