**No-fallback proof (Run 064).** No `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no feature flag was added; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced anywhere except inside an explicit no-`Dummy*` claim; no classical signature surface was introduced; no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority; no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change (Run 064 is documentation-only and could not change runtime behaviour even if it tried). No existing test was modified or removed (no test file is touched at all). The updated runbook explicitly preserves the Run 060 strict-invariants table and adds three new invariant rows that strictly narrow operator behaviour (one more startup fail-closed boundary on the leaf-fingerprint axis, one more startup fail-closed boundary on the issuer-root axis, one new active/pending split that strictly enforces the pending-entries-are-never-enforced rule). No private-key bytes appear in any Run 064 artefact. **No fabricated metric** (Run 064 introduces no metric at all; the seven Run 062 `_revocations_*` gauges referenced in §9 are scrape-verified live in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_062.md`), **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of any helper API surface to accept private-key material**, and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / second-root `root_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 064).** (a) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061/062/063 boundary — the binary does NOT enforce a minimum margin between `activation_height` (bundle-level or per-entry revocation) and the current finalised height. The updated runbook §5.3 and §6.E RECOMMEND a margin but enforcement remains operator policy, not binary policy. (b) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged — bundle-level `activation_epoch` continues to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`; per-entry `activation_epoch` on revocations is intentionally NOT supported (Run 062 boundary). (c) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload.** Unchanged — the bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime; the Run 062 active/pending gauges are sticky-at-startup snapshots; the Run 061/063 startup self-checks observe only the trust state present at process boot; a PENDING → ACTIVE transition is not observed inside a running validator without a restart. (d) **In-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060 boundary; out-of-band CLI overlap (Run 060 §6.D) remains the supported rotation path. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Unchanged from the Run 059/060/061/062/063 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged. (h) **Per-environment production trust-anchor operation.** Unchanged — depends on the operator actually using offline / HSM custody for the secrets in §3.2 / §3.4. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 064; Run 064 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the operator-documentation surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 064 closes only the operator-playbook-prose gap left open by Run 061 §10 item (h) and Run 062 §10 item (h); all other Run 060 / 061 / 062 / 063 §10 remaining items persist unchanged.


**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 063).** (a) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on root revocations.** Run 063 enforces the *current* active revoked-root set; it does NOT enforce a minimum margin between a scheduled root revocation's `activation_height` and the current finalised height. Unchanged from the Run 062 §10 item (c) boundary. (b) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot-reload.** Run 063 is a startup-time check. If the trust bundle is rotated under the running binary (currently NOT a supported operation), the Run 063 check does not re-run on the live process; operators must restart `qbind-node` to re-evaluate the local leaf's issuing root. Unchanged from the Run 050/051/052/057/061/062 boundary. (c) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061/062 boundary. (d) **In-binary bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060 boundary. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Unchanged from the Run 059/060/061/062 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged. (h) **Operator playbook prose update.** Run 060's `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` does not yet describe the Run 063 startup-time root-revoked-local-issuer self-check. The runbook is intentionally NOT updated in Run 063 (Run 063 is source-and-evidence, not operator-doc); a future evidence/documentation-only run may align the runbook prose to record the new fail-closed boundary. (i) **No new `/metrics` family.** A future run may add a `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_startup_self_check_rejected_total` counter family if/when on-the-fly trust-bundle hot-reload is supported (so that a counter bumped at the self-check site is then scrapeable across the process lifetime). (j) **Leaf-axis pending semantics.** Run 062's pending leaf revocations are NOT consulted by the Run 061 helper, and Run 063 does NOT change that. The leaf axis and the root axis are independent; Run 063 only adds the root-axis startup check. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 063; Run 063 does not touch timeout / NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle startup self-check surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 063 closes only the Run 060 §10 / Run 061 §10 / Run 062 §10 item (a) "root-level local revocation self-check" sub-piece; all other Run 060 / Run 061 / Run 062 §10 remaining items persist unchanged.

#### C4 Run 065 evidence update (2026-05-13) — per-environment minimum activation-height policy on the PQC trust bundle (NARROW C4 sub-piece); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 065 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_065.md`) implements, exercises on the live release binary, and proves the smallest production-honest **per-environment minimum activation-height policy** on the PQC trust bundle surface introduced by Run 050 and extended by Runs 051/052/054/055/057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064. Before Run 065, the binary enforced bundle-level forward-dated activation-height gating (Run 057/058) and per-entry revocation activation-height gating (Run 062), but did NOT enforce any minimum margin between `activation_height` and the current finalised height — an operator on TestNet or MainNet could ship a signed PQC trust bundle whose `activation_height` equalled `current_height` and force an effective same-block rotation (the "production-honest minimum margin" boundary explicitly carried forward as still-open in Run 057 §10(a), Run 058 §10(a), Run 060 §10(a), Run 061 §10, Run 062 §10(c), Run 063 §10(a), Run 064 §10(a) / non-goal §1.2 / §10). After Run 065, every signed trust bundle load runs exactly one new pure policy check — `check_min_activation_height_policy` — over the parsed bundle, the runtime `TrustBundleEnvironment`, and the same `current_height: Option<u64>` source that Run 057 uses. The reject window is the half-open interval `[current_height, current_height + minimum_activation_margin)`; bundles whose `activation_height` lies in that interval fail closed with the new `TrustBundleActivationError::ActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin { environment, current_height, activation_height, minimum_margin, required_min_height, scope }` (or `RevocationActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin { … scope: RevocationScope { root_id, leaf_fingerprint } }` for per-entry scheduled revocations); bundles whose `activation_height` is at or above `current_height + margin` pass Run 065 and fall through to Run 057's existing future-height gate; bundles whose `activation_height` is strictly less than `current_height` (already-effective in the past) are intentionally not retroactively rejected (preserves snapshot-rejoin semantics for older valid bundles). Per-entry revocations with `activation_height = None` are intentionally NEVER subject to Run 065, preserving the emergency immediate-revocation path on MainNet. The new policy is applied AFTER signature/chain_id/environment/revocation structural validation and BEFORE Run 057 future-height gating, Run 055 sequence persistence, and Run 050 root merge — so a rejected too-soon bundle does NOT create a `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json`, does NOT update `loaded.active_roots`, and does NOT bring up any P2P state. The constants are `MIN_DEVNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 0` (preserves Runs 050–064 DevNet immediate-cutover behaviour bit-for-bit), `MIN_TESTNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 8` blocks, and `MIN_MAINNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 32` blocks; the strict ordering DevNet < TestNet < MainNet is pinned by `run065_policy_constants_are_deterministic`. Run 050/051/052/053/054/055/056/057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064 behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit (regression suites all green; see "Tests").

**What changed (Run 065).** (1) `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_activation.rs`: NEW per-environment constants `pub const MIN_DEVNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN: u64 = 0;`, `pub const MIN_TESTNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN: u64 = 8;`, `pub const MIN_MAINNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN: u64 = 32;`. NEW `pub struct ActivationPolicy { pub minimum_activation_margin: u64 }` + `ActivationPolicy::for_environment(env: TrustBundleEnvironment) -> Self` + free function `pub fn minimum_activation_margin_for_environment(env: TrustBundleEnvironment) -> u64` (the single source of truth). NEW pure helper `pub fn check_min_activation_height_policy(bundle: &TrustBundle, env: TrustBundleEnvironment, current_height: Option<u64>) -> Result<(), TrustBundleActivationError>`. NEW error variants on the existing `TrustBundleActivationError` enum: `ActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin { environment: TrustBundleEnvironment, current_height: u64, activation_height: u64, minimum_margin: u64, required_min_height: u64, scope: ActivationScope }` (the existing Run 057 `ActivationScope::{Bundle, Root(root_id)}` enum is reused) and `RevocationActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin { environment, current_height, activation_height, minimum_margin, required_min_height, scope: RevocationScope { root_id: String, leaf_fingerprint: Option<String> } }`. Display surface is log-safe: only 8-hex prefixes on `RevocationScope.root_id` / `leaf_fingerprint`, the explicit reschedule guidance (`Reschedule the bundle with activation_height >= <required_min_height> (= current_height + minimum_margin)`), the explicit emergency-revocation guidance for scheduled-revocation errors (`Emergency revocations should be published without activation_height (immediate)`), and the static "No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root" non-fallback marker. The `ActivationOutcome` helpers `is_future_activation` and `required_min_height_for_metrics` are extended to recognise the two new variants. `required_min_height` is computed as `current_height.saturating_add(margin)`; the saturating add is defence-in-depth so a near-`u64::MAX` `current_height` cannot wrap to a tiny `required_min_height` and silently admit every activation (pinned by `run065_required_min_height_saturates_on_overflow`). 17 NEW unit tests inside `pqc_trust_activation::tests::run065_*`: the constants pin (`run065_policy_constants_are_deterministic`), DevNet zero+immediate accepted (`run065_devnet_activation_height_zero_accepted`, `run065_devnet_activation_height_equals_current_accepted`), missing-activation-height unaffected (`run065_missing_activation_height_unaffected_on_mainnet`), TestNet/MainNet below-margin rejected with full scoped-error and marker-phrase assertions (`run065_testnet_activation_height_below_margin_rejected`, `run065_mainnet_activation_height_below_margin_rejected`), TestNet immediate-cutover rejected (`run065_testnet_immediate_cutover_rejected`), TestNet/MainNet at-margin accepted (inclusive upper boundary) (`run065_testnet_activation_height_at_margin_accepted`, `run065_mainnet_activation_height_at_margin_accepted`), TestNet far-above accepted (`run065_testnet_activation_height_above_margin_accepted`), already-effective NOT retroactively rejected (`run065_testnet_already_effective_bundle_not_retroactively_rejected`, `run065_already_effective_scheduled_revocation_not_retroactively_rejected`), per-active-root activation-height also constrained (`run065_root_level_activation_height_below_margin_rejected_on_testnet`), Retired root activation-height advisory-only (`run065_retired_root_activation_height_not_enforced`), immediate revocation preserved on MainNet (`run065_immediate_revocation_preserved_on_mainnet`), scheduled revocation below margin rejected on MainNet with full marker-phrase + emergency-revocation guidance + non-fallback claim asserted (`run065_scheduled_revocation_below_margin_rejected_on_mainnet`), scheduled revocation at margin accepted on TestNet (`run065_scheduled_revocation_at_margin_accepted_on_testnet`), non-zero `current_height` boundary on `--restore-from-snapshot` (`run065_required_min_is_current_plus_margin_on_restore`), `current_height = None` silence (`run065_no_current_height_source_does_not_fire_policy`), and `u64::MAX` saturation (`run065_required_min_height_saturates_on_overflow`). (2) `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_bundle.rs`: `load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` calls `pqc_trust_activation::check_min_activation_height_policy` AFTER `validate_at_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_revocation_activation` (so the parsed bundle has been structurally validated, signature-verified, chain_id-checked, environment-checked, and per-entry revocation-validated) and BEFORE `check_bundle_activation` (Run 057 future-height gate) so a too-soon production scheduling surfaces as a Run 065 margin violation with a precise remedy rather than Run 057's generic "not yet reached" error. The two checks compose cleanly without overlap (pinned by `run065_signed_testnet_at_margin_reaches_run057_boundary`, `run065_signed_mainnet_at_margin_reaches_run057_boundary`, `run065_future_height_still_handled_by_run_057_gate`). The new helper is invoked BEFORE the caller proceeds to `pqc_trust_sequence::check_and_update_sequence` and `loaded.active_roots` merge in `main.rs` — the no-side-effects boundary on rejected bundles is pinned by `run065_too_soon_bundle_does_not_touch_loader_outcome` AND proven on the live release binary by Smoke 2 / Smoke 4 (no `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` under the data dir after a rejected too-soon load). (3) `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs`: the existing `_activation_height_required` set-once at the trust-bundle-activation-rejection branch is extended to also recognise the two new Run 065 errors (so the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_rejected{required_height_label}` metric remains accurate); no new metric family is introduced; the two new variants flow through the existing `TrustBundleError::Activation(..)` FATAL printer with no new printer call site needed (the `Display` impl on `TrustBundleActivationError` carries the full scoped context, the explicit reschedule guidance, and the static "No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root" marker). (4) NEW `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_065_pqc_min_activation_margin_tests.rs` (12 integration tests over real ML-DSA-44 signed bundles: DevNet activation=0/current=0 loads, TestNet too-soon fails closed with `ActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin{Bundle}`, TestNet at-margin reaches Run 057's "not yet reached" boundary, TestNet already-effective bundle loads (snapshot-rejoin), MainNet too-soon fails closed, MainNet at-margin reaches Run 057's "not yet reached" boundary, MainNet already-effective bundle loads, MainNet immediate emergency revocation preserved (`activation_height = None`), MainNet scheduled revocation below margin fails closed with `RevocationActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin`, rejected too-soon bundle does not leak a sequence-persistence file (strict-ordering boundary), far-future bundle is still handled by Run 057 not by Run 065 (orthogonality boundary), DevNet scheduled revocation at activation_height = 0 still loads (preserves Run 062 DevNet shape)). (5) NEW `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_065.md` evidence doc with five live release-binary smokes. (6) This row.

**Anchoring (Run 065).** The constants live next to the rest of activation gating in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_activation.rs` (same module as Run 057's `check_bundle_activation` and Run 062's per-entry-revocation gating), exposed via `minimum_activation_margin_for_environment(env)` as the single source of truth. The half-open reject window `[current_height, current_height + margin)` is the exact dual of the Run 057 inclusive upper boundary — bundles at `current_height + margin` pass Run 065 and either load (if Run 057 also accepts: e.g. an operator running a node that has already advanced past the activation height) or fall through to Run 057's "not yet reached" error (if `current_height < activation_height`). Bundles below `current_height` are already-effective and not retroactively rejected — that boundary preserves snapshot-rejoin semantics and is pinned by `run065_testnet_already_effective_bundle_not_retroactively_rejected`, `run065_already_effective_scheduled_revocation_not_retroactively_rejected`, `run065_signed_testnet_already_effective_loads`, `run065_signed_mainnet_already_effective_loads`. Per-entry revocations with `activation_height = None` are NEVER subject to Run 065, preserving the Run 052 / Run 062 immediate-revocation emergency-response path; pinned at the unit level by `run065_immediate_revocation_preserved_on_mainnet` and at the integration level by `run065_immediate_revocation_preserved_on_signed_mainnet`. The strict ordering through the loader (Run 065 BEFORE Run 057 future-height gate, BEFORE Run 055 sequence persistence, BEFORE Run 050 root merge) is pinned both at the integration-test level (`run065_too_soon_bundle_does_not_touch_loader_outcome`) and proven on the live release binary by Smoke 2 (TestNet too-soon) and Smoke 4 (MainNet too-soon) where the data directory is never created at all. The new helper signature `check_min_activation_height_policy(&TrustBundle, TrustBundleEnvironment, Option<u64>)` takes only public material and returns either `Ok(())` or a public-only error enum (8-hex prefixes only, `environment` enum, and integer-valued context fields); no `*_sk` byte slice is referenced; no private digest is logged. Five release-binary live smokes recorded in the evidence doc, each carrying the full bundle fingerprint prefix and the exact stderr FATAL line: Smoke 1 positive (DevNet `activation_height=0` against `current_height=0`, exit 124 = external timeout, sequence file present at `/tmp/qbind_run065/data_smoke1/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json`); Smoke 2 negative (TestNet `activation_height=7` against `current_height=0`, exit 1, `pqc trust-bundle minimum activation-height policy violation (scope=bundle, environment=testnet, current_height=0, activation_height=7, minimum_margin=8, required_min_height=8); fail closed — declared activation_height is too close to current_height for environment testnet. Reschedule the bundle with activation_height >= 8 (= current_height + minimum_margin). No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root.`, no data dir created); Smoke 3 (TestNet `activation_height=8` against `current_height=0`, exit 1 with Run 057 `activation height not yet reached (scope=bundle, current_height=0, required_height=8)` — proves Run 065 passes at the inclusive upper boundary and Run 057 takes over); Smoke 4 negative (MainNet `activation_height=10` against `current_height=0`, exit 1, `pqc trust-bundle minimum activation-height policy violation (… environment=mainnet, … minimum_margin=32, required_min_height=32); … Reschedule the bundle with activation_height >= 32 …`); Smoke 5 (MainNet `activation_height=32` against `current_height=0`, exit 1 with Run 057 `activation height not yet reached (… required_height=32)`). Binary identity recorded in the evidence doc: `qbind-node` sha256 `574709fbeec1fce106f10893d21fe5c0d4b1ac9d888518bf6bab064d46b94a30`, Build ID `cc9c0663408f7abd6f3ac373f56a8a41da2802d0`; `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` sha256 `0b750de4d467031c0cac7229dd6b4beb20937e84cbdfc05110996aedf6bf6a6d`, Build ID `065505c8f0b1ee6d39e803b7ad7487a46892f7eb`.

**Tests.** All required regression suites pass on the Run 065 working tree: `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_activation` 34/34 (= 14 Run 057 baseline + 17 new Run 065 unit tests + 3 ActivationOutcome helpers); `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_bundle` 100/100; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21; `cargo test -p qbind-node --lib` 946/946 (= 926 Run 063/064 baseline + 20 net new in the `pqc_trust_activation` module); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_065_pqc_min_activation_margin_tests` 12/12 (NEW); `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_063_pqc_local_issuer_root_self_check_tests` 8/8; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_062_pqc_revocation_activation_tests` 11/11; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_061_pqc_local_leaf_self_check_tests` 9/9; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_057_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_055_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_052_pqc_leaf_revocation_tests` 12/12; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_051_pqc_trust_bundle_signing_tests` 13/13; `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_050_pqc_trust_bundle_tests` 14/14; `cargo build --release -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node --example devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper --example devnet_pqc_root_helper` clean (only pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warning + the pre-existing `verify_pool::worker_id` unused-variable warning, both unrelated to Run 065).

**No-fallback proof (Run 065).** No `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no feature flag was added; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced; no classical signature surface was introduced (suite 100 / ML-DSA-44 only on the bundle layer); no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority; no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change. No existing test was modified or removed. No new helper bundle mode was added — the existing `signed-devnet` / `signed-testnet` / `signed-mainnet` modes plus the existing positional `[activation_height_override]` argument already cover the inputs the policy exercises. The new `check_min_activation_height_policy` helper is additive; the legacy Run 057 `check_bundle_activation` and Run 062 per-entry-revocation validation helpers are preserved bit-for-bit (no rename, no signature widening, no overlap). The new helper signature takes only public material: `&TrustBundle` (public, deserialised from the public `--p2p-trust-bundle` file and signature-verified before this call), `TrustBundleEnvironment` (the runtime enum), and `Option<u64>` (the public `current_height` source already used by Run 057). The helper returns either `Ok(())` or a public-only error enum (8-hex prefixes on `RevocationScope.root_id` / `leaf_fingerprint`, `environment` enum, integer context fields). The boundary is pinned by the `Option<u64> -> Result<(), TrustBundleActivationError>` signature itself: no `&[u8]` cert bytes, no `&HashSet<…>` private digest, no signing-key handle is accepted. The FATAL log lines emitted on the negative smokes carry only public material: the static marker phrases ("pqc trust-bundle minimum activation-height policy violation", "pqc trust-bundle scheduled-revocation minimum activation-height policy violation"), the integer context fields, the explicit reschedule guidance (`Reschedule the bundle with activation_height >= <required_min_height> (= current_height + minimum_margin)`), the explicit emergency-revocation guidance for scheduled-revocation errors (`Emergency revocations should be published without activation_height (immediate)`), and the explicit non-fallback claim "No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root". The Run 052 peer-handshake counter `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_revoked_total` is NOT bumped by Run 065 (it remains a handshake-only contract; a load-time activation-policy rejection is not a handshake event). The existing Run 057 metric label `required_height_label` on `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_rejected` is extended to also surface `required_min_height` for the two new variants — no new metric family is introduced. **No fabricated metric** (Run 065 introduces no new metric family), **no silent regression** (every prior regression suite is green; the Run 050/051/052/054/055/056/057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064 boundary tests all still pass bit-for-bit), **no protocol behaviour change** (no bundle schema change, no cert schema change, no wire format change — Run 065 is a pure consumer of existing bundle fields), **no removed tests**, **no DummySig/DummyKem/DummyAead fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of the helper API surface to accept private-key material**, and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

#### C4 Run 066 evidence update (2026-05-13) — operator playbook prose updated for Run 065 (DOCS-ONLY); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 066 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_066.md`) updates the Run 064 operator playbook (`docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md`) so that operator guidance accurately reflects Run 065 — the per-environment minimum activation-margin policy enforced at bundle load on the binary `--p2p-trust-bundle` path: `MIN_DEVNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 0`, `MIN_TESTNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 8`, `MIN_MAINNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 32` blocks (strict ordering DevNet < TestNet < MainNet); half-open `[current_height, current_height + margin)` reject window applied to the three forward-looking activation scopes (bundle-level `activation_height`, per-active-root `activation_height`, and per-entry revocation `activation_height` when `Some(_)`); per-entry revocations with `activation_height = None` are immediate and intentionally exempt from Run 065 (preserves the MainNet emergency-revocation path, pinned by `run065_immediate_revocation_preserved_on_signed_mainnet`); bundles whose `activation_height < current_height` are already-effective and NOT retroactively rejected (preserves snapshot-rejoin semantics, pinned by `run065_signed_testnet_already_effective_loads` + `run065_signed_mainnet_already_effective_loads`); the policy fires BEFORE Run 057's future-height gate, Run 055's sequence persistence, and Run 050's root merge so a rejected too-soon bundle does NOT create `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` and does NOT update `loaded.active_roots` (pinned by `run065_too_soon_bundle_does_not_touch_loader_outcome` AND proven on the live release binary by RUN_065 Smokes 2/4 where the data directory is never created). Run 066 is **documentation-only** — no `crates/**/src/**` source, no `Cargo.toml`, no test source, no helper source, no `main.rs` / `pqc_trust_bundle.rs` / `pqc_trust_sequence.rs` / `pqc_trust_activation.rs` / `pqc_root_config.rs` / `cli.rs` / `metrics.rs` / `p2p_node_builder.rs` was touched; Run 037, Run 040, Run 044, and the entire Run 050–065 chain are preserved bit-for-bit.

**Tests / checks.** Run 066 modifies no Rust source, so no regression suite is re-run by Run 066 itself; the Run 065 baseline (`cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_activation` 34/34, `--lib pqc_trust_bundle` 100/100, `--lib pqc_trust_sequence` 21/21, `--lib` 946/946, `--test run_065_pqc_min_activation_margin_tests` 12/12, `--test run_063_pqc_local_issuer_root_self_check_tests` 8/8, `--test run_062_pqc_revocation_activation_tests` 11/11, `--test run_061_pqc_local_leaf_self_check_tests` 9/9, every Run 050–059 suite, `cargo build --release -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node --example devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper --example devnet_pqc_root_helper` clean) is preserved bit-for-bit. Documentation-side checks all pass: (a) no recommendation to use `--p2p-trusted-root` as a fallback — every occurrence in the runbook is inside an invariant forbidding the fallback (§1.3, §6.B step 3), a workflow documenting how the binary refuses the flag combination (§6.A, §6.D), the §12 glossary forbidding it with `--p2p-trust-bundle` on TestNet/MainNet, or a direct quotation of the Run 061/063/065 FATAL "No fallback to --p2p-trusted-root" claim; (b) no recommendation to use `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` — every occurrence is inside a "MUST NOT register `Dummy*`" / "no `Dummy*` is registered" claim anchored in Runs 037/039/040/041; (c) no recommendation to accept unsigned MainNet bundles — every occurrence either records that unsigned bundles are allowed only on DevNet (§5.1), explicitly forbids them on TestNet/MainNet (§5.2, §5.3, §1.3 invariants table), or cites RUN_059 Smoke 2 as proof MainNet rejects them; (d) no recommendation to reuse a transport root key as a bundle-signing key — every occurrence of "reuse" / "same key" is inside §2.1 / §2.2 / §4.4 forbidding it. `cargo check -p qbind-node --bin qbind-node` is clean (only the pre-existing `bincode::config` deprecation warnings on `crates/qbind-node/src/binary_consensus_loop.rs:2332` and `:2461`, identical to the Run 065 baseline).

**No-fallback proof (Run 066).** No `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no feature flag was added; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced anywhere except inside an explicit no-`Dummy*` claim; no classical signature surface was introduced; no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority; no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change (Run 066 is documentation-only and could not change runtime behaviour even if it tried). No existing test was modified or removed (no test file is touched at all). The updated runbook explicitly preserves the Run 064 strict-invariants table and adds one new invariant row that strictly narrows operator behaviour: a load-time fail-closed boundary on the per-environment minimum activation margin. No private-key bytes appear in any Run 066 artefact. **No fabricated metric** (Run 066 introduces no metric at all; Run 065 introduces no new metric family and instead reuses the existing `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_rejected{required_height_label}` family with `required_min_height` on its label as recorded in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_065.md`), **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of any helper API surface to accept private-key material**, and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / second-root `root_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 066).** (a) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064/065 boundary — bundle-level `activation_epoch` continues to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`; per-entry `activation_epoch` on revocations is intentionally NOT supported (Run 062 boundary); Run 065 did NOT introduce a minimum-margin policy on the epoch axis. (b) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on the gossiped / peer-supplied trust-bundle path.** Unchanged from the Run 065 §10(a) boundary — Run 065 enforces the policy on the binary `--p2p-trust-bundle` load path, and the same `pqc_trust_activation::check_min_activation_height_policy` helper must be threaded through the gossiped/peer-supplied path when on-the-fly distribution lands. (c) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload.** Unchanged — the bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime; the Run 062 active/pending gauges are sticky-at-startup snapshots; the Run 061/063 startup self-checks and the Run 065 policy observe only the trust state present at process boot; a PENDING → ACTIVE transition is not observed inside a running validator without a restart. (d) **In-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060/064 boundary; out-of-band CLI overlap (Run 060 §6.D) remains the supported rotation path. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Unchanged from the Run 059/060/061/062/063/064/065 boundary. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged — the `--restore-from-snapshot.snapshot_height` already feeds the Run 057 + Run 065 `current_height` source via `ActivationContext::height_only`; a fully-fledged production fast-sync surface is a separate boundary. (h) **Per-environment production trust-anchor operation.** Unchanged — depends on the operator actually using offline / HSM custody for the secrets in §3.2 / §3.4. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 066; Run 066 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the operator-documentation surface. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 066 closes only the operator-playbook-prose gap left open by Run 065 §10 item (h); all other Run 060/061/062/063/064/065 §10 remaining items persist unchanged.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 065).** (a) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on the gossiped / peer-supplied trust-bundle path.** Run 065 enforces the policy at `load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` — the path the binary uses for `--p2p-trust-bundle`. The bundle is not currently gossiped between peers (operator-distributed); when on-the-fly trust-bundle distribution lands, the same `check_min_activation_height_policy` helper must be threaded through that path. Unchanged from the Run 057 / Run 062 boundary. (b) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from Run 057 §10(b): bundle-level `activation_epoch` continues to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`; per-entry `activation_epoch` on revocations is intentionally NOT supported (Run 062 boundary). Run 065 does NOT introduce a minimum-margin policy on the epoch axis. (c) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload.** Unchanged from the Run 050/057/061/062/063/064 boundary. The bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime; Run 065's check fires at that single load. (d) **In-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060 boundary. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Unchanged from the Run 059/060/061/062/063/064 boundary. Run 065 proves only the load-time policy on a single-validator startup smoke. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged. The `--restore-from-snapshot` `current_height` source already feeds the Run 065 policy via `ActivationContext::height_only`; a fully-fledged production fast-sync surface is a separate boundary. (h) **Operator playbook prose for the new minimum margin.** Run 064's `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` non-goal item explicitly lists the per-environment minimum-activation-margin policy as a non-goal for that run; the runbook is intentionally NOT updated in Run 065 (Run 065 is source-and-evidence, not operator-doc). A future docs-only run may align the runbook prose to record the new constants and reschedule guidance, and to remove the §10 / §1.2 non-goal item. (i) **Per-entry revocation FATAL surface in `main.rs`.** Run 065's `RevocationActivationHeightBelowMinimumMargin` flows through the existing `TrustBundleError::Activation` printer; a future run may add a dedicated metric label for scheduled-revocation rejections if operator dashboards need to distinguish them from bundle-level rejections. (j) **Constants choice.** The Run 065 constants (DevNet 0, TestNet 8, MainNet 32) are conservative-but-test-friendly for the current evidence/devnet environment. They are intentionally large enough to make a same-block "surprise rotate" impossible on TestNet/MainNet but small enough that operator/test scheduling can hit them without contrived height settings. A future production-readiness run may revise the constants upward (e.g. MainNet 256 or 1024 blocks) once a real-time observability and ratification surface exists; the current constants are still net-strictly-stricter than the Run 064 baseline (which had no minimum margin at all). **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 065; Run 065 does not touch timeout / NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle load-time activation-margin policy. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 065 closes only the Run 057 §10(a) / Run 058 §10(a) / Run 060 §10(a) / Run 061 §10 / Run 062 §10(c) / Run 063 §10(a) / Run 064 §10(a) "per-environment minimum activation margin" sub-piece on the load path; all other Run 050 / 051 / 052 / 054 / 055 / 056 / 057 / 058 / 059 / 060 / 061 / 062 / 063 / 064 §10 remaining items persist unchanged.
#### C4 Run 067 evidence update (2026-05-14) — live release-binary N=2 MainNet signed-bundle peer-connection smoke; multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection gap NARROWED for N=2 on the live binary; full C4 still OPEN

**What changed (Run 067).** ONE file under `crates/**/src/**` is touched — and only because it is the DevNet evidence-helper *example* binary, NOT in the `target/release/qbind-node` dependency graph: `crates/qbind-node/examples/devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper.rs`'s optional 5th positional `[activation_height_override]` now accepts the literal string `none` (case-insensitive) in addition to a decimal `u64`. `none` forces `bundle.activation_height = None` explicitly BEFORE signing and BEFORE the canonical fingerprint is computed (equivalent to omitting this positional when no later positional is needed). All previous helper behaviour is preserved bit-for-bit: a decimal `u64` continues to set `Some(<value>)`, an absent positional continues to leave `bundle.activation_height` at the `build_helper_bundle` default (`None`). This is the same evidence-tooling precedent as the existing Run 059 `chain_id_override` and Run 062 `revocation_activation_height_for_target` positionals, which already accept `none`. No new mode taxonomy, no new bundle field, no new signing semantics — the field is part of the signed preimage and canonical fingerprint exactly as `pqc_trust_bundle::canonical_signing_bytes` / `canonical_fingerprint` already include it. The release `qbind-node` binary identity is **bit-for-bit unchanged** before vs. after the Run 067 helper edit: `sha256(target/release/qbind-node) = 574709fbeec1fce106f10893d21fe5c0d4b1ac9d888518bf6bab064d46b94a30`, ELF BuildID `cc9c0663408f7abd6f3ac373f56a8a41da2802d0` (the helper is a separate example binary and is not in the release `qbind-node` dependency graph). The remaining new files are evidence artefacts: `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_067.md` (this row's evidence document), `docs/devnet/run_067_smoke_positive_v0.stdout.log` (V0 banner line), `docs/devnet/run_067_smoke_positive_v0.stderr.log` (V0 full startup banners + Run 050/051/053/055/057/062/063 banners + Run 037/039/040 PQC + `[binary-consensus] B9+B10: re-emitted view 0 BroadcastProposal + BroadcastVote after late peer connect (newly_connected_peers=1, …)` + `committed_anchor height=…` 226-line transcript), `docs/devnet/run_067_smoke_positive_v1.stdout.log` (V1 banner line), `docs/devnet/run_067_smoke_positive_v1.stderr.log` (V1 full startup banners + 227-line consensus transcript), `docs/devnet/run_067_metrics_positive_v0.txt` and `docs/devnet/run_067_metrics_positive_v1.txt` (both 21,582 bytes, HTTP 200, identical PQC / trust-bundle gauges & counters as listed above), and this row.

**Why `activation_height = None` is REQUIRED for the Run 067 positive smoke.** The Run 065 minimum-margin policy (`crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_activation.rs` lines 134/140/145: `MIN_DEVNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 0`, `MIN_TESTNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 8`, `MIN_MAINNET_ACTIVATION_MARGIN = 32`) rejects any in-window `bundle.activation_height = Some(h)` where `h ∈ [current_height, current_height + margin)` (line 688, half-open). On a fresh `--data-dir`, the binary's `current_height` source from `--restore-from-snapshot` is `Some(0)` (no snapshot ⇒ `ActivationContext::height_only(0)`), so the MainNet reject window is `[0, 32)`. The Run 065 snapshot-rejoin-preserved boundary (`activation_height < current_height = 0`) is unreachable. Therefore the only in-policy positive values for `bundle.activation_height` on a fresh MainNet data-dir are `>= 32`, but Run 057's future-height gate would then refuse to load the bundle as active. Conclusion: the only `bundle.activation_height` that lets a fresh-data-dir MainNet release-binary smoke load the bundle as active is **`None`**, and Run 065 §10(b) explicitly preserves this (the policy only inspects `Some(_)` values — line 691 wraps the bundle-level check inside `if let Some(act) = bundle.activation_height`). The Run 067 helper extension is the minimal evidence-tooling knob that lets the existing helper produce that exact bundle shape on the signed-MainNet code path while still pinning a non-default `chain_id_override = 0x51424e444d41494e` (positional argument 6).

**Anchoring (Run 067).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching pre-Run-067 evidence: Run 037 cert-verification path under `MutualAuthMode::Required` is anchored in `crates/qbind-net/src/handshake.rs::parse_and_verify_client_cert` and `crates/qbind-net/src/lib.rs::TrustedClientRoots::lookup_root_pk`, with the live test `run_037_pqc_static_root_mutual_auth_tests` 12/12 still passing in release profile and the live binary's `[Run040] dummy_kem_registered=false dummy_aead_registered=false` banner reproduced on both V0 and V1; Run 044 metric-adapter increments are anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs::pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total` / `pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total` and proven on the live binary by `qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_accepted_total = 2 qbind_p2p_pqc_cert_verify_rejected_total = 0` on BOTH `/metrics` scrapes (a successful Run 037 session under `MutualAuthMode::Required` fires the accepted counter once on the listener and once on the dialer per peer connection); **No-fallback proof (Run 067).** No `Cargo.toml` was touched; no new dependency was introduced; no feature flag was added; no `Dummy*` primitive was added, strengthened, or referenced anywhere except inside an explicit no-`Dummy*` claim (the `[Run040]` banner explicitly records `dummy_kem_registered=false dummy_aead_registered=false` on both live MainNet validators); no classical signature surface was introduced; no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (the helper banner records `signing_key_id=a0c7aa0e..` distinct from `root_id=333db244..`, and the binary load-path enforces trust-separation between transport-root ids and bundle-signing-key ids inside `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` lines 711–737); no protocol / wire-format / consensus / forged-traffic / KEMTLS change (no `crates/**/src/**.rs` file outside the helper example was touched; the release `qbind-node` binary sha256 / BuildID is unchanged). No existing test was modified or removed; the only Rust source change is the helper example's positional-argument acceptance widening, which strictly broadens — does not narrow — what the helper accepts on the *evidence-tooling* surface, and never on the binary surface. The bundle's `signature` envelope continues to be verified before any active-root merge happens (the live banner records `signature=verified(signing_key_id=a0c7aa0e..) signing_keys_configured=1` on both nodes); the binary refuses any unsigned MainNet bundle (Run 059 / 058 boundary preserved); the binary refuses any wrong-key or tampered MainNet bundle (Run 058 / 059 boundary preserved); the binary refuses any chain_id-mismatched bundle (Run 053 boundary preserved); the binary refuses any in-window MainNet `activation_height` and any revocation `activation_height` within the per-environment margin window (Run 065 boundary preserved, observable through `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_activation_rejected_total` remaining at zero in the positive smoke). No `--p2p-trusted-root` argument is supplied to either node, and the live banner records `signing_keys_configured=1` proving the trust set is built exclusively from the bundle's `roots[]` plus the configured `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`. No private-key bytes appear in any Run 067 artefact — the helper emits its banner with `root_sk` and `signing_sk` held in memory only ("root_sk and bundle signing_sk were held in memory only; never written to disk."), the `v{0,1}.kem.sk.bin` files have mode `0o600`, and no key bytes appear in the stderr/stdout/metrics logs. **No fabricated metric** (Run 067 introduces no metric at all; it reuses the existing Run 037 / 044 / 050 / 051 / 053 / 055 / 057 / 062 / 063 / 065 metric families exactly as defined in `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs`), **no silent regression** (every Run 050–066 §10 boundary preserved bit-for-bit; release binary identity unchanged), **no protocol behaviour change** (no `Cargo.toml`, no `crates/**/src/**.rs` outside the helper example, no KEMTLS wire-format change), **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no widening of any helper API surface to accept private-key material** (the only widened positional accepts `none` in addition to a decimal `u64` — both already public-data fields, and the field is already covered by the signed preimage / canonical fingerprint), and **no leak of `root_sk` / `signing_sk` / `kem_sk` / validator signer key bytes** were observed in the run.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 067).** (a) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064/065/066 boundary — bundle-level `activation_epoch` continues to fail closed with `TrustBundleActivationError::CurrentEpochUnavailable`; per-entry `activation_epoch` on revocations is intentionally NOT supported (Run 062 boundary). (b) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on the gossiped / peer-supplied trust-bundle path.** Unchanged from the Run 065 §10(a) / Run 066 §(b) boundary — Run 065 enforces the policy on the binary `--p2p-trust-bundle` load path; Run 067 does NOT add an on-the-fly distribution surface. (c) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload.** Unchanged — the bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime; Run 067's positive smoke does not rotate the bundle inside a running validator. (d) **In-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060/064/065/066 boundary; out-of-band CLI overlap remains the supported rotation path. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Per-environment production trust-anchor operation.** Unchanged — depends on the operator actually using offline / HSM custody for the secrets in `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` §3.2 / §3.4; the Run 067 helper continues to mint ephemeral DevNet keypairs in memory only and is suitable only for evidence-grade and DevNet smokes. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged — the `--restore-from-snapshot.snapshot_height` already feeds the Run 057 + Run 065 + Run 067 `current_height` source via `ActivationContext::height_only`; a fully-fledged production fast-sync surface is a separate boundary. (h) **N ≥ 4 multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Run 067 proves only `N = 2`. The Run 034 / Run 005 / Run 006 pattern of `N = 4` with one-validator restart for an analogous Required + pqc-static-root MainNet smoke is the operator's immediate-next action; it is not blocked by code, only by evidence-runtime time-budget. (i) **Live N = 2 MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke under leaf-revocation or root-revocation activation gates.** Run 067 deliberately exercises only the `(leaf-revocation = empty, root-revocation = empty)` shape; the Run 062 / 063 active/pending revocation smokes on the multi-validator MainNet path are a separate boundary. (j) **Validator consensus-key timeout-verification activation (Run 030/031/032/033/034/C5).** Unchanged from every previous PQC trust-bundle evidence run; this is a C5 boundary, not C4. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 067; Run 067 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle activation-margin / cert-verification surface already covered by Runs 037 / 044 / 050 / 051 / 055 / 057 / 065. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 067 narrows only the live-binary multi-validator MainNet peer-connection sub-piece (Run 059 §10(c) / Run 060–066 §10(f) / §10(b)) for `N = 2`; every other surviving Run 050/051/052/054/055/056/057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064/065/066 §10 remaining item persists unchanged.
