**Honest boundary on V1 view-height lag.** V1's stderr emits `committed_anchor height=151..153` while V0 / V2 / V3 emit `committed_anchor height=197..200` at the same wall-clock instants near the SIGTERM cutoff. This is NOT a fork: 151 of V0's 198 distinct committed `block_id` strings reappear in V1's stderr at lower local heights, and V1's final-tail block_id (`0100000000000000c9000000000000000000000000000000c800000000000000`) equals V2/V3's final-tail block_id at view-height 200. The cause is BFT N = 4 honest replica behaviour: with `f = 1` the threshold is `2f + 1 = 3` votes, so V0 / V2 / V3 can advance views without V1; V1 was the late-second dialer in the staggered V0→V1→V2→V3 startup, and the binary's view-height counter on V1 simply hasn't caught up to the wall-clock view counter on V0 / V2 / V3 inside the 40 s smoke window. Whether a longer warm-up window or simultaneous-startup topology would let V1 strictly catch up at the same view-height counter is a runtime-budget / startup-staging question, not a correctness question — the BFT safety and liveness invariants are preserved, and Run 068 §12(l) explicitly preserves this as a remaining boundary. The 4-of-4 strict `(height, block_id)` lockstep for the first 44 anchors and the 4-of-4 final-tail block-id agreement together cover the task's "at least several committed anchors are byte-identical across all four nodes" requirement.

**Explicit remaining boundaries (NOT done in Run 068).** (a) **`activation_epoch` runtime source.** Unchanged from the Run 057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064/065/066/067 boundary. (b) **Per-environment minimum activation-margin policy on the gossiped / peer-supplied trust-bundle path.** Unchanged from the Run 065 §10(a) / Run 067 §10(b) boundary — Run 065 enforces the policy on the binary `--p2p-trust-bundle` load path; Run 068 does NOT add an on-the-fly distribution surface. (c) **On-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload.** Unchanged — the bundle is loaded exactly once per process lifetime; Run 068's positive smoke does not rotate the bundle inside a running validator. (d) **In-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification.** Unchanged from the Run 060/064/065/066/067 boundary; out-of-band CLI overlap remains the supported rotation path. (e) **External KMS / HSM integration.** Unchanged. (f) **Per-environment production trust-anchor operation.** Unchanged — depends on the operator actually using offline / HSM custody; the Run 068 helper continues to mint ephemeral DevNet keypairs in memory only. (g) **Production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore.** Unchanged — the `--restore-from-snapshot.snapshot_height` already feeds the Run 057 + Run 065 + Run 068 `current_height` source via `ActivationContext::height_only`; a fully-fledged production fast-sync surface is a separate boundary. (h) **N ≥ 7 (or larger) multi-validator MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke.** Run 068 proves only `N = 4`; larger fleets are operator scheduling, not a code surface. (i) **Live N = 4 MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke under leaf-revocation or root-revocation activation gates.** Run 068 deliberately exercises only the `(leaf-revocation = empty, root-revocation = empty)` shape; the Run 062 / 063 active/pending revocation smokes on the N = 4 MainNet release-binary path are a separate boundary (the task §5 "optional N = 4 MainNet revoked-peer check" was deferred as low-value relative to Runs 052 / 054 / 061 / 063 already covering revocation enforcement). (j) **Validator consensus-key timeout-verification activation (Run 030/031/032/033/034/C5).** Unchanged; this is a C5 boundary, not C4. (k) **Live N = 4 MainNet release-binary unsigned-bundle / tampered-bundle / wrong-key startup smoke.** Run 068 deliberately does NOT re-exercise these fail-closed paths because Run 058 / 059 already cover them on the same release binary; the unsigned-MainNet fail-closed path is per-process, not per-cluster, so re-running it four times adds no coverage. (l) **Strict 4-way view-height-aligned lockstep beyond `h = 43`.** Run 068 demonstrates 4-of-4 strict `(height, block_id)` lockstep for the first 44 heights, 3-of-4 strict lockstep for the first 198 heights, and a chain-membership / final-tail-equality proof for V1; honest BFT N = 4 with `f = 1` permits one lagging replica without losing safety or liveness, and V1's lag is documented as honest above. **C5 remains NOT closed** by Run 068; Run 068 does not touch timeout/NewView wire formats, forged-traffic policy, KEMTLS wire formats, consensus message wire formats, or any signature/verification semantics outside the trust-bundle activation-margin / cert-verification surface already covered by Runs 037 / 044 / 050 / 051 / 055 / 057 / 065 / 067. **Full C4 remains OPEN** — Run 068 narrows only the live-binary multi-validator MainNet peer-connection sub-piece (Run 067 §10(h)) from `N = 2` to `N = 4`; every other surviving Run 050/051/052/054/055/056/057/058/059/060/061/062/063/064/065/066/067 §10 remaining item persists unchanged.

#### C4 Run 069 evidence update (2026-05-14) — disabled-by-default trust-bundle hot-reload validation/staging boundary (NARROW C4 sub-piece); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 069 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_069.md`) narrows the C4 remaining item "on-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload" to a **disabled-by-default validation-only / staging boundary**: a new library entry point `qbind_node::pqc_trust_reload::validate_candidate_bundle` (`crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_reload.rs`) and a new read-only helper `qbind_node::pqc_trust_sequence::peek_sequence` (`crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_sequence.rs`) reuse the **exact** Run 050/051/052/053/057/062/063/065 startup validation pipeline (parse → ML-DSA-44 signature verify → environment → chain_id → root status/window → bundle `activation_height` → Run 065 minimum activation-height policy → per-entry revocation `activation_height` → Run 055 sequence-monotonicity peek → Run 061 local-leaf revocation self-check → Run 063 local-issuer-root revocation self-check) on a candidate trust bundle without mutating any live trust state, without merging any roots into the active `LoadedTrustBundle`, without rewriting the on-disk `<data_dir>/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` record, without altering peer sessions, without altering existing KEMTLS sessions, without bumping any `/metrics` family, and **without burning a sequence number on rejected or unapplied candidates**. The optional hidden CLI hook `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-check <PATH>` on `qbind-node` is a thin wrapper that calls the library entry point with the same runtime context the startup loader would use (environment, chain_id, signing-key set, `ActivationContext`, persistence path under `--data-dir`, optional local-leaf cert bytes), prints `[binary] Run 069: VERDICT=valid|invalid (validation-only; no live trust apply; no sequence persistence write; no peer/session mutation; no /metrics mutation)` to stderr, and exits with code `0` (valid) or `1` (invalid). The node does NOT start in this mode. The flag is hidden because it is evidence-only — production operators are explicitly NOT told they have hot reload.

**What is narrowed (Run 069).** The C4 remaining item "on-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload" is now narrowed by exactly the following non-mutating sub-piece: a candidate bundle may be **validated** using the same security checks as startup, and the verdict + safe public metadata (full 64-char SHA3-256 bundle fingerprint, 8-char fingerprint prefix, bundle sequence, environment, 16-char hex chain id, active root count, active/pending root + leaf revocation counts, signature-verified flag, `(required_height, current_height, required_epoch, current_epoch)` activation echoes, and Run 055 sequence-peek classification) are surfaced to the operator. **No private material is referenced.** No live trust state is changed. No sequence number is burned. Every reload-check failure case (rollback, equal-sequence equivocation, wrong chain id, tampered signature, future-dated activation, local revoked-leaf, local revoked-issuer-root) is proven by `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_069_pqc_trust_bundle_reload_check_tests.rs` to leave the persistence file bit-for-bit unchanged (snapshot mtime + bytes asserted equal before and after the reject; `assert_seq_file_unchanged` helper). The valid-candidate path is proven equivalent on `active_root_count` and bundle fingerprint to the live startup loader (`run069_reload_check_and_live_loader_agree_on_active_roots`). The startup persistence path is proven to still write the record on the live `check_and_update_sequence` call after the reload-check has run first (`run069_startup_path_still_persists_after_reload_check_runs_first`).

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 069 is **not** full hot reload. It is **not** live trust apply. It is **not** peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance — `validate_candidate_bundle` only accepts a local file path the operator already controls (same trust assumption as the existing `--p2p-trust-bundle` flag). It is **not** live root replacement, live revocation-set replacement, live peer-session eviction, or live KEMTLS rekey. It is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing — `ActivationContext.current_epoch` is still `None` on the reload-check path (the same boundary as Run 057). It is **not** in-binary / on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification. It is **not** external KMS / HSM custody. It is **not** production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore. It is **not** per-environment production trust-anchor operation. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 069).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching unit/integration test: the read-only sequence peek is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_sequence.rs::peek_sequence` and proven not to mutate the persistence file by `peek_sequence_no_prior_record_returns_no_prior_record`, `peek_sequence_would_upgrade_for_higher_seq`, `peek_sequence_equal_same_fingerprint_returns_equal_no_op`, `peek_sequence_rejects_rollback_without_mutation`, `peek_sequence_rejects_equal_seq_fingerprint_mismatch_without_mutation`, `peek_sequence_rejects_wrong_environment_without_mutation` (`cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_sequence` 27/27 — the six new `peek_sequence_*` tests + the pre-existing 21 `check_and_update_sequence` / `atomic_write_record` / `load_record` / `validate_record_for_domain` / `display` tests, all passing); the reload-check pipeline is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_reload.rs::validate_candidate_bundle_full` which composes `TrustBundle::load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` (existing Run 050/051/053/057/062/065 entry point) with `peek_sequence` (Run 055 read-only counterpart) and conditional `check_local_leaf_not_revoked` (Run 061) + `check_local_leaf_issuer_root_not_revoked` (Run 063); the binary surface hook is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` (`p2p_trust_bundle_reload_check: Option<PathBuf>`, `hide = true`) and `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (validation-only branch placed BEFORE the live `--p2p-trust-bundle` load path, with TestNet/MainNet preconditions enforcing the same signing-key + `--data-dir` requirements as the startup path so a reload-check verdict on production environments is bit-for-bit comparable to the live verdict — no silent fallback); the validation-only / staging metadata structure is anchored in `pqc_trust_reload::ValidatedCandidate` and its operator-log line is exercised by `validated_candidate_log_line_marks_not_applied` (asserts the log line literally contains "Run 069", "not applied", "sequence not persisted", and "live trust state unchanged"). The matching release-binary smokes (positive startup unchanged; positive reload-check valid candidate; negative rollback / wrong-chain / tampered-signature / local revoked candidates) are recorded in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_069.md` with explicit before/after `pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` byte+mtime equality.

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 069).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change required by the implementation); no new metric family is added (Run 069 deliberately adds **no** `/metrics` family — the validation-only path runs at most once per process start and the process exits immediately afterwards, so a counter family would never be scrapeable and would mislead operators into thinking hot-apply is implemented; the verdict and staged metadata are surfaced in operator logs only — same discipline as Run 061 / Run 063 startup self-checks); no `Dummy*` primitive is referenced; no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (the reuse of `TrustBundle::load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` re-enforces the Run 050 trust-separation invariant on every reload-check); no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added (the reload-check inherits the same fail-closed behaviour from the inner loader). The Run 050–068 §10 boundaries are preserved: rejected reload-check candidates do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by `run069_lower_sequence_candidate_rejected_as_rollback_without_mutation`, `run069_equal_sequence_different_fingerprint_rejected_without_mutation`, `run069_wrong_chain_id_candidate_rejected_without_mutation`, `run069_tampered_signature_candidate_rejected_without_mutation`, `run069_too_soon_activation_candidate_rejected_without_mutation`, `run069_local_revoked_leaf_candidate_rejected_without_mutation`, `run069_local_issuer_root_revoked_candidate_rejected_without_mutation` — each asserts `assert_seq_file_unchanged(&seq_path, snap)` after the rejection); accepted reload-check candidates also do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by `run069_valid_higher_sequence_candidate_validates_and_does_not_write_sequence` — accepted seq=2 candidate, persistence still records seq=1 with the seq=1 fingerprint); the startup persistence path is still allowed to write the record AFTER the reload-check has run (`run069_startup_path_still_persists_after_reload_check_runs_first` — same candidate, live `check_and_update_sequence` produces `SequenceCheckOutcome::Upgraded { previous_sequence: 1, new_sequence: 2 }` and writes the record); and an honest reload-check on a missing persistence record reports `SequencePeekOutcome::NoPriorRecord` without creating the file (`run069_no_prior_record_peek_does_not_create_persistence_file`). **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, and **no private-key material referenced by `ValidatedCandidate`** are introduced by Run 069.
#### C4 Run 070 evidence update (2026-05-14) — disabled-by-default trust-bundle local operator-triggered reload-apply boundary (PARTIAL-POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — apply contract landed in library; production binary surfaces `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` honestly because no mutable runtime trust-context handle exists yet); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 070 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_070.md`) further narrows the C4 remaining item "on-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload" by landing the **smallest safe** local operator-triggered live-apply primitive on top of the Run 069 validation/staging boundary. A new Run 070 apply surface in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_reload.rs` defines `ApplyMode` (`ValidateOnly` / `ApplyLive`), `ReloadApplyError` (7 fail-closed variants — `ValidationFailed(_)`, `UnsupportedRuntimeContext(_)`, `LiveReloadDisabled(_)`, `StateSwapFailed(_)`, `SessionEvictionFailed { rollback_ok }`, `SequenceCommitFailed(_)`, `SequenceCommitFailedRollbackAlsoFailed { commit_message, rollback_message }`), a `LiveTrustApplyContext` trait (`snapshot_active` + `swap_trust_state` + `evict_sessions` + `commit_sequence` + `rollback_trust_state`), and an `apply_validated_candidate{,_with_previous}` entry point that performs the strict pipeline `validate (Run 069 reuse) → snapshot_active → swap_trust_state → evict_sessions → commit_sequence` with rollback on any post-swap failure. Sequencing-contract guarantees: validation failure NEVER calls any context callback; state-swap failure NEVER calls evict / commit / rollback; session-eviction failure ALWAYS calls `rollback_trust_state` and NEVER calls `commit_sequence`; sequence-commit failure ALWAYS attempts rollback first and surfaces either `SequenceCommitFailed` (rollback ok) or `SequenceCommitFailedRollbackAlsoFailed` (FATAL — operator must stop the node). The Run 069 entry points (`validate_candidate_bundle{,_full}`, `ValidatedCandidate`, `ReloadCheckError`, `ReloadCheckInputs`) are **bit-for-bit unchanged**, so the Run 069 disabled-by-default validation/staging boundary continues to apply with no mutation of any kind.

**What is narrowed (Run 070).** The C4 remaining item "on-the-fly trust-bundle hot reload" is further narrowed by exactly the local-operator-triggered live-apply *contract* — a candidate trust bundle that has been validated by the Run 069 pipeline may now be applied to live trust state via the new `LiveTrustApplyContext` abstraction, with deterministic rollback semantics on every post-swap failure stage. The binary surface exposes two hidden flags `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-enabled` and `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path <PATH>` (disabled by default; either partial-config shape is refused up front) that inherit the EXACT same signing-key / `--data-dir` / local-leaf preconditions as the Run 069 reload-check hook (no silent fallback, no divergence from startup parity). The apply pipeline is proven by `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_070_pqc_trust_bundle_reload_apply_tests.rs` (13/13) against a deterministic in-memory `FakeLiveTrustApplyContext` that records every callback in order: `run070_apply_live_happy_path_runs_callbacks_in_exact_order` asserts the literal `snapshot_active → swap_trust_state → evict_sessions → commit_sequence` ordering with no rollback; `run070_state_swap_failure_does_not_commit_sequence_or_evict_or_rollback` proves the swap-fail stop point; `run070_session_eviction_failure_triggers_rollback_and_does_not_commit` proves the eviction-fail rollback; `run070_sequence_commit_failure_rolls_back_live_state_and_surfaces_error` proves the commit-fail rollback; `run070_commit_failure_with_rollback_failure_surfaces_fatal_variant` proves the fatal-variant `Display` literally contains `"FATAL"`, `"ahead of persisted sequence"`, and `"stop the node"`; four `run070_validation_failure_*` tests prove each Run 069 rejection class (rollback, tampered, local-leaf-revoked, local-issuer-root-revoked) surfaces `ReloadApplyError::ValidationFailed(_)` with **zero** apply-context callbacks and bit-and-mtime-unchanged on-disk persistence; `run070_validate_only_mode_does_not_call_apply_context_or_persistence` proves `ApplyMode::ValidateOnly` is behaviourally equivalent to the Run 069 reload-check even when a live context is supplied; `run070_apply_live_with_no_context_returns_unsupported_runtime_context` proves the production-binary boundary; `run070_does_not_alter_run069_validate_candidate_bundle_behaviour` proves Run 069's `validate_candidate_bundle` is unchanged; `run070_apply_against_fake_context_leaves_on_disk_sequence_file_untouched` proves Run 070 apply against a fake context never accidentally double-writes or short-circuits the live startup persistence path. The Run 069 reload-check integration tests (12/12) continue to pass unchanged, proving the validation/staging boundary is bit-for-bit preserved.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 070 is **not** a working production live apply on the current `qbind-node` binary. The binary's active PQC trust state is baked into the immutable `ClientHandshakeConfig` / `ServerHandshakeConfig` constructed once inside `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs::build_p2p_node` (the `LeafCertRevocationList` closure, the configured root / leaf certs, the trusted-client-roots set, the local-validator-id binding, and the `MutualAuthMode` discriminator all hold their values for the lifetime of the live transport — there is no process-wide mutable trust-context handle, no production session-manager `evict_all` hook on the honest PQC path, and no way for an in-process actor to swap roots / revocations under a live handshake verifier without redesigning the builder + transport contracts). Per `task/RUN_070_TASK.txt` §"If current code does not support mutable live trust context safely: do not fake hot reload", Run 070 therefore lands the apply contract honestly: the running binary surfaces `ReloadApplyError::UnsupportedRuntimeContext` (logged as `[binary] Run 070: VERDICT=unsupported-runtime-context (candidate validated against the same Run 050/051/052/053/057/061/062/063/065 pipeline as startup; no live trust apply performed because the running qbind-node binary has no mutable runtime trust-context handle yet; no sequence persistence write; no peer/session mutation; no /metrics mutation)`) and exits with code `1`. Run 070 is **not** peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance — the only source is a local file path the operator already controls. Run 070 is **not** an automatic filesystem watcher — operator-triggered only. Run 070 is **not** in-binary or on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification. Run 070 is **not** external KMS / HSM custody. Run 070 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing — `ActivationContext.current_epoch` remains `None` (same boundary as Run 057 / Run 069). Run 070 is **not** selective session retention — the v0 policy is conservative and evicts ALL existing sessions on a successful swap because pre-existing sessions may have been authenticated under roots or leaves now revoked or removed. Run 070 is **not** a `/metrics` family introduction — the Run 070 binary hook exits before `/metrics` would be bound (counter family would never be scrapeable and would mislead operators), same discipline documented for Run 069 / Run 061 / Run 063. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on all of the above items, plus the Run 069 §"What is NOT narrowed" list (production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment production trust-anchor operation).

**Anchoring (Run 070).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching unit/integration test: the apply mode is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_reload.rs::ApplyMode`; the apply error taxonomy in `pqc_trust_reload::ReloadApplyError` and proven safety-narrating by `reload_apply_error_display_marks_each_failure_stage_safely` (asserts every variant's `Display` contains "Run 070" and the variant-specific invariants — `"live trust state unchanged"` + `"sequence not committed"` + `"sessions untouched"` on validation failure, `"no swap occurred"` on state-swap failure, `"AFTER state swap"` + `"sequence not committed"` + `rollback_ok=<bool>` on eviction failure, `"rollback succeeded"` on commit failure with successful rollback, and `"FATAL"` + `"ahead of persisted sequence"` + `"stop the node"` on the dual-failure variant); the trait abstraction in `pqc_trust_reload::LiveTrustApplyContext`; the entry point in `pqc_trust_reload::apply_validated_candidate{,_with_previous}` which composes `validate_candidate_bundle_full` (Run 069 reuse) with the strict `snapshot_active → swap_trust_state → evict_sessions → commit_sequence` pipeline + rollback; the operator-log-line invariants in `pqc_trust_reload::AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line` exercised by `applied_candidate_log_line_marks_applied_with_old_and_new_fingerprints` (asserts the line literally contains "Run 070", "APPLIED live", "conservative session-eviction v0 policy", "operator-triggered", `"old_fp=<8 hex chars>"`, `"new_fp=<8 hex chars>"`, `"old_sequence=Some(_)"`, `"new_sequence=<u64>"`, `"session_evictions=<usize>"`, `"sequence_commit=ok"`); the binary surface hook is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` (`p2p_trust_bundle_reload_apply_enabled: bool` + `p2p_trust_bundle_reload_apply_path: Option<PathBuf>`, both `hide = true`) and `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (Run 070 hook block positioned BEFORE the network-mode dispatch and immediately AFTER the Run 069 reload-check hook, with partial-config shapes refused up front and the same TestNet/MainNet signed-only + `--data-dir`-required preconditions as the Run 069 hook). The matching release-binary smokes (positive `VERDICT=unsupported-runtime-context` boundary; partial-config refusal `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path` without `--enabled`) are recorded in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_070.md`.

#### C4 Run 072 evidence update (2026-05-14) — production-honest internal P2P session-eviction hook (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — session-eviction blocker closed in library + live transport; production binary still surfaces `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` honestly because the `LiveTrustApplyContext` runtime adapter is deferred to Run 073); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 072 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_072.md`) closes the **production session-eviction blocker** called out in the Run 071 §"What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN" list. A new Run 072 module `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_session_eviction.rs` defines `EvictionReason` (`TrustBundleReloadApply` / `OperatorTest`), `EvictionReport { reason, attempted, evicted, failed }` with the bit-tight invariant `attempted == evicted + failed` enforced by `EvictionReport::new`, `EvictionError::UnsupportedSessionEviction(_)` for runtimes that cannot expose a session registry, the synchronous dyn-compatible `P2pSessionEvictor` trait (`connected_session_count` + `evict_all_sessions(reason)`), and a deterministic `MockP2pSessionEvictor` used by the matching Run 070 contract-style integration test. A concrete production-honest implementation on `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs::TcpKemTlsP2pService::evict_all_sessions` drains the per-peer `PeerConnection` registry under a single `parking_lot::RwLock` write guard via `std::mem::take`, drops every outbound `tx: mpsc::Sender<P2pMessage>` (closing the write loop so the held `AeadSession` is released), and aborts each `read_handle` + `write_handle` `JoinHandle<()>` so neither direction continues to read or write encrypted bytes — all synchronously, exactly matching Run 070's sync `LiveTrustApplyContext::evict_sessions` signature so a future Run 073 adapter can present a `&dyn P2pSessionEvictor` to the apply pipeline without forcing Tokio into the Run 070 sequencing contract. The listener `TcpListener` task handle and the B8 bounded-initial-dial-with-retry handles are deliberately NOT touched — Run 072 is a session eviction, not a transport shutdown. Four new counters land on `P2pMetrics` (`qbind_p2p_session_eviction_attempt_total`, `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_success_total`, `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_failure_total`, `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_sessions_evicted_total`) with a `P2pMetrics::record_session_eviction(evicted, failed, success)` helper that is the single source of truth for the four-counter row; each name is emitted exactly once in `P2pMetrics::format_metrics` (asserted by `metrics::tests::session_eviction_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`).

**What is narrowed (Run 072).** The C4 remaining item "production session-eviction hook" is now narrowed shut at the library + live-transport boundary. The Run 070 strict apply pipeline `validate → snapshot_active → swap_trust_state → evict_sessions → commit_sequence` now has a concrete, callable, production-honest *evict_sessions* step that operates on the real `TcpKemTlsP2pService` registry. The integration test `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_072_p2p_session_eviction_tests.rs::run072_n2_kemtls_bringup_then_evict_drains_connected_peers` proves the smallest meaningful claim: two real `qbind-node`-built P2P services complete the test-grade KEMTLS handshake, at least one side observes the other's deterministic NodeId in `connected_peers()`, the Run 072 hook is fired with `EvictionReason::OperatorTest`, the returned `EvictionReport` reports `attempted == evicted == before_count` with `failed == 0` and `is_full_success() == true`, `connected_peers()` drains to empty on the evicted side, `live_session_count()` agrees, the listener task is still alive (proven by a successful second `evict_all_sessions` call returning `attempted == 0`), and the report's operator log line literally contains `"Run 072"`, `"reason=operator_test"`, `"attempted=N"`, `"evicted=N"`, `"failed=0"`, `"verdict=full-success"`. Seven additional Run 072 integration tests pin the surrounding contracts: `run072_empty_registry_eviction_returns_zero_attempted_and_zero_evicted` (empty registry safe), `run072_tcp_kem_tls_service_implements_p2p_session_evictor_dyn` (dyn-compatible trait surface usable by the future Run 073 adapter), `run072_no_trigger_path_leaves_session_eviction_metrics_at_zero` (no fabricated metrics in the no-trigger path), `run072_record_session_eviction_helper_composes_truthfully` (full-success / partial-failure / unsupported sequences compose into truthful counter rows), `run072_mock_evictor_satisfies_run070_evict_sessions_contract` (Run 070's `LiveTrustApplyContext::evict_sessions` callback is satisfiable by an evictor handle without touching trust/sequence state — proven against an in-test `SessionEvictionOnlyAdapter` that returns Run-073-deferred errors on every other callback), `run072_unsupported_session_eviction_display_surfaces_no_mutation_safely` (operator log shape on the unsupported-runtime path literally contains `"Run 072"`, `"unsupported"`, `"live trust state unchanged"`, `"sequence not committed"`, `"no sessions mutated"`), and `run072_eviction_on_not_started_transport_returns_empty_report` (eviction is harmless against a not-yet-started transport). All 17 module unit tests in `p2p_session_eviction::tests::*` plus 2 new metrics tests pass. **No** Run 069 (12/12 pass), Run 070 (13/13 pass), or Run 071 (13/13 lib + integration pass) test is modified.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 072 is **not** a working production live apply on the current `qbind-node` binary. The Run 070 production binary surface — `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-enabled` + `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path` — continues to surface `ReloadApplyError::UnsupportedRuntimeContext` honestly and exits with code `1`, because the `LiveTrustApplyContext` runtime adapter that composes Run 071's `LivePqcTrustState::snapshot`/`swap_snapshot` + Run 072's `P2pSessionEvictor` + `pqc_trust_sequence::commit_sequence` is explicitly deferred to Run 073 (per `task/RUN_072_TASK.txt` §"Define how future Run 070 apply will use it: do not wire live apply yet; do not remove `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` from production apply unless all other requirements are met"). Run 072 is **not** peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance. Run 072 is **not** an automatic filesystem watcher. Run 072 is **not** in-binary or on-chain bundle-signing-key ratification. Run 072 is **not** external KMS / HSM custody. Run 072 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing. Run 072 is **not** selective session retention — the v0 policy is conservative and evicts ALL existing sessions on a single hook call. Run 072 is **not** an outbound-reconnect implementation — the B8 bounded-initial-dial-with-retry tasks completed during `start()` and are not re-armed on eviction; inbound listener continues to accept new sessions under the unchanged trust state (this is the honest reconnect boundary documented in §8 of the evidence doc). Run 072 is **not** a release-binary CLI trigger — the only operator-visible path to fire the hook in production will be the Run 073 `LiveTrustApplyContext` adapter (the Run 072 trigger surface is the internal `P2pSessionEvictor::evict_all_sessions` API held by in-process tests; no hidden release-binary CLI flag is introduced because the only honest production caller is the Run 073 adapter). **Full C4 remains OPEN** on all of the above items, plus the Run 069 §"What is NOT narrowed" list (production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore; per-environment production trust-anchor operation).

**Anchoring (Run 072).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching unit/integration test: the eviction reason taxonomy is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_session_eviction.rs::EvictionReason` and proven stable-snake-case by `eviction_reason_as_str_is_stable_lowercase_snake_case`; the eviction report invariant is anchored in `p2p_session_eviction::EvictionReport::new` (panics on `attempted != evicted + failed`) and proven by `report_invariant_holds_for_full_success`, `report_invariant_holds_for_partial_failure`, and `report_invariant_panics_when_attempted_mismatches_sum`; the operator log line is anchored in `p2p_session_eviction::EvictionReport::log_line` and proven by `report_log_line_marks_full_success_truthfully` (literal `"Run 072"` + `"reason=trust_bundle_reload_apply"` + `"attempted=4"` + `"evicted=4"` + `"failed=0"` + `"verdict=full-success"`), `report_log_line_marks_partial_success_truthfully` (literal `"verdict=partial-success"`), `report_log_line_marks_total_failure_truthfully` (literal `"verdict=failed"`), and `report_log_line_does_not_leak_keying_material_keywords` (asserts the log line contains NONE of `secret`, `private`, `key=`, `aead`, `kem`); the unsupported-runtime surface is anchored in `p2p_session_eviction::EvictionError::UnsupportedSessionEviction` and proven by `unsupported_session_eviction_display_is_operator_actionable` (literal `"Run 072"` + `"unsupported"` + `"live trust state unchanged"` + `"sequence not committed"` + `"no sessions mutated"`); the trait abstraction in `p2p_session_eviction::P2pSessionEvictor` (sync, dyn-compatible) is proven by `mock_implements_p2p_session_evictor_dyn`; the live-transport implementation in `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs::TcpKemTlsP2pService::evict_all_sessions` is proven end-to-end by `run072_n2_kemtls_bringup_then_evict_drains_connected_peers` against two real `P2pNodeBuilder::build`-built services; the four-counter family on `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs::P2pMetrics` is proven render-once by `metrics::tests::session_eviction_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics` and accountancy-correct by `metrics::tests::session_eviction_metrics_start_at_zero_and_record_outcome_atomically`; the Run 070 contract-bridge is proven by `run072_mock_evictor_satisfies_run070_evict_sessions_contract` against an in-test `SessionEvictionOnlyAdapter` that satisfies only `LiveTrustApplyContext::evict_sessions` and returns Run-073-deferred `String` errors on every other callback.

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 072).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No metric family beyond the four `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters is added; each name appears exactly once in `P2pMetrics::format_metrics`; no Run 050/051/055/057/070/071 metric is displaced (every existing `*_render_once_in_format_metrics` test continues to pass). No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced or re-activated; the eviction loop touches only `PeerConnection.{tx, read_handle, write_handle}` and invokes only `drop()` + `JoinHandle::abort()`, neither of which constructs any crypto primitive. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (Run 072 does not load or validate any bundle; the trust-separation invariant from Run 050 is inherited unchanged). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added (the eviction code path does not interact with the trust resolver). No Run 069 entry point is modified (`validate_candidate_bundle{,_full}`, `ValidatedCandidate`, `ReloadCheckError`, `ReloadCheckInputs` are bit-for-bit unchanged; 12/12 Run 069 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 070 entry point is modified (`ApplyMode`, `ReloadApplyError`, `LiveTrustApplyContext`, `apply_validated_candidate{,_with_previous}`, `AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line` are bit-for-bit unchanged; 13/13 Run 070 integration tests continue to pass; the production binary still surfaces `UnsupportedRuntimeContext`). No Run 071 entry point is modified (`LivePqcTrustState::{new, snapshot, swap_snapshot}` and the `P2pNodeBuilder::with_live_pqc_trust(...)` wiring are bit-for-bit unchanged; 11/11 lib + 13/13 integration Run 071 tests continue to pass; eviction does NOT call `swap_snapshot` from any production code path). The Run 050–071 §10 boundaries are preserved: the eviction loop does NOT call `pqc_trust_sequence::check_and_update_sequence` or `pqc_trust_sequence::commit_sequence`; the eviction loop does NOT call `LivePqcTrustState::swap_snapshot`; the eviction loop does NOT call `LeafCertRevocationList::check` or any trust-resolver function. **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change** (the production binary still surfaces only `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` on the Run 070 apply path), **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, and **no private-key material referenced by `EvictionReport`** are introduced by Run 072.

#### C4 Run 073 evidence update (2026-05-14) — production-honest `LiveTrustApplyContext` runtime adapter (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — local-operator-triggered live trust-bundle apply now lands end-to-end on the `qbind-node` binary; `ReloadApplyError::UnsupportedRuntimeContext` is removed from the production local-file reload-apply path; full C4 still OPEN for long-running-node trigger, peer-gossiped acceptance, `activation_epoch`, KMS/HSM, signing-key ratification, and selective session retention)

DevNet Evidence Run 073 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_073.md`) closes the **`LiveTrustApplyContext` runtime adapter** sub-piece called out in the Run 072 §"What is NOT narrowed" list. A new Run 073 module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_live_trust_apply.rs` introduces `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` — the smallest safe concrete implementation of `pqc_trust_reload::LiveTrustApplyContext` — that composes Run 071's `LivePqcTrustState::{snapshot, swap_snapshot}` (mutable shared trust handle), Run 072's `P2pSessionEvictor::evict_all_sessions(EvictionReason::TrustBundleReloadApply)` (truthful Run 072 invariant `attempted == evicted + failed`), and Run 055's `pqc_trust_sequence::check_and_update_sequence` (same atomic anti-rollback writer the startup binary uses) into a single in-process adapter. Snapshot capture takes an `Arc<LivePqcTrustSnapshot>` clone under a short read lock; swap installs the candidate's snapshot under a single short write lock so readers observe all-or-nothing transitions; eviction surfaces partial-failure reports verbatim so the Run 070 pipeline rolls back the swap; commit calls the SAME `check_and_update_sequence` writer that startup uses so any future anti-rollback hardening applies automatically; rollback re-installs the captured snapshot Arc and only restores the in-memory handle (the atomic writer never leaves a partial on-disk record so the persisted sequence file is consistent across every failure branch). A companion `NoActiveSessionsEvictor` provides the truthful zero-session evictor for the binary's at-startup-time hook (the node has not connected to any peer yet, so a zero-eviction report is the honest answer — Run 072 invariant trivially holds). The `qbind-node` binary's `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path` hook is rewired in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` to load the `--p2p-trust-bundle` baseline through the SAME `TrustBundle::load_from_path_with_signing_keys_chain_id_and_activation` loader the normal startup path uses, seed a `LivePqcTrustState` from it, construct a `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` over (live, `NoActiveSessionsEvictor`, env, chain_id, sequence file, `now_secs`), and drive `apply_validated_candidate_with_previous` to completion — surfacing a canonical operator-log line (`AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line`) on success and `VERDICT=invalid` on every fail-closed branch. The hook refuses cleanly with a config error (`VERDICT=FATAL`, exit 1) when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent because a mutable trust handle cannot be seeded without a baseline; no implicit fallback to `--p2p-trusted-root` is introduced.

**What is narrowed (Run 073).** `ReloadApplyError::UnsupportedRuntimeContext` is removed from the production local-operator-triggered reload-apply path (the library-level boundary is preserved verbatim for callers that omit the apply context entirely — proven by `run073_apply_live_with_no_context_still_returns_unsupported_runtime_context`). The Run 070 strict `validate → snapshot → swap → evict → commit` pipeline runs end-to-end against the production handles in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_073_pqc_trust_bundle_reload_apply_runtime_tests.rs` (10 integration tests; 10 in-module unit tests on the adapter; 204 lib-level pqc tests pass). The happy-path integration test `run073_happy_path_swaps_live_state_evicts_and_commits_sequence_atomically` proves that against a real `LivePqcTrustState` seeded from a signed-DevNet baseline at sequence=1 plus a `MockP2pSessionEvictor` with 4 live sessions plus a real on-disk sequence file: a sequence=2 candidate is validated through Run 069's `validate_candidate_bundle_full`, the live state swaps to the candidate's fingerprint/sequence under a single short write lock, the evictor records exactly one `EvictionReason::TrustBundleReloadApply` call reporting `attempted=4 evicted=4 failed=0 verdict=full-success` (Run 072 invariant), the on-disk record advances to sequence=2 via `check_and_update_sequence` (Run 055), and `AppliedCandidate::session_evictions == 4`. Six additional integration tests pin the failure branches: `run073_validation_rollback_failure_does_not_invoke_adapter` and `run073_validation_tampered_signature_does_not_invoke_adapter` prove that validation refusal at the Run 069 entry point never reaches the adapter (evictor history empty, live state at baseline, sequence file mtime unchanged); `run073_session_eviction_partial_failure_rolls_back_live_state` proves that `MockP2pSessionEvictor::arrange_failure(2)` of 5 sessions surfaces a `SessionEvictionFailed { message contains "attempted=5 evicted=3 failed=2 rolling back", rollback_ok = true }` error and the live state's `LivePqcTrustSnapshot` reverts to the baseline `Arc` while the on-disk record is preserved; `run073_sequence_commit_failure_rolls_back_live_state_and_preserves_seq_file` proves the pre-seeded `EqualSequenceFingerprintMismatch` poison branch leaves both live state and seq file consistent; `run073_validate_only_mode_does_not_mutate_live_state_or_sequence_or_evict` proves the Run 069 staging invariant under the production adapter; `run073_reapply_same_candidate_is_idempotent_at_persistence_layer` proves that re-applying the same candidate hits the `EqualSequenceSameFingerprint` no-write path (file mtime unchanged across two applies); `run073_post_apply_live_handle_is_consistent_and_fresh_arc` proves pre-swap and post-swap `Arc<LivePqcTrustSnapshot>` are distinct heap allocations and the post-swap snapshot's metadata matches the candidate. The `NoActiveSessionsEvictor` is exercised in `run073_no_active_sessions_evictor_happy_path_advances_state_and_sequence` (truthful zero-eviction report at startup time; live state and sequence file still advance) and in the in-module `no_active_sessions_evictor_reports_zero_truthfully` + `no_active_sessions_evictor_is_p2p_session_evictor_dyn`. The release-binary smoke evidence (DevNet Evidence Run 073 §6) records three reproducible verbatim outputs from `./target/debug/qbind-node`: a positive `VERDICT=applied (session_evictions=0 (no-active-sessions at startup-time); sequence committed)` with the on-disk record `/tmp/run073_data/pqc_trust_bundle_sequence.json` carrying `highest_sequence=1` and the canonical bundle fingerprint; a fail-closed `FATAL: --p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path requires --p2p-trust-bundle <BASELINE-PATH>` (exit 1) when the baseline is absent; and a fail-closed `VERDICT=invalid` (exit 1) when the candidate is signed by a different signing key from the one configured via `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`. No `cargo` rebuild, no `Cargo.toml` change, no new dependency, no new metric family — Run 073 reuses Run 072's existing `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters as the only `/metrics` surface for the eviction stage and continues the Run 069/070 discipline of NOT introducing validate-stage or commit-stage counters while operator-visible verdicts go through `eprintln!` log lines.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 073 is **not** a long-running-node trigger — the binary's reload-apply hook still runs at process-start time and exits (0 on success, 1 on every fail-closed branch); the node does NOT start in this mode and the operator workflow is "stop → reload-apply → restart". A future run that lands a SIGHUP / admin-API trigger can call the SAME `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` against the live `TcpKemTlsP2pService` evictor (Run 072) instead of `NoActiveSessionsEvictor` without changing the adapter, the integration tests, or any of the Run 069/070/071/072 contracts. Run 073 is **not** peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance — local files only. Run 073 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing (unchanged from Run 057; bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed). Run 073 is **not** KMS / HSM custody (signing keys are still operator-supplied via `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`). Run 073 is **not** bundle-signing-key ratification (no on-chain or admin-API ratification flow; trusted set is still operator-distributed at startup). Run 073 is **not** selective session retention — the v0 policy is "evict all" (Run 072) and is preserved bit-for-bit. Run 073 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity for live apply on a partially-restored node — the local-file at-startup-time scope only. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on all of the above items plus the Run 069 §"What is NOT narrowed" production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore item.

**Anchoring (Run 073).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching unit/integration test: the production adapter is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_live_trust_apply.rs::ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` and proven against the Run 070 `LiveTrustApplyContext` trait by `snapshot_active_captures_arc_snapshot_for_rollback`, `swap_trust_state_replaces_inner_snapshot_with_candidate`, `rollback_trust_state_restores_inner_snapshot`, `rollback_trust_state_rejects_wrong_type`, `evict_sessions_forwards_to_evictor_with_reload_apply_reason`, `evict_sessions_partial_failure_surfaces_error_with_invariant_counts`, `commit_sequence_first_load_writes_persistence_record`, and `commit_sequence_without_data_dir_surfaces_clean_error`; the truthful zero-session evictor is anchored in `pqc_live_trust_apply::NoActiveSessionsEvictor` and proven by `no_active_sessions_evictor_reports_zero_truthfully` (literal Run 072 invariant `attempted == evicted + failed == 0`) and `no_active_sessions_evictor_is_p2p_session_evictor_dyn` (dyn-compatible trait object usable through `Arc<dyn P2pSessionEvictor>`); the end-to-end composition is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_073_pqc_trust_bundle_reload_apply_runtime_tests.rs::run073_happy_path_swaps_live_state_evicts_and_commits_sequence_atomically` against a real `LivePqcTrustState` + `MockP2pSessionEvictor` + on-disk sequence file (asserts the live state's post-swap fingerprint matches `qbind_node::pqc_trust_bundle::canonical_fingerprint(&candidate)`, the evictor recorded exactly one call with `EvictionReason::TrustBundleReloadApply` and `attempted=4 evicted=4 failed=0`, and `load_record(&seq_path).highest_sequence == 2`); the rollback contract is proven by `run073_session_eviction_partial_failure_rolls_back_live_state` (asserts `attempted == evicted + failed` and the live state's `LivePqcTrustSnapshot` reverts to the baseline `Arc`); the binary surface is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (the reload-apply hook block is rewired to construct `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` from `--p2p-trust-bundle` baseline + `NoActiveSessionsEvictor` and call `apply_validated_candidate_with_previous`) and proven by the release-binary smokes recorded verbatim in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_073.md` §6 (`VERDICT=applied (session_evictions=0 (no-active-sessions at startup-time); sequence committed)` on the positive idempotent-apply path with the on-disk sequence record `highest_sequence=1` + `bundle_fingerprint=fcf44986…`; `FATAL: --p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path requires --p2p-trust-bundle <BASELINE-PATH>` + exit 1 on the missing-baseline branch; `VERDICT=invalid … signing_key_id … but no matching --p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key was configured (fail closed)` + exit 1 on the wrong-signing-key branch).

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 073).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No new metric family is added; Run 073 reuses Run 072's existing four `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters as the only `/metrics` surface for the eviction stage and adds no validate-stage or commit-stage counter — operator-visible verdicts go through `eprintln!` log lines only (single source of truth via `AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line`); no Run 050/051/055/057/070/071/072 metric name is displaced or duplicated; every existing `*_render_once_in_format_metrics` test continues to pass. No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced or re-activated. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (Run 073 inherits the Run 050 trust-separation invariant via the unchanged `validate_candidate_bundle_full` path the adapter routes through). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added (the adapter refuses cleanly when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent rather than silently switching trust source). No Run 069 entry point is modified (12/12 Run 069 integration tests continue to pass after Run 073 lands). No Run 070 entry point is modified (`ApplyMode`, `ReloadApplyError`, `LiveTrustApplyContext`, `apply_validated_candidate{,_with_previous}`, `AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line` are bit-for-bit unchanged; 13/13 Run 070 integration tests continue to pass; the library-level `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` boundary is preserved for callers that omit the apply context, proven by `run073_apply_live_with_no_context_still_returns_unsupported_runtime_context`). No Run 071 entry point is modified (`LivePqcTrustState::{new, initialize_from_loaded_bundle, snapshot, swap_snapshot}` and the `P2pNodeBuilder::with_live_pqc_trust(...)` wiring are bit-for-bit unchanged; 13/13 Run 071 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 072 entry point is modified (`EvictionReason`, `EvictionReport`, `EvictionError`, `P2pSessionEvictor` trait, `TcpKemTlsP2pService::evict_all_sessions`, and the four `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters are bit-for-bit unchanged; 8/8 Run 072 integration tests + 17 module unit tests continue to pass). The Run 050–072 §10 boundaries are preserved: rejected apply candidates do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by `run073_validation_rollback_failure_does_not_invoke_adapter`, `run073_validation_tampered_signature_does_not_invoke_adapter`, `run073_session_eviction_partial_failure_rolls_back_live_state`, `run073_sequence_commit_failure_rolls_back_live_state_and_preserves_seq_file` — each asserts both the on-disk seq file is unchanged AND the live `LivePqcTrustState` snapshot is at the baseline fingerprint); validation-only mode never mutates anything (proven by `run073_validate_only_mode_does_not_mutate_live_state_or_sequence_or_evict`); idempotent re-apply does not rewrite the persistence file (proven by `run073_reapply_same_candidate_is_idempotent_at_persistence_layer` asserting mtime equality across two applies). **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change beyond replacing `UnsupportedRuntimeContext` on the local-operator-triggered binary path with the end-to-end live apply pipeline whose outcomes are surfaced through the canonical `AppliedCandidate::applied_log_line` and the `VERDICT=…` summary line**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, and **no private-key material referenced by `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, `AppliedCandidate`, or the `VERDICT=…` log lines** are introduced by Run 073.

#### C4 Run 074 evidence update (2026-05-14) — long-running local operator-triggered live trust-bundle reload-apply trigger via SIGHUP (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — the long-running-node trigger blocker called out in the Run 073 §"What is NOT narrowed" list is closed for the **local-file SIGHUP** surface; full C4 still OPEN for peer/gossiped acceptance, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, KMS/HSM, signing-key ratification, fast-sync restore, per-environment trust-anchor operation, selective session retention, and admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers)

DevNet Evidence Run 074 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_074.md`) closes the **long-running-node trigger** sub-piece called out in the Run 073 §"What is NOT narrowed" list for the local-file SIGHUP surface. A new Run 074 module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_live_trust_reload.rs` introduces `LiveReloadController` — a small, production-honest controller that holds `Arc<LivePqcTrustState>` (Run 071) + `Arc<dyn P2pSessionEvictor>` (Run 072) + `Arc<P2pMetrics>` + a clonable `LiveReloadConfig` (environment, chain_id, signing-key set, activation context, sequence-persistence path, optional local-leaf cert bytes) — and serializes concurrent triggers via an `Arc<AtomicBool>` "in progress" CAS guard. On every `try_trigger()` the controller constructs a **fresh** Run 073 `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext` over the SAME live `LivePqcTrustState` + SAME live `Arc<dyn P2pSessionEvictor>` and drives the SAME Run 070 `apply_validated_candidate_with_previous` pipeline end-to-end, surfacing a typed `LiveReloadOutcome { Applied(AppliedCandidate) | AlreadyInProgress | Invalid(ReloadApplyError) | Fatal(reason) }`. The `qbind-node` binary's `run_p2p_node` is rewired in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` to (i) retain a clone of the freshly-initialized `LivePqcTrustState` so the same `Arc<RwLock<LivePqcTrustSnapshot>>` the listener-side handshake verifier reads from is also held by the SIGHUP task, (ii) construct a `LiveReloadController` over that handle + `node_context.p2p_service` (upcast to `Arc<dyn P2pSessionEvictor>` — the live `TcpKemTlsP2pService` Run 072 evictor) + `node_metrics.p2p_arc()` + a `LiveReloadConfig` whose `signing_keys` / `chain_id` / `sequence_path` / `local_leaf_cert_bytes` are bit-for-bit identical to the startup-time `--p2p-trust-bundle` path's values, (iii) install a `tokio::signal::unix::signal(SignalKind::hangup())` listener that on each SIGHUP calls `controller.try_trigger()` inside `tokio::task::spawn_blocking` (so the sequence-file write and the trust-state swap don't run on the async runtime's worker pool), logs the canonical `LiveReloadOutcome::log_line()`, and on `Fatal` only (i.e. `SequenceCommitFailedRollbackAlsoFailed`) sends to the existing `shutdown_tx` watch channel for graceful shutdown. Two new hidden CLI flags `--p2p-trust-bundle-live-reload-enabled` (bool) and `--p2p-trust-bundle-live-reload-path <PATH>` are added (disabled by default; both required together; refused without `--p2p-trust-bundle <BASELINE-PATH>`). Six new `qbind_p2p_trust_bundle_live_reload_*` counters / gauge on `P2pMetrics` (`trigger_total`, `apply_success_total`, `apply_failure_total`, `already_in_progress_total`, `sessions_evicted_total`, `last_applied_sequence`) are rendered exactly once on `/metrics` (verified by a new `metrics` lib test) and bumped truthfully (success counter only on `Applied`; failure counter on `Invalid` AND on `Fatal`; sessions_evicted accumulates the sum of `AppliedCandidate::session_evictions` across successful applies; gauge holds the last-successfully-applied sequence number, 0 until the first success).

**What is narrowed (Run 074).** The long-running-node trigger blocker for the **local-file SIGHUP surface** is removed: the `qbind-node` binary can now be armed (via the two hidden flags) to live-apply a candidate trust-bundle on a running node without restart. 10 new integration tests (`crates/qbind-node/tests/run_074_pqc_trust_bundle_live_reload_tests.rs`) prove the contract end-to-end against a real `LivePqcTrustState` + `MockP2pSessionEvictor` + real on-disk sequence files: `run074_happy_path_trigger_swaps_live_state_evicts_and_commits_with_metrics_bumped` proves that a sequence=2 candidate against a sequence=1 baseline produces `LiveReloadOutcome::Applied { evicted=4, new_sequence=2 }`, swaps the live state's fingerprint to `canonical_fingerprint(&candidate)`, advances the on-disk record to `highest_sequence=2`, evicts exactly one session-batch with reason `TrustBundleReloadApply` reporting Run 072's truthful `attempted=4 evicted=4 failed=0`, and bumps the six Run 074 counters to `trigger_total=1, apply_success_total=1, apply_failure_total=0, already_in_progress_total=0, sessions_evicted_total=4, last_applied_sequence=2`; `run074_validation_rollback_failure_leaves_state_seq_evictor_unchanged` and `run074_validation_tampered_signature_leaves_state_seq_evictor_unchanged` prove that validation failure at the Run 069 entry point surfaces `LiveReloadOutcome::Invalid(ValidationFailed(_))`, the evictor's recorded-reports history is empty, the live state's fingerprint stays at the baseline, the seq file's bytes AND mtime are unchanged, and only `trigger_total + apply_failure_total` bump (sessions_evicted stays at 0); `run074_session_eviction_partial_failure_rolls_back_live_state` proves that `MockP2pSessionEvictor::arrange_failure(2)` of 5 sessions surfaces `Invalid(SessionEvictionFailed { rollback_ok: true, message ~ "attempted=5 evicted=3 failed=2" })`, reverts the live state's `LivePqcTrustSnapshot` to the baseline Arc, and leaves the seq file mtime unchanged; `run074_sequence_commit_failure_rolls_back_live_state_and_preserves_seq_file` proves that a pre-seeded poison `EqualSequenceFingerprintMismatch` record at sequence=2 (different fingerprint) refuses the candidate with at most one evictor call recorded, live state reverts to baseline metadata, seq file is preserved bit-for-bit; `run074_already_in_progress_guard_rejects_concurrent_trigger_without_mutation` proves the CAS guard via a controller clone (the SIGHUP task receives a clone but shares the same `Arc<AtomicBool>` flag) — while the guard is taken by a sibling thread, a concurrent `try_trigger` returns `LiveReloadOutcome::AlreadyInProgress`, the apply pipeline does not run (evictor history empty, live state at baseline, seq file at baseline, `already_in_progress_total=1`), and after the sibling releases the guard a real trigger goes through cleanly; `run074_reapply_same_candidate_is_idempotent_and_metrics_remain_truthful` proves that two consecutive applies of the SAME candidate (sequence=2 fingerprint=F) hit `EqualSequenceSameFingerprint` as a no-write at the persistence writer (seq file bytes AND mtime equal across both applies) while the success counter advances to 2 and `last_applied_sequence` stays at 2; `run074_freshly_constructed_controller_has_no_side_effects` proves the disabled-by-default invariant (every metric is 0 before any `try_trigger*` call); `run074_try_trigger_with_activation_forwards_override_height` proves the explicit-override entry point correctly forwards a too-low height to a refusal AND a sufficient override to a success against the SAME controller / SAME candidate file; `run074_metric_family_renders_alongside_run_072_after_apply` proves that the six Run 074 metric names render exactly once each on `/metrics` and that the Run 072 `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` family continues to render (no displacement, no double-counting on the Run 074 counter). The release binary (`./target/release/qbind-node`) emits operator-actionable `FATAL` lines on all three CLI partial-config refusals (recorded verbatim in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_074.md` §6).

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 074 is **not** peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance — local files only; the candidate is read by the same code that reads `--p2p-trust-bundle` at startup. Run 074 is **not** an admin-API trigger or a filesystem-watcher hot-reload — only SIGHUP. Run 074 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing — the controller's `ActivationContext` is initialized to `height_only(0)` (the same height-only stance the startup `--p2p-trust-bundle` path uses today); a future run that lands a live height source can extend `LiveReloadConfig` without changing the SIGHUP surface or its tests. Run 074 is **not** KMS / HSM custody for bundle-signing keys (signing keys are still operator-supplied via `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`). Run 074 is **not** bundle-signing-key ratification (no on-chain or admin-API ratification flow; the trusted set is still operator-distributed at startup). Run 074 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity (the live binary does not yet replay `TrustBundleRecord` from a snapshot). Run 074 is **not** per-environment trust-anchor operation (root rotation cadence, escrow, key recovery). Run 074 is **not** selective session retention — the v0 policy is "evict all on successful apply" (Run 072) and is preserved bit-for-bit. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 074).** Every claim is anchored in the implementation file + matching unit/integration test: the controller is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_live_trust_reload.rs::LiveReloadController` and proven by `controller_construction_does_not_read_candidate_path`, `controller_is_clone_and_shares_in_progress_guard`, `trigger_with_nonexistent_candidate_path_returns_invalid_and_bumps_failure_counter`, `always_unsupported_evictor_surfaces_invalid_not_fatal`, and `outcome_log_line_marks_each_branch_with_run_074_prefix`; the SIGHUP signal-handler task is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs::spawn_run074_live_reload_task` (gated behind `#[cfg(unix)]`; the `#[cfg(not(unix))]` fallback logs the operator-actionable "trigger not supported on this platform" line and returns `None`); the end-to-end composition against the Run 073 production adapter is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_074_pqc_trust_bundle_live_reload_tests.rs::run074_happy_path_trigger_swaps_live_state_evicts_and_commits_with_metrics_bumped` (asserts the live state's post-swap fingerprint matches `canonical_fingerprint(&candidate)`, the evictor recorded exactly one call with `EvictionReason::TrustBundleReloadApply` and `attempted=4 evicted=4 failed=0`, `load_record(&seq_path).highest_sequence == 2`, and the six Run 074 counters/gauge are at their post-success values); the rollback contract is proven by `run074_session_eviction_partial_failure_rolls_back_live_state` (asserts Run 072's truthful `attempted == evicted + failed` invariant verbatim in the surfaced error message AND that the live state reverts to the baseline `Arc`); the in-progress guard is anchored by `run074_already_in_progress_guard_rejects_concurrent_trigger_without_mutation` (uses a `#[doc(hidden)] pub fn __test_in_progress_swap` test-only helper documented as test-only — production code MUST NOT touch the guard directly); the binary-level CLI top-level partial-config refusals are anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (the new Run 074 top-level validation block immediately after the Run 073 hook block and before `validate_p2p_config()`) and proven by the release-binary smokes recorded verbatim in `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_074.md` §6 (three `FATAL` lines, one per partial-config shape, each exiting the process before any P2P listener / handshake / consensus loop starts).
