#### C4 Run 076 evidence update (2026-05-15) — disabled-by-default peer/gossiped trust-bundle candidate validation boundary (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — library-level peer-supplied candidate **validation-only** path that reuses the Run 069 pipeline; full C4 still OPEN for peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, selective per-peer session retention, KMS/HSM custody, on-chain signing-key ratification, fast-sync restore parity, per-environment trust-anchor operation, and the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke)

DevNet Evidence Run 076 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_076.md`) closes the smallest defensible piece of the long-standing "peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance remains C4-OPEN" Run 075 §10 residual. Before Run 076 the project had **no** library surface — let alone a binary surface — that even *parsed* a peer-supplied trust-bundle candidate. Run 076 lands the safest possible foundation: a **library-level, disabled-by-default** `pqc_trust_peer_candidate::PeerCandidateValidator` that can receive a bounded peer-supplied candidate envelope and validate it through the **same** Run 069 `validate_candidate_bundle_full` entry point that startup, the local reload-check, the Run 073 process-start apply, and the Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply already use. The validator exposes **no** apply function. It **cannot** swap `LivePqcTrustState`. It **cannot** evict P2P / KEMTLS sessions. It **cannot** persist a sequence number (Run 055 `peek_sequence` is read-only). It **cannot** propagate the candidate. It **cannot** be reached by the production binary in this run — there is no CLI flag and no wire integration. The default-constructed value (`PeerCandidateValidator::disabled()`) returns `PeerCandidateOutcome::Disabled` on every call without touching the payload.

**What is narrowed (Run 076).** A new module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_peer_candidate.rs` adds: (1) `PeerCandidateEnvelope { envelope_version, domain_tag, peer_id, environment, chain_id_hex, declared_sequence, declared_fingerprint_prefix, declared_length, bundle_bytes }` — a strict, log-safe wire/test envelope with a hard `MAX_PEER_CANDIDATE_BUNDLE_BYTES = 256 KiB` ceiling that drops oversized payloads BEFORE any ML-DSA work; (2) `PeerCandidateConfig { enabled, duplicate_lru_capacity, duplicate_suppression, rate_limit_window_ms, max_in_window }` with `enabled = false` by default; (3) `PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept(envelope, ctx) -> PeerCandidateOutcome` whose outcome variants are `Disabled | Oversize | RateLimited | DuplicateSuppressed | Validated(ValidatedPeerCandidate) | Rejected(PeerCandidateRejection)` — every variant is non-mutating for live trust state, sequence persistence, and P2P sessions; (4) `PeerCandidateRejection::{Envelope, ValidationFailed, DeclaredMetadataMismatch}` with display strings that explicitly state `live trust state unchanged; sequence not persisted; sessions untouched`; (5) `ValidatedPeerCandidate::observed_log_line()` — the single source of truth for the "validated but NOT applied" operator-log line (contains the literal substrings `Run 076`, `NOT applied`, `not propagated`, `sequence not persisted`, `live trust state unchanged`, `sessions untouched`, plus log-safe metadata: peer-id, 8-hex-char fingerprint prefix, environment, chain-id-hex, sequence, signature_verified, active root/revoked-root/revoked-leaf counts); (6) a bounded `PeerCandidateDuplicateCache` LRU keyed by 8-hex-char fingerprint prefix that prevents repeated expensive ML-DSA verification of identical bytes; and (7) a fixed-window `PeerCandidateRateLimiter` (no background timer task — window edges are observed on the next call, matching the Run 074 "no unbounded task spawning" discipline). Seven new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` Prometheus counters land on `P2pMetrics` (`received_total` bumped on every entry, `validated_total`, `rejected_total`, `dropped_oversize_total`, `rate_limited_total`, `duplicate_total`, `disabled_total`) — **with no `_applied_total` family** (intentional; the validator never applies). The Run 076 metrics render exactly once each in `P2pMetrics::format_metrics` (verified by `peer_candidate_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`). Integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_076_pqc_peer_candidate_validation_tests.rs` (16/16 pass) cover: disabled-by-default no-op + no scratch file written; valid higher-sequence candidate validates but is NOT applied (`assert_seq_file_unchanged` after success); tampered-signature rejected at loader stage; wrong-environment / wrong-chain-id envelopes rejected BEFORE crypto with no scratch file; lower-sequence rollback rejected by Run 055 read-only peek; equal-sequence different-fingerprint rejected as equivocation; local-revoked-leaf rejected by Run 061 self-check; local-issuer-root-revoked rejected by Run 063 self-check; oversize candidate dropped pre-crypto with no scratch file; declared-length-vs-payload mismatch rejected at envelope; declared-fingerprint-prefix and declared-sequence mismatches rejected AFTER loader cross-check; duplicate-fingerprint suppression skips the second crypto call; rate limit blocks after `max_in_window`; and a side-by-side test proving the Run 069 reload-check entry point is unaffected by Run 076 (both work without mutating each other's state). Module unit tests (`cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_trust_peer_candidate`) add 16 more checks covering the envelope pre-check error surface, the LRU's bounded capacity, the rate limiter's window roll-over, the disabled-by-default short-circuit, and the operator-log line shape. Metrics unit tests on `P2pMetrics` add two new tests (`peer_candidate_metrics_start_at_zero_and_record_outcomes_atomically`, `peer_candidate_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`) — both assert that **no** `peer_candidate_applied_total` family exists and that no Run 074 apply-related counter is bumped by any Run 076 outcome.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 076 is **not** peer-driven live apply — the validator has no apply function and `LivePqcTrustState` is untouched on every return path (the strict library-level boundary is the entire point of Run 076). Run 076 is **not** a peer/gossip propagation surface — the validator never re-broadcasts; the candidate is end-of-line. Run 076 is **not** an admin-API trigger or filesystem-watcher hot reload — Run 074's SIGHUP-only trigger surface is unchanged; Run 076 adds **no** new trigger surface. Run 076 is **not** a CLI / wire change to the `qbind-node` binary — no new flag, no new network listener, no new gossip subscription, and no production caller of the validator exists in this run (this is the strict "no behavior change unless enabled" boundary). Run 076 is **not** a change to startup trust-bundle validation, Run 069 reload-check, Run 070 apply contract, Run 071 `LivePqcTrustState`, Run 072 session-evictor, Run 073 `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, or Run 074 `LiveReloadController` — all six are bit-for-bit unchanged (12/12 Run 069, 13/13 Run 070, 13/13 Run 071, 17 + 8 Run 072, 10 + 10 Run 073, and 5 + 10 Run 074 tests continue to pass after Run 076 lands). Run 076 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing (unchanged from Run 057; bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed via the inherited loader). Run 076 is **not** KMS / HSM custody. Run 076 is **not** bundle-signing-key on-chain / in-binary ratification. Run 076 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity. Run 076 is **not** selective per-peer session retention. Run 076 is **not** the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 076).** The validator is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_trust_peer_candidate.rs` and proven by the 16 module unit tests (`run076_disabled_by_default`, `run076_max_size_is_bounded_and_drops_before_crypto`, `run076_envelope_pre_check_rejects_{wrong_domain_tag,declared_length_mismatch,wrong_env,wrong_chain_id,unknown_version}`, `run076_duplicate_cache_lru_evicts_oldest`, `run076_duplicate_cache_capacity_at_least_one`, `run076_rate_limiter_admits_up_to_cap_then_blocks`, `run076_rate_limiter_zero_cap_always_blocks`, `run076_envelope_error_display_marks_pre_crypto_rejection_safely`, `run076_validated_log_line_marks_not_applied`, `run076_outcome_helpers`, `run076_config_default_is_disabled_by_default`, `run076_is_lower_hex_strict`) plus the 16 integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_076_pqc_peer_candidate_validation_tests.rs`. The reuse-not-fork discipline is anchored at `pqc_trust_peer_candidate::PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` where the inner call is the *same* `crate::pqc_trust_reload::validate_candidate_bundle_full` that Runs 069, 070, 073, and 074 already call (so any future hardening of the validation pipeline automatically applies to Run 076 too). The non-mutation contract is anchored verbatim by `run076_valid_higher_sequence_candidate_validates_but_not_applied` (calls `assert_seq_file_unchanged` AFTER the success path), `run076_rollback_candidate_rejected_by_read_only_peek`, `run076_equal_sequence_different_fingerprint_rejected`, `run076_tampered_signature_candidate_rejected_at_loader`, `run076_local_revoked_leaf_candidate_rejected`, `run076_local_issuer_root_revoked_candidate_rejected`, `run076_oversize_candidate_dropped_pre_crypto_no_scratch`, and `run076_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path` (proves Run 069 still validates the same bundle cleanly after Run 076 has seen it). The seven new metric counters are anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/metrics.rs` (`peer_candidate_*` fields on `P2pMetrics`; matching `record_peer_candidate_*` recorders; matching accessors; rendered exactly once each in `P2pMetrics::format_metrics`); the intentional absence of an `_applied_total` family is anchored by the explicit `assert!(!out.contains("qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_applied_total"))` in `peer_candidate_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`.

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 076).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change required). The seven new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters are the only `/metrics` surface added; they are bumped only when callers explicitly invoke the matching `record_peer_candidate_*` helper (the validator itself does not hold a `P2pMetrics` reference — Run 076 is library-pure and leaves the bump decision to a future wire integration or a test harness). No existing Run 044/050/051/055/057/070/071/072/073/074 metric name is displaced or duplicated (verified by `peer_candidate_metrics_render_once_in_format_metrics`, which also asserts existing series like `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_sequence_highest`, `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_attempt_total`, and `qbind_p2p_trust_bundle_live_reload_trigger_total` are still present). No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced or re-activated. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (Run 076 inherits the Run 050 trust-separation invariant via the unchanged `validate_candidate_bundle_full` path). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added — Run 076 introduces no CLI flag whatsoever. No Run 069 entry point is modified (12/12 integration tests continue to pass after Run 076 lands; `run076_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path` exercises both paths in the same test). No Run 070 entry point is modified (`ApplyMode`, `ReloadApplyError`, `LiveTrustApplyContext`, `apply_validated_candidate{,_with_previous}` are bit-for-bit unchanged; 13/13 Run 070 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 071 entry point is modified (13/13 Run 071 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 072 entry point is modified (the four `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters are bit-for-bit unchanged; 17 module unit tests + 8 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 073 entry point is modified (`ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, `NoActiveSessionsEvictor`, and the at-startup-time `--p2p-trust-bundle-reload-apply-path` hook are bit-for-bit unchanged; 10/10 Run 073 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 074 entry point is modified (`LiveReloadController`, `LiveReloadOutcome`, `spawn_run074_live_reload_task`, and the six `qbind_p2p_trust_bundle_live_reload_*` counters/gauge are bit-for-bit unchanged; 10/10 Run 074 integration tests continue to pass). The Run 050–075 §10 boundaries are preserved bit-for-bit: rejected peer-candidate envelopes do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by every `assert_seq_file_unchanged` call in the Run 076 integration suite); the validator does NOT mutate `LivePqcTrustState` (proven by construction — the type holds no live-state handle); idempotent re-acceptance of the same bytes does NOT pay ML-DSA verification cost twice (proven by `run076_duplicate_suppression_skips_second_crypto`); rate-limited or oversized envelopes do NOT touch the disk-side scratch (proven by `count_scratch_files(...) == 0` assertions in those tests); the disabled-by-default short-circuit guarantees zero side effects when the validator is constructed by `PeerCandidateValidator::disabled()` (proven by `run076_disabled_by_default_is_noop`). **No fabricated metric** (there is no `_applied_total` because the validator never applies), **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change** (no binary surface introduced, no peer wire integration introduced, no admin-API surface introduced, no gossip subscription introduced), **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, **no admin-API / network surface added**, and **no private-key material referenced by `PeerCandidateEnvelope`, `PeerCandidateConfig`, `PeerCandidateValidator`, `ValidatedPeerCandidate`, or any Run 076 log line** are introduced by Run 076.

#### C4 Run 077 evidence update (2026-05-15) — production-binary-facing, disabled-by-default peer-candidate validation local check mode (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — release `qbind-node` binary can now exercise the Run 076 validator from two hidden required-together CLI flags against a local JSON envelope fixture, without starting the node, without applying the candidate, without persisting its sequence, without evicting any P2P session, without propagating, and without introducing any peer / gossip / admin-API / filesystem-watcher wire surface; full C4 still OPEN for peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, selective per-peer session retention, KMS/HSM custody, on-chain signing-key ratification, fast-sync restore parity, per-environment trust-anchor operation, and the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke)

DevNet Evidence Run 077 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_077.md`) closes the smallest defensible **binary-facing** piece of the long-standing "peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance remains C4-OPEN" Run 076 §"What is NOT narrowed" residual. Before Run 077 the Run 076 `PeerCandidateValidator` had **no** caller on the production `qbind-node` binary — there was no CLI flag, no wire integration, no operator surface at all. Run 077 wires the validator into the binary under the safest possible boundary: two hidden, required-together CLI flags `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-validation-enabled` and `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-check <ENVELOPE_PATH>` that, when both supplied, parse a local JSON `PeerCandidateEnvelope` fixture, run the **same** Run 076 `try_accept` (which routes through the **same** Run 069 `validate_candidate_bundle_full` pipeline used at startup, by the local reload-check, by the Run 073 process-start apply, and by the Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply), bump the **same** seven Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` Prometheus counters (no new metric family; no `_applied_total` family — none exists by design), print the canonical `[binary] Run 077: VERDICT=<label> (NOT applied; not propagated; sequence not persisted; live trust state unchanged; sessions untouched). Envelope path=<path>.` operator-log line, and exit (`0` only on `Validated`; `1` on every fail-closed outcome and every partial-config / I/O / parse refusal). The node does **not** start in this mode. No `LivePqcTrustState` is constructed. No `P2pSessionEvictor` is constructed. No `LiveReloadController` is spawned. No KEMTLS listener is bound. No peer / network wire surface, admin-API endpoint, or filesystem watcher is introduced. The on-disk anti-rollback sequence record (under `--data-dir`, when supplied) is **never** modified — only consulted via the read-only Run 055 `peek_sequence` inherited from Run 069. The default behavior of every existing `qbind-node` CLI invocation is unchanged: neither flag → the Run 077 hook is a complete no-op and the normal startup flow continues.

**What is narrowed (Run 077).** A new module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_binary.rs` adds a pure-function `run_local_check(Run077Inputs, &P2pMetrics) -> Run077Result` entry point with `Run077Result::Refused { reason }` (for partial-config / I/O / parse / preconditions) and `Run077Result::Ran { outcome, verdict_line, observed_log_line }` (for every reached `try_accept` outcome). `Run077Result::exit_code() -> i32` is `0` only for `Ran { outcome: PeerCandidateOutcome::Validated(_), .. }` and `1` for every other variant. `Run077RefusalReason` enumerates the nine fail-closed boundaries (`EnabledFlagMissing`, `EnvelopePathMissing`, `UnsignedRequiredOnEnvironment`, `DataDirRequiredOnEnvironment`, `LeafCredentialFlagsUnpaired`, `FixtureIoError`, `FixtureParseError`, `SigningKeyParseError`, `LeafCredentialLoadError`) with log-safe `Display` impls. `PeerCandidateEnvelope` now derives `serde::Serialize` / `serde::Deserialize`; `bundle_bytes` is serialised as a lowercase-hex string via a small internal `peer_candidate_bundle_bytes_hex` serde module (no new dependency; diff-friendly fixture format; strictly fixture-only — Run 077 introduces no peer/gossip wire surface). `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` gains two new hidden `clap` args. `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` gains a Run 077 hook positioned AFTER the Run 069 reload-check block and BEFORE the Run 073 process-start reload-apply block — same staging discipline as Run 069 → Run 073 — that enforces the top-level required-together partial-config refusal, parses signing keys with the SAME parser Run 069 uses (TestNet/MainNet refuse unsigned bundles here; no fallback), loads leaf credentials via the SAME `PqcLeafCredentialPaths::load()` Run 069 uses for the Run 061/063 self-checks, refuses TestNet/MainNet without `--data-dir`, creates a scratch dir under `--data-dir/run077-peer-candidate-scratch` (or `std::env::temp_dir()` on DevNet without `--data-dir`), assembles `Run077Inputs`, calls `run_local_check`, prints the verdict + observed log line + (on rejection) `Debug`-formatted `PeerCandidateOutcome` for operator audit, and exits with the deterministic exit code. Integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_077_binary_peer_candidate_check_tests.rs` (12/12 pass) cover: disabled-by-default boundary (`run077_disabled_by_default_hook_is_inactive`); partial-config refusal in both directions (`run077_partial_config_path_only_refuses_and_does_not_bump_metrics`, `run077_partial_config_enabled_only_refuses_and_does_not_bump_metrics`); fixture I/O / parse refusal before the validator is constructed and BEFORE `received_total` is bumped (`run077_fixture_io_error_refuses_before_validator`, `run077_fixture_parse_error_refuses_before_validator`); valid higher-sequence candidate → `Validated`, exit code 0, sequence file bit-for-bit unchanged after the success path, scratch file removed, `received_total` and `validated_total` each bumped by exactly 1, every other Run 076 counter still 0 (`run077_valid_candidate_validates_and_does_not_apply`); oversize payload dropped pre-crypto with no scratch leak (`run077_oversize_candidate_dropped_pre_crypto_no_scratch`); wrong-environment / wrong-chain-id envelope rejected pre-crypto (`run077_wrong_environment_envelope_rejected_pre_crypto`, `run077_wrong_chain_id_envelope_rejected_pre_crypto`); tampered-signature candidate rejected at loader with sequence file bit-for-bit unchanged (`run077_tampered_signature_rejected_at_loader`); a side-by-side test proving the Run 069 reload-check entry point still validates the SAME bundle cleanly AFTER a successful Run 077 check has seen it (`run077_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path`); and an explicit `format_metrics()` text assertion that `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_applied_total` is **not** present and that the Run 074 trigger counter has not been bumped (`run077_metrics_output_never_contains_applied_total_family`). Module unit tests (`cargo test -p qbind-node --lib pqc_peer_candidate_binary`, 11/11 pass) cover the hook-active guard predicate, the partial-config refusal surface, the refusal-exit-code contract, the log-safe `Display` impls, the stable `VERDICT=...` label set, and the canonical Run 077 verdict log line shape. **No new metric family is introduced**; the seven Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters are the only `/metrics` surface bumped, and the binary exits before `metrics::serve_metrics_http` is called — matching the same discipline as the Run 069 / Run 073 process-start hooks.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 077 is **not** peer-driven live apply — the validator type holds no live-state handle and there is no apply function to call. Run 077 is **not** a peer/gossip propagation surface — the validator never re-broadcasts; the candidate is end-of-line. Run 077 is **not** an in-running-node hot reload — Run 074's SIGHUP trigger remains the only long-running-node trust-reload trigger; Run 077 exits before the node is constructed. Run 077 is **not** an admin-API endpoint or filesystem watcher — no such surface is introduced. Run 077 is **not** a peer / gossip wire integration — no new network listener, dialer, or subscription is added. Run 077 is **not** a change to startup trust-bundle validation, Run 069 reload-check, Run 070 apply contract, Run 071 `LivePqcTrustState`, Run 072 session-evictor, Run 073 `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, Run 074 `LiveReloadController`, or Run 076 `PeerCandidateValidator` — every one of them is bit-for-bit unchanged (12/12 Run 069, 13/13 Run 070, 17 + 8 Run 072, 10/10 Run 073, 10/10 Run 074, and 16 + 16 Run 076 tests continue to pass after Run 077 lands). Run 077 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing (unchanged from Run 057; bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed via the inherited loader). Run 077 is **not** KMS / HSM custody. Run 077 is **not** bundle-signing-key on-chain / in-binary ratification. Run 077 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity. Run 077 is **not** selective per-peer session retention. Run 077 is **not** the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 077).** The binary entry point is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_binary.rs` (module unit tests in the same file, integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_077_binary_peer_candidate_check_tests.rs`). The reuse-not-fork discipline is anchored at `pqc_peer_candidate_binary::run_local_check` where the inner call is the SAME `pqc_trust_peer_candidate::PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` (Run 076) whose inner call is in turn the SAME `pqc_trust_reload::validate_candidate_bundle_full` (Run 069) that startup, the local reload-check, Run 073 process-start apply, and Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply all use. The non-mutation contract is anchored verbatim by `run077_valid_candidate_validates_and_does_not_apply` (calls `assert_seq_file_unchanged` AFTER the success path), `run077_oversize_candidate_dropped_pre_crypto_no_scratch`, `run077_wrong_environment_envelope_rejected_pre_crypto`, `run077_tampered_signature_rejected_at_loader`, and `run077_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path` (proves Run 069 still validates the same bundle cleanly after Run 077 has seen it, even when both share the same `--data-dir` and the SAME sequence-persistence path). The intentional absence of an `_applied_total` family is anchored by `run077_metrics_output_never_contains_applied_total_family` (explicit `format_metrics()` substring assertion). The disabled-by-default boundary is anchored by `run077_disabled_by_default_hook_is_inactive` (the binary `main` only enters the Run 077 hook when `run077_hook_active(...)` returns `true`, i.e. when at least one of the two flags is set) and by `run077_partial_config_*` (the SAME hook then refuses with a fail-closed `exit 1` when only one of the two required-together flags is supplied).

#### C4 Run 078 evidence update (2026-05-15) — disabled-by-default P2P wire receive path for peer-candidate validation only (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — typed/versioned/bounded wire envelope `PeerCandidateWireEnvelopeV1`, dedicated frame discriminator `0x05` distinct from `p2p_tcp.rs` 0x01/0x02/0x03, strict frame-layer codec, disabled-by-default `PeerCandidateWireReceiver` that routes decoded frames through the **same** Run 076 `PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` → Run 069 `validate_candidate_bundle_full` pipeline; one hidden CLI banner flag; **no production gossip dispatcher publishes 0x05 frames on the wire today** — the armed receiver is library-level only; full C4 still OPEN for peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, selective per-peer session retention, KMS/HSM custody, on-chain signing-key ratification, fast-sync restore parity, per-environment trust-anchor operation, and the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke)

DevNet Evidence Run 078 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_078.md`) closes the smallest defensible **wire-receive surface** piece of the long-standing "peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance remains C4-OPEN" residual previously narrowed by Runs 076 (library-level validator) and 077 (binary-facing local-file fixture check). Before Run 078, the production `qbind-node` binary had **no** decode surface for a peer-supplied trust-bundle candidate frame — there was no wire envelope type, no frame discriminator reservation, no codec, and no receiver. Run 078 lands the safest possible wire-receive foundation under the same strict non-mutation contract every prior Run 069–077 hot-reload sub-piece inherits from Run 069: a typed, versioned, bounded wire envelope decoded over the existing length-prefixed framing layer used by `p2p_tcp.rs`, routed through the **same** Run 076 `PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` (which itself reuses the **same** Run 069 `validate_candidate_bundle_full` pipeline used at startup, by the Run 069 reload-check, by the Run 073 process-start apply, by the Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply, and by the Run 077 binary-facing local check), bumping the **same** seven Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` Prometheus counters (no new metric family; no `_applied_total` family — none exists by design; no `peer_candidate_wire_*` family — none introduced by design), and end-of-line at the receiver (no propagation, no apply, no session eviction, no live trust state mutation, no sequence persistence).

**What is narrowed (Run 078).** A new module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_wire.rs` adds: (1) `PeerCandidateWireEnvelopeV1 { envelope_version=1, domain_tag="QBIND:PQC_TRUST_BUNDLE_PEER_CANDIDATE_WIRE:v1", peer_id, environment, chain_id_hex, declared_sequence, declared_fingerprint_prefix, declared_length, bundle_bytes }` — a strict, log-safe, versioned wire envelope **distinct** from the Run 076 / Run 077 local fixture envelope (`"qbind-peer-trust-bundle-candidate-v0"`): different domain tag, different version namespace, separate type, so a fixture file can never be replayed as a wire frame and vice versa; `bundle_bytes` reuses the Run 076 lowercase-hex serde codec (now publicly re-exported as `peer_candidate_bundle_bytes_hex_pub`) so captured wire frames are operator-inspectable with the same tooling as Run 077 fixtures; (2) `DISCRIMINATOR_PEER_CANDIDATE_WIRE = 0x05` — a reserved P2P frame discriminator that does **not** collide with the existing `p2p_tcp.rs` consensus (`0x01`), DAG (`0x02`), or control (`0x03`) discriminators (`0x04` left reserved for any future control-plane extension); (3) `MAX_PEER_CANDIDATE_WIRE_FRAME_BYTES = 2 × MAX_PEER_CANDIDATE_BUNDLE_BYTES + 16 KiB` enforced on the **declared** `payload_len` from the 5-byte frame header **before** any allocation / decode / signature work (DoS-resistant); (4) `encode_peer_candidate_wire_frame` / `decode_peer_candidate_wire_frame` — strict, fail-closed frame codec with `PeerCandidateWireFrameError` enumerating the seven frame-layer fail-closed boundaries (`FrameTooShort`, `UnknownDiscriminator`, `DeclaredPayloadOversize`, `FrameTruncated`, `PayloadParseError`, `UnsupportedEnvelopeVersion`, `UnknownDomainTag`) with log-safe `Display` impls that contain the canonical disclaimer substrings; (5) `PeerCandidateWireReceiverConfig` — disabled-by-default wrapper; `Default::default()` returns `enabled = false`; `PeerCandidateWireReceiver::new` forces `inner.enabled = config.enabled` so a misconfigured caller cannot accidentally bypass the validator; (6) `PeerCandidateWireReceiver` — the disabled-by-default receive handler. Wraps a Run 076 `PeerCandidateValidator` one-to-one. Holds **no** live PQC trust state, **no** session evictor, **no** broadcast handle, **no** admin-API endpoint, **no** filesystem watcher, **no** sequence persistence handle; the receiver's only entry point is `try_handle_frame(frame_bytes, ctx, metrics) -> PeerCandidateWireOutcome`; (7) `PeerCandidateWireOutcome` — three-variant return shape (`Disabled`, `FrameRejected(PeerCandidateWireFrameError)`, `ValidatorRan(PeerCandidateOutcome)`); every variant is non-mutating for live trust state, sequence persistence, and P2P sessions; (8) `wire_observed_log_line` — single source of truth for the operator log line; contains the stable substrings `Run 078`, `NOT applied`, `not propagated`, `sequence not persisted`, `live trust state unchanged`, `sessions untouched`. A new hidden CLI flag `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-validation-enabled` (disabled by default) lands in `cli.rs`; a one-line banner hook in `main.rs` positioned AFTER the Run 077 binary-facing local check hook and BEFORE the Run 073 process-start reload-apply hook records the armed state — when the flag is unset, the hook is byte-for-byte silent; when the flag is set, a single safe banner line records the armed state and **the banner is the ONLY behaviour the flag adds to the production startup path in this run** (no new network listener, no new gossip subscription, no new admin-API endpoint, no filesystem watcher). Integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_078_pqc_peer_candidate_wire_tests.rs` (19/19 pass) cover: disabled-by-default boundary (default-constructed receiver never decodes the payload, never calls the validator, bumps only `received_total` + `disabled_total`); encode/decode roundtrip preserves all envelope fields byte-for-byte; unknown-discriminator frame (`0x01` consensus discriminator stamped on the first byte) rejected at the frame layer with `rejected_total` bumped (not `dropped_oversize_total`); oversize declared payload (`MAX_PEER_CANDIDATE_WIRE_FRAME_BYTES + 1`) dropped BEFORE any allocation / decode / crypto with `dropped_oversize_total` bumped without any scratch file write; truncated frame, malformed JSON payload, unknown envelope version (`9999`), and unknown domain tag (the Run 076 fixture domain tag stamped onto a wire envelope — cross-protocol replay attempt) each rejected at the frame layer with `rejected_total`; enabled + valid higher-sequence candidate validates and is NOT applied — on-disk sequence file bit-for-bit unchanged, no scratch file left behind, `received_total` AND `validated_total` each bumped by exactly one, every other peer-candidate counter remains at zero, the operator log line contains the stable disclaimer substrings; enabled + tampered-signature candidate (first hex nibble of `sig_bytes` flipped post-signing) rejected at the Run 069 loader stage; enabled + wrong-environment envelope (claims Mainnet, runtime expects Devnet) rejected at the envelope pre-check BEFORE any crypto runs; enabled + wrong-chain-id envelope rejected pre-crypto; enabled + duplicate-fingerprint frame's second call short-circuits via the Run 076 LRU without paying ML-DSA verification cost twice with `duplicate_total` bumped; enabled + rate-limit kicks in after `max_in_window = 1` admissions with `rate_limited_total` bumped; Run 069 reload-check entry point still validates the SAME bundle bytes cleanly AFTER a successful Run 078 wire-receive has seen them; Run 077 binary-facing local fixture check still validates the SAME bundle bytes cleanly AFTER a successful Run 078 wire-receive has seen them (both paths share the same `--data-dir` but neither writes to it); `P2pMetrics::format_metrics()` output rendered after a Run 078 `Validated` outcome contains the seven Run 076 counters but does NOT contain `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_applied_total` and does NOT contain any `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_wire_*` family; wire envelope ↔ Run 076 fixture envelope bridge round trip preserves `bundle_bytes` byte-for-byte; wire-frame cap strictly exceeds the Run 076 inner bundle cap so a legitimate maximum-sized Run 076 bundle is never dropped at the wire layer. Module unit tests in the same module (16/16 pass) cover: the frame discriminator non-collision invariant (`0x05` ≠ `0x01` consensus, ≠ `0x02` DAG, ≠ `0x03` control); the encode/decode roundtrip; every frame-layer error variant (short, unknown discriminator, declared-oversize-before-allocation, truncated, unknown version, unknown domain tag, malformed payload); the disabled-by-default short-circuit; the receiver-armed oversize / unknown-version paths; the `PeerCandidateWireReceiverConfig` default; the `PeerCandidateWireReceiver::new` `inner.enabled = enabled` forcing; the disabled-outcome stable log-line shape; and the wire cap / inner cap relationship.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 078 is **not** peer-driven live apply — the receiver type holds no live-state handle and there is no apply function to call. Run 078 is **not** a peer/gossip propagation surface — the receiver never re-broadcasts; the candidate is end-of-line at the receiver. Run 078 is **not** an in-running-node hot reload — Run 074's SIGHUP trigger remains the only long-running-node trust-reload trigger; Run 078's CLI flag only sets a startup banner. Run 078 is **not** an admin-API endpoint or filesystem watcher — no such surface is introduced. Run 078 is **not** a production gossip subscription — no Run 078 code path *publishes* a peer-candidate frame on the wire today; no `P2pMessage` variant is added; no `TcpKemTlsP2pService` read loop is modified; no `qbind-net` handshake is changed. The wire codec + receiver are library-level types only, and the binary banner hook is the only operator-visible production-binary surface added by Run 078. Run 078 is **not** a change to startup trust-bundle validation, Run 069 reload-check, Run 070 apply contract, Run 071 `LivePqcTrustState`, Run 072 session-evictor, Run 073 `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, Run 074 `LiveReloadController`, Run 076 library-level peer-candidate validator, or Run 077 binary-facing local check — all eight are bit-for-bit unchanged (12/12 Run 069, 13/13 Run 070, 10/10 Run 073, 10/10 Run 074, 16/16 Run 076, and 12/12 Run 077 integration tests continue to pass after Run 078 lands). Run 078 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing (unchanged from Run 057; bundles that declare `activation_epoch` continue to fail closed via the inherited loader). Run 078 is **not** KMS / HSM custody. Run 078 is **not** bundle-signing-key on-chain / in-binary ratification. Run 078 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity. Run 078 is **not** selective per-peer session retention. Run 078 is **not** the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 078).** The wire receive surface is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_wire.rs` (16 module unit tests in the same file, 19 integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_078_pqc_peer_candidate_wire_tests.rs`). The reuse-not-fork discipline is anchored at `pqc_peer_candidate_wire::PeerCandidateWireReceiver::try_handle_frame` where the inner call is the SAME `pqc_trust_peer_candidate::PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` (Run 076) whose inner call is in turn the SAME `pqc_trust_reload::validate_candidate_bundle_full` (Run 069) that startup, the local reload-check, Run 073 process-start apply, Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply, and Run 077 binary-facing local check all use. The non-mutation contract is anchored verbatim by `run078_valid_candidate_validates_but_is_not_applied` (calls `assert_seq_file_unchanged` AFTER the success path), `run078_oversize_declared_payload_dropped_before_allocation` (asserts `dropped_oversize_total` bumped and no scratch file written), `run078_unknown_discriminator_rejected_at_frame_layer`, `run078_unknown_domain_tag_rejected_at_frame_layer`, `run078_tampered_signature_candidate_rejected_at_loader`, `run078_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path`, and `run078_coexists_with_run077_binary_local_check_path` (proves the Run 069 reload-check and Run 077 binary-facing local check entry points still validate the same bundle cleanly after Run 078 has seen it, even when all three share the same `--data-dir` and the SAME sequence-persistence path). The intentional absence of an `_applied_total` family **and** the intentional absence of any new `peer_candidate_wire_*` metric family are anchored by `run078_metrics_output_never_contains_applied_total_family` (explicit `format_metrics()` substring assertion). The disabled-by-default boundary is anchored by `run078_disabled_by_default_does_not_decode_or_call_validator` (default-constructed receiver short-circuits on the cheap discriminator-check path and never decodes the payload) and by `PeerCandidateWireReceiverConfig::default()` returning `enabled = false`.

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 078).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No new metric family is added — the seven existing Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters are the only `/metrics` surface bumped by the wire path, and `run078_metrics_output_never_contains_applied_total_family` asserts both that `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_applied_total` does **not** appear and that no `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_wire_*` family appears. No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced or re-activated. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (Run 078 inherits the Run 050 trust-separation invariant via the unchanged `validate_candidate_bundle_full` path). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added — Run 078 introduces only one new hidden CLI flag whose on-its-own effect is only the startup banner. No Run 069 entry point is modified (12/12 integration tests continue to pass; `run078_does_not_affect_run069_reload_check_path` exercises both paths in the same test). No Run 070 entry point is modified (13/13 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 071 entry point is modified. No Run 072 entry point is modified (the four `qbind_p2p_session_eviction_*` counters are bit-for-bit unchanged). No Run 073 entry point is modified (10/10 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 074 entry point is modified (`LiveReloadController`, `LiveReloadOutcome`, `spawn_run074_live_reload_task`, and the six `qbind_p2p_trust_bundle_live_reload_*` counters/gauge are bit-for-bit unchanged; 10/10 integration tests continue to pass). No Run 076 entry point is modified (`PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` and the seven `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters are bit-for-bit unchanged; 16/16 integration tests + 16 module unit tests continue to pass; the public re-export of the existing `peer_candidate_bundle_bytes_hex` serde codec is a strictly mechanical visibility change with no behavioural impact). No Run 077 entry point is modified (`run_local_check`, `Run077Inputs`, `Run077Result`, `Run077RefusalReason`, the binary-facing local check hook, and the canonical Run 077 `VERDICT=...` log line are bit-for-bit unchanged; 12/12 integration tests + 11 module unit tests continue to pass; `run078_coexists_with_run077_binary_local_check_path` proves Run 077 still validates the same bundle cleanly after Run 078 has seen it). The Run 050–077 §10 boundaries are preserved bit-for-bit: rejected wire frames do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by every `assert_seq_file_unchanged` call in the Run 078 integration suite); the receiver does NOT mutate `LivePqcTrustState` (proven by construction — the type holds no live-state handle); idempotent re-acceptance of the same bytes does NOT pay ML-DSA verification cost twice (proven by `run078_duplicate_fingerprint_frame_short_circuits_via_lru`); rate-limited or oversized frames do NOT touch the disk-side scratch (proven by `count_scratch_files(...) == 0` assertions in those tests); the disabled-by-default short-circuit guarantees zero side effects when the receiver is constructed by `PeerCandidateWireReceiver::disabled()` (proven by `run078_disabled_by_default_does_not_decode_or_call_validator`). **No fabricated metric** (there is no `_applied_total` because the receiver never applies; there is no `peer_candidate_wire_*` because Run 078 reuses the Run 076 counters), **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change** (the production binary does not publish or subscribe to `0x05` frames in this run; the discriminator is reserved, not actively wired into any existing P2P read loop), **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, **no admin-API / network listener added**, **no peer/gossip subscription added**, and **no private-key material referenced by `PeerCandidateWireEnvelopeV1`, `PeerCandidateWireReceiverConfig`, `PeerCandidateWireReceiver`, `PeerCandidateWireOutcome`, or any Run 078 log line** are introduced by Run 078.

#### C4 Run 079 evidence update (2026-05-15) — live P2P receive-loop dispatch wiring for the disabled-by-default peer-candidate wire path (POSITIVE NARROW C4 sub-piece — the previously library-level-only Run 078 wire receiver is now reachable from the production `qbind-node` binary's per-peer KEMTLS `read_loop` via a `PeerCandidateWireFrameSink` trait + `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher` adapter, gated on the existing Run 078 hidden `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-validation-enabled` flag; **release-binary release-build now compiles with the dispatch wired**, but **no production publisher / gossip dispatcher publishes `0x05` frames on the wire today** — peer-candidate frames can only appear on the wire if an opted-in peer running a future publisher implementation sends them, and the receive-side dispatch is **validation-only**: no apply, no propagation, no sequence persistence, no `LivePqcTrustState` mutation, no `P2pSessionEvictor` call; full C4 still OPEN for peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, selective per-peer session retention, KMS/HSM custody, on-chain signing-key ratification, fast-sync restore parity, per-environment trust-anchor operation, and the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke)

DevNet Evidence Run 079 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_079.md`) closes the smallest defensible **live receive-loop dispatch wiring** piece of the long-standing "peer-supplied / gossiped bundle acceptance remains C4-OPEN" residual previously narrowed by Runs 076 (library-level validator), 077 (binary-facing local-file fixture check), and 078 (typed/versioned/bounded wire envelope + library-level `PeerCandidateWireReceiver`). Before Run 079 the Run 078 `PeerCandidateWireReceiver` had **no** caller in the production per-peer transport read loop — the Run 078 banner hook only recorded the armed state at startup, and the per-peer KEMTLS `read_loop` in `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs` had no branch on the reserved `0x05` discriminator. Run 079 lands the safest possible read-loop dispatch surface under the same strict non-mutation contract every prior Run 069–078 hot-reload sub-piece inherits from Run 069: a `PeerCandidateWireFrameSink: Send + Sync + 'static` trait whose only method is `handle_frame(&self, frame_bytes: &[u8])`, a `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher` adapter that owns a Run 078 `PeerCandidateWireReceiver` one-to-one + the runtime context fields (`expected_environment`, `expected_chain_id`, `scratch_dir`, `signing_keys`, `activation_ctx`, `sequence_persistence_path`, `local_leaf_cert_bytes`, `validation_time_secs`) and routes every received frame through the **same** Run 078 → Run 076 → Run 069 chain, a cheap-discard `DiscardPeerCandidateWireSink` that bumps only `received_total` + `disabled_total` and nothing else, a `read_loop_dispatch_peer_candidate_wire_frame(frame_bytes, sink) -> ReadLoopFrameDecision` pure-function helper that peeks the first byte, returns `ConsumedPeerCandidateWire` if it equals `DISCRIMINATOR_PEER_CANDIDATE_WIRE` (and routes to the sink when one is installed or drops cheaply when not), and returns `PassThrough` otherwise so the existing `decode_frame` demuxer for `0x00` / `0x01` consensus / `0x02` DAG / `0x03` control discriminators runs bit-for-bit unchanged. The per-peer `TcpKemTlsP2pService::read_loop` gains exactly one branch — a peek-and-route call to the helper before the existing `decode_frame` call — and continues the read loop in BOTH the consumed and dropped cases so a peer-supplied wire frame can NEVER poison the connection for honest traffic. The slot is plumbed end-to-end through `spawn_peer_handlers`, the accept-loop `handle_inbound_connection`, the legacy `dial_peer` single-shot path, AND the B8 `DialerHandle::dial_once` retry path so every per-peer session — inbound, outbound, and retry-dialed — sees the SAME installed sink.

**What is narrowed (Run 079).** `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_wire.rs` adds (relative to Run 078, which already landed the wire envelope + receiver): `PeerCandidateWireFrameSink` trait, `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher` + `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcherConfig`, `DiscardPeerCandidateWireSink`, `ReadLoopFrameDecision` enum (`PassThrough` | `ConsumedPeerCandidateWire`), and `read_loop_dispatch_peer_candidate_wire_frame` helper. `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs` adds an `Arc<RwLock<Option<Arc<dyn PeerCandidateWireFrameSink>>>>` field on `TcpKemTlsP2pService`, a `set_peer_candidate_wire_frame_sink(&self, Arc<dyn ...>)` public installer, a `has_peer_candidate_wire_frame_sink(&self) -> bool` read accessor (used by tests / observability), and one `read_loop_dispatch_peer_candidate_wire_frame(...)` call positioned BEFORE the existing `decode_frame(...)` call in `TcpKemTlsP2pService::read_loop`. The same field is added to `DialerHandle` and threaded through `spawn_peer_handlers` / `handle_inbound_connection` / `dial_peer` / `DialerHandle::dial_once` so the retry-dialed peer's read loop sees the same sink as the accept-loop's read loop. `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` adds an `Option<Arc<dyn PeerCandidateWireFrameSink>>` field on `P2pNodeBuilder` and a `with_peer_candidate_wire_sink(self, Arc<dyn ...>) -> Self` builder setter; `build()` installs the sink on the freshly constructed service via `set_peer_candidate_wire_frame_sink` BEFORE `start()` so the very first accepted or dialed peer's read loop already sees it. `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs::run_p2p_node` constructs the dispatcher (or cheap-discard fallback) when `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-validation-enabled` is supplied: with a `--p2p-trust-bundle` baseline + `trust_bundle_loaded` available, a full `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher` is built using the same `config.environment` + `config.environment.chain_id()` the existing startup loader uses, the same `bundle_signing_keys` parsed from `--p2p-trust-bundle-signing-key`, the same `ActivationContext::height_only(0)` baseline used by the Run 069 reload-check hook, the same `pqc_trust_sequence::sequence_file_path(data_dir)` for read-only sequence cross-check (the wire path never writes the sequence file), and the seven Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters via `node_metrics.p2p_arc()`; without a baseline, a `DiscardPeerCandidateWireSink` is installed instead so the operator opt-in is honoured truthfully (frames recognised at the discriminator layer, counted via `received_total + disabled_total`, dropped without decode). When the flag is absent the entire Run 079 install block is bit-for-bit silent — every existing `qbind-node` startup invocation is unchanged.

Run 079 introduces **no** new metric family — the seven existing Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters (`received_total`, `validated_total`, `rejected_total`, `dropped_oversize_total`, `rate_limited_total`, `duplicate_total`, `disabled_total`) are the only `/metrics` surface bumped by the live dispatch, and no `_applied_total` family appears anywhere in `P2pMetrics::format_metrics()` output (asserted by `run079_format_metrics_does_not_introduce_new_family` and `run079_live_dispatcher_validates_without_applying_or_persisting`). Run 079 introduces **no** new CLI flag — it reuses the Run 078 hidden `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-validation-enabled` flag verbatim and only changes the flag's runtime effect from "banner only" to "banner + install live read-loop sink". Run 079 introduces **no** new wire envelope, **no** new discriminator (`0x05` was already reserved by Run 078), **no** new payload type, **no** new `qbind-net` handshake step, and **no** change to KEMTLS session bring-up.

Integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_079_pqc_peer_candidate_wire_live_dispatch_tests.rs` (11/11 pass) cover: disabled-by-default builder boundary (`run079_default_service_has_no_wire_sink_installed` — the default `P2pNodeBuilder` constructs services with the slot empty so pre-Run-079 builder/test callers are unaffected); read-loop helper correctness (`run079_read_loop_helper_routes_only_0x05_to_sink` exhaustively checks that `0x00`, `0x01` consensus, `0x02` DAG, `0x03` control, `0x04` reserved, `0x06`, `0xff` all return `PassThrough` and only `0x05` returns `ConsumedPeerCandidateWire`; `run079_read_loop_helper_drops_0x05_without_sink` proves cheap-drop when no sink is installed); cheap-discard sink contract (`run079_discard_sink_only_bumps_received_and_disabled` proves exactly `received_total` + `disabled_total` are bumped and every other Run 076 counter remains at zero); enabled live dispatcher validates without applying (`run079_live_dispatcher_validates_without_applying_or_persisting` — `received_total` and `validated_total` each bumped by exactly one, every other counter at zero, `format_metrics()` output contains neither `peer_candidate_applied_total` nor any `peer_candidate_wire_*` family); tampered-signature candidate rejected at the Run 069 loader stage (`run079_live_dispatcher_rejects_tampered_signature`); oversize declared payload dropped BEFORE allocation / decode / crypto (`run079_live_dispatcher_drops_oversize_before_decode` — `dropped_oversize_total +1`, `rejected_total` unchanged); rate-limit fires after `max_in_window = 1` admissions with the truthful invariant that `validated + rate_limited + rejected + dropped_oversize + duplicate + disabled == received` (`run079_live_dispatcher_rate_limit_kicks_in`); co-existence with Run 069 reload-check on the same bundle bytes with no cross-mutation (`run079_dispatcher_composes_with_reload_check_no_cross_mutation`); `Arc<dyn PeerCandidateWireFrameSink>` is `Send + Sync` across threads (`run079_sink_trait_object_is_send_sync_across_threads`); and the `format_metrics()` family-absence invariant (`run079_format_metrics_does_not_introduce_new_family`).

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4-OPEN.** Run 079 is **not** peer-driven live apply — the dispatcher type holds no live-state handle and there is no apply function to call from the receive path. Run 079 is **not** peer/gossip propagation — the dispatcher never re-broadcasts; the candidate is end-of-line at the receiver. Run 079 is **not** a production gossip *publisher* — no `qbind-node` code path in this run *sends* a `0x05` frame on the wire; the discriminator is only routed *inbound*. Run 079 is **not** in-running-node hot apply — Run 074's SIGHUP trigger remains the only long-running-node trust-reload trigger; the wire path can NEVER trigger Run 074, Run 073, or Run 070 by construction (the dispatcher holds no `LivePqcTrustState`, no `LiveReloadController`, no `LiveTrustApplyContext`, no `P2pSessionEvictor`). Run 079 is **not** an admin-API endpoint or filesystem watcher. Run 079 is **not** a change to startup trust-bundle validation, Run 069 reload-check, Run 070 apply contract, Run 071 `LivePqcTrustState`, Run 072 session-evictor, Run 073 `ProductionLiveTrustApplyContext`, Run 074 `LiveReloadController`, Run 076 library-level peer-candidate validator, Run 077 binary-facing local check, or the Run 078 library-level wire receive surface — all nine are bit-for-bit unchanged (12/12 Run 069, 13/13 Run 070, 10/10 Run 073, 10/10 Run 074, 16/16 Run 076, 12/12 Run 077, and 19/19 Run 078 integration tests continue to pass after Run 079 lands; the existing 16-test Run 076 lib suite, 11-test Run 077 lib suite, and 24-test Run 078 lib suite all continue to pass — Run 078's lib suite grew by 8 tests for the new Run 079 dispatcher / discard sink / read-loop helper surface, all green). Run 079 is **not** `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing. Run 079 is **not** KMS / HSM custody. Run 079 is **not** bundle-signing-key on-chain / in-binary ratification. Run 079 is **not** fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity. Run 079 is **not** selective per-peer session retention. Run 079 is **not** the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, on-the-wire production *publisher* implementation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and on all of the above items.

**Anchoring (Run 079).** The live receive-loop dispatch surface is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_peer_candidate_wire.rs` (8 new module unit tests on top of the 16 Run 078 unit tests = 24 lib tests total, all pass) + `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_tcp.rs` (sink slot + setter + read accessor + one read-loop branch + `DialerHandle` field threading) + `crates/qbind-node/src/p2p_node_builder.rs` (`with_peer_candidate_wire_sink` builder setter + `build()` install hook) + `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (`run_p2p_node` install block gated on the existing Run 078 flag), with 11 integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_079_pqc_peer_candidate_wire_live_dispatch_tests.rs`. The reuse-not-fork discipline is anchored at `pqc_peer_candidate_wire::LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher::handle_frame` where the inner call is the SAME `PeerCandidateWireReceiver::try_handle_frame` (Run 078) whose inner call is the SAME `PeerCandidateValidator::try_accept` (Run 076) whose inner call is in turn the SAME `validate_candidate_bundle_full` (Run 069) that startup, the local reload-check, Run 073 process-start apply, Run 074 SIGHUP live reload-apply, Run 077 binary-facing local check, and Run 078 library-level wire receive all use. The non-mutation contract is anchored verbatim by `run079_live_dispatcher_validates_without_applying_or_persisting` (asserts `received_total + validated_total` only, no `_applied_total` and no `peer_candidate_wire_*` family in `format_metrics()` output), `run079_live_dispatcher_drops_oversize_before_decode` (asserts `dropped_oversize_total` bumped before any allocation / decode), `run079_dispatcher_composes_with_reload_check_no_cross_mutation` (proves Run 069 reload-check still validates the same bundle cleanly after Run 079 has seen it on the wire path), and `run079_format_metrics_does_not_introduce_new_family` (explicit `format_metrics()` substring assertion that no new family is rendered, including the live-reload `applied_total` counter not advancing). The disabled-by-default builder boundary is anchored by `run079_default_service_has_no_wire_sink_installed` (the default builder constructs services with the slot empty) and by the `run_p2p_node` install block's outer `if args.p2p_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_wire_validation_enabled` guard (bit-for-bit silent without the flag). The cheap-drop / no-poison contract for honest traffic is anchored by `run079_read_loop_helper_routes_only_0x05_to_sink` (every other discriminator returns `PassThrough` so the existing `decode_frame` path runs unchanged) and by the `continue` rather than `break` in the `ConsumedPeerCandidateWire` arm of `TcpKemTlsP2pService::read_loop` (peer-supplied `0x05` frames NEVER close the KEMTLS session).

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 079).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No new metric family is added — the seven Run 076 `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_*` counters are the only `/metrics` surface bumped by the live dispatch, and `run079_format_metrics_does_not_introduce_new_family` + `run079_live_dispatcher_validates_without_applying_or_persisting` both assert that `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_applied_total` does **not** appear and that no `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_peer_candidate_wire_*` family appears. No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced or re-activated. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority (Run 079 inherits the Run 050 trust-separation invariant via the unchanged `validate_candidate_bundle_full` path). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added — Run 079 introduces no new CLI flag and changes only the runtime effect of the existing Run 078 flag (banner → banner + install sink). No Run 069 / 070 / 071 / 072 / 073 / 074 / 076 / 077 / 078 entry point is modified at the *behavioural* level — every one of those modules' public API signatures and existing test suites continues to pass bit-for-bit; Run 079 only adds NEW public items (the trait, the dispatcher, the discard sink, the helper, the builder setter, the service setter / read accessor) plus one NEW field on each of `TcpKemTlsP2pService` and `DialerHandle` and `P2pNodeBuilder` with `Default::default() == None` so pre-Run-079 callers observe the same behaviour. The `decode_frame` demuxer in `p2p_tcp.rs` is bit-for-bit unchanged — Run 079 only adds a single peek-and-route call *before* the `decode_frame` call, and the call's `PassThrough` arm falls through to the unchanged `decode_frame`. The KEMTLS handshake (`qbind-net` `handshake::*`) is bit-for-bit unchanged. The consensus / DAG / control discriminators (`0x00` / `0x01` / `0x02`) continue to route exactly as before. The B8 retry policy `DialRetryPolicy` and the `is_transient_dial_error` classifier are bit-for-bit unchanged. The Run 050–078 §10 boundaries are preserved bit-for-bit on the wire receive path: rejected wire frames do NOT advance the persisted highest sequence (proven by the `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher` holding only a `sequence_persistence_path` for **read-only** anti-rollback cross-check inside `validate_candidate_bundle_full`; the dispatcher has no write path), the dispatcher does NOT mutate `LivePqcTrustState` (proven by construction — the type holds no live-state handle), the dispatcher does NOT call `P2pSessionEvictor` (proven by construction — the type holds no evictor handle), idempotent re-acceptance of the same bytes does NOT pay ML-DSA verification cost twice (inherited from Run 076's LRU short-circuit), rate-limited or oversized frames do NOT touch the disk-side scratch (inherited from Run 076), the disabled-by-default short-circuit guarantees zero side effects when `--p2p-trust-bundle-peer-candidate-wire-validation-enabled` is unset (proven by the bit-for-bit silent install block in `main.rs`), and an opted-in operator with no `--p2p-trust-bundle` baseline gets a cheap-discard sink that bumps only `received_total + disabled_total` (proven by `run079_discard_sink_only_bumps_received_and_disabled`). **No fabricated metric** (there is no `_applied_total` because the dispatcher never applies; there is no `peer_candidate_wire_*` family because Run 079 reuses the Run 076 counters), **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change** (the production binary does not *publish* `0x05` frames in this run; the discriminator is only routed inbound; honest peers that never send `0x05` see byte-for-byte-pre-Run-079 behaviour), **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, **no admin-API / network listener added**, **no peer/gossip subscription added** (the receive-side dispatch is not a subscription — it consumes whatever a peer happens to send on the existing KEMTLS-protected session and routes only when the operator has opted in), and **no private-key material referenced by `PeerCandidateWireFrameSink`, `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcher`, `LivePeerCandidateWireDispatcherConfig`, `DiscardPeerCandidateWireSink`, `ReadLoopFrameDecision`, the `read_loop_dispatch_peer_candidate_wire_frame` helper, or any Run 079 log line** are introduced by Run 079.
