#### C4 Run 084 evidence update (2026-05-18) — committed release-binary N=2 peer-candidate `0x05` matrix harness lands and passes end-to-end (STRONGEST POSITIVE for the Run 081/082/083 validation-only evidence gap; full C4/C5 still OPEN)

DevNet Evidence Run 084 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_084.md`) completes the exact follow-up left open by Runs 081, 082, and 083: the release-binary N=2 peer-candidate `0x05` matrix is now reproducible inside the repository via `scripts/devnet/run_084_peer_candidate_0x05_matrix.sh`. The harness builds release `qbind-node`, `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper`, `devnet_pqc_root_helper`, and the existing `devnet_consensus_signer_keystore_helper`; records sha256 and ELF BuildID; mints signed N=2 DevNet trust-bundle material plus DevNet consensus signer keystores; generates valid, invalid/wrong-chain, and duplicate peer-candidate envelopes; starts two release `qbind-node` processes over loopback; scrapes `/metrics`; captures stderr; captures `[Run040]` and `[binary] Run 033` lines; hashes the receiver sequence file before/after each candidate scenario; and asserts the validation-only invariants. The final harness run at committed revision `8170189975d21673eb0986c8d7f209f3befb0d92` passes baseline startup, valid `0x05` send/validate, receiver-disabled cheap-ignore, invalid/wrong-chain rejection, and duplicate suppression. Release artifact identities: `qbind-node` sha256 `d28c5493d3782dea5a20b03449eb01ab582f69c32e36d0a657c5f356fdb2ca49`, BuildID `c7ae28418d107f7e467fd4346f85644e6fcd943a`; `devnet_pqc_trust_bundle_helper` sha256 `39b4a9a5d61aa3c3c0117ceefe5849d087f13e0ee5024b90d95ebaeb08076efb`, BuildID `5050ded02408a3a27d1eccc382a5f48fa47b2501`; `devnet_pqc_root_helper` sha256 `58298104e52b687d28d6ca5a0606f54191cad28a84f2b8cda896a43dbbe005e4`, BuildID `7e514ca79e45bea41d743266f3224f631769902f`; `devnet_consensus_signer_keystore_helper` sha256 `18f455bd0e8891381ee00dd31472beade2409d843ddae25fcf327843620d8b4c`, BuildID `ebb61100054d043ad0e0d2dc4272968641233f38`.

**What Run 084 narrows.** The N=2 validation-only peer-candidate matrix that was deferred in Run 083 now has committed, repeatable release-binary evidence. Valid candidate frames increment sender `sent_total=1` and receiver `received_total=1` / `validated_total=1`; receiver-disabled runs keep receiver candidate counters at zero; invalid wrong-chain frames increment receiver `rejected_total=1`; duplicate replay increments receiver `duplicate_total=1` after the first validation. The receiver sequence-file hash remains unchanged across every candidate scenario; live-reload apply metrics and session-eviction metrics remain zero; sessions remain healthy with accepted cert verification and no cert rejection; logs continue to state `NOT applied; not propagated; sequence not persisted; live trust state unchanged; sessions untouched`. Run 084 also closes the Run 081/082/083 no-Dummy evidence gap for this matrix: the harness supplies real DevNet consensus signer keystores and explicit `--validator-consensus-key VID:100:HEXPK` entries, so `[binary] Run 033` reports `active=true reason=n/a` with signer and key-provider loaded, while `[Run040]` reports `pqc_root_mode=pqc-static-root`, ML-KEM-768, ChaCha20-Poly1305, `dummy_kem_registered=false`, and `dummy_aead_registered=false`. No runtime log contains `DummySig`, `DummyKem`, `DummyAead`, `dummy_kem_registered=true`, `dummy_aead_registered=true`, or a `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback line.

**What remains C4/C5-open.** Run 084 is evidence harness work only. It does not add peer-driven live apply, peer/gossip propagation, admin-API or filesystem-watcher triggers, `activation_epoch` runtime sourcing, KMS/HSM custody, on-chain or in-binary signing-key ratification, selective per-peer session retention, production fast-sync / consensus-storage restore parity, production per-environment trust-anchor operations, or an N-node MainNet peer-connection smoke. It does not redesign KEMTLS or consensus. Therefore full C4 remains OPEN for those production lifecycle/operability items, and C5 is not claimed closed. The immediate next action is to keep the Run 084 harness as the repeatable regression artifact for future peer-candidate changes and only pursue peer-driven live apply / propagation under a separate explicit task.
#### C4 Run 100 update (2026-05-21) — production trust-anchor authority and bundle-signing-key ratification MODEL landed (design/spec only); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 100 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_100.md`) and the new protocol specification `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` complete the **design-only** Run 100 scope per `task/RUN_100_TASK.txt`. Run 100 is a spec-first run: it produces a production-grade authority and ratification specification for PQC trust anchors and bundle-signing keys that future implementation runs (101–106) are required to follow, and it explicitly does **not** implement any of the specified behaviour. **No `crates/**/src/**` source change, no `crates/**/tests/**` test change, no `Cargo.toml` change, no new dependency, no new metric family, no new CLI flag, no protocol change, no wire format change** is introduced by Run 100. The Run 050–099 invariants are preserved bit-for-bit.

**What Run 100 narrows.** The two long-standing C4 sub-pieces "production trust-anchor authority model" and "bundle-signing-key ratification" — which until Run 099 were "open with operator-implicit signing-key trust on TestNet/MainNet and no formal design model" — now have a **formal, concrete, spec-first design model**: (a) **initial production authority comes from a genesis configuration file bound by a boot-time cryptographic hash**, NOT from Rust source-code constants — production static MainNet root anchors as source-code constants are explicitly rejected as an unsafe design (spec §11), as are hidden fallback anchors, implicit trust roots outside genesis/config, and environment-ambiguous root anchors; (b) **bundle-signing keys are authorized by typed, PQC-signed, deterministically-encoded ratification objects** bound to `(chain_id, environment, genesis_hash, authority_epoch)` with a monotonically non-decreasing `highest_authority_epoch` persisted to a new `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` file (spec §5, §8); (c) **per-environment policy** separates DevNet (explicit local shortcuts allowed; no silent fallback), TestNet (genesis-bound authority required; staged ratification allowed; DevNet shortcuts rejected), and MainNet (genesis-bound authority and ratification required; no operator-only shortcuts; no fallback static roots; no `--p2p-trusted-root` combined with `--p2p-trust-bundle`; no `make_test_crypto_provider` / `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead`) (spec §7); (d) **anti-rollback** is the standard Run-055-shaped atomic-rename pattern with restore semantics mirroring Run 097's snapshot epoch parity (`AuthorityRestoreInconsistent` typed error on snapshot rollback; pre-spec snapshots restore cleanly without silently treating missing authority epoch as `0`) (spec §8); (e) **emergency authority** defines three revocation classes (`Retired`, `Revoked`, `EmergencyRevoked`); the third bypasses Run 065 minimum margin on MainNet and applies on next observation; genesis-authority compromise has no in-protocol recovery (out-of-band by construction; the spec refuses to introduce a "rotate genesis authority on the running chain" surface because that would re-create the static-source-code anchor drift it forbids); equivocating ratifications at the same epoch fail closed with `AuthorityEpochEquivocation` (spec §9); (f) **peer-driven live apply remains forbidden** until the ratification verifier (Run 102), the anti-rollback machinery (Run 103), defined KMS/HSM custody assumptions (Run 105), operator override / emergency controls (§9), and release-binary evidence (Run 104) all exist, and even then peer-driven apply MUST stay disabled-by-default and inherit the Run 087 propagation/apply safety specification verbatim (spec §10). The future implementation plan is staged as Run 101 (additive genesis-config fields + canonical-serialization extension + boot-time `expected_genesis_hash` comparison + initial `LiveAuthorityState` derivation + environment separation), Run 102 (in-binary ratification verifier + persistent `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` + ratification install CLI flag + six new `qbind_p2p_pqc_trust_bundle_authority_*` counters), Run 103 (authority-state persistence and anti-rollback), Run 104 (release-binary rotation/revocation evidence matrices following the Run 084 / 085 / 089 shape, including emergency-revocation immediate-apply proven on the release binary), Run 105 (KMS/HSM custody model), and Run 106+ (peer-driven apply gates — only after Runs 102–104 are positive) (spec §13).

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4/C5-open.** Run 100 is design-only. It does **not** implement the genesis-bound authority fields, does **not** implement the bundle-signing-key ratification verifier, does **not** add the new persistent `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` file, does **not** add any new metric family or CLI flag, does **not** introduce KMS/HSM custody, does **not** implement governance, does **not** implement validator-set rotation, does **not** add peer-driven live apply, does **not** change the trust-bundle wire format or peer-candidate wire format, does **not** change consensus or KEMTLS, does **not** change `activation_epoch` semantics, does **not** introduce production static root anchors as source-code constants, does **not** add fallback roots or fallback signing keys, and does **not** weaken any existing signed-bundle / chain_id / environment / sequence anti-rollback / activation-height / `activation_epoch` / Run 065 minimum-margin / revocation / reload-check non-mutation / reload-apply ordering check. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on: production trust-anchor authority **implementation** (Run 101/102), bundle-signing-key ratification **verifier** (Run 102), authority-state **persistence and anti-rollback** (Run 103), release-binary rotation/revocation **evidence** (Run 104), **KMS/HSM custody** (Run 105), **peer-driven live apply** (Run 106+, gated by spec §10), in-binary / on-chain signing-key ratification, production fast-sync / broader consensus-storage restore, per-environment production trust-anchor operation, MainNet governance authorization path, the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke, `activation_epoch` runtime source (narrowed but still open per Run 099), peer-driven apply / propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and selective per-peer session retention. **C5 remains OPEN / unchanged** — Run 100 does not touch KEMTLS, consensus message wire formats, signature/verification semantics outside the design surface, or any C5-relevant code path. Run 100 does **not** claim full C4 closure and does **not** claim C5 closure.

**Anchoring (Run 100).** The spec is anchored at `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` (§1 scope and non-goals, §2 threat model, §3 trust assumptions, §4 current state investigation with file+line citations into `crates/qbind-ledger/src/genesis.rs:{448-489, 753, 855-873}` and `crates/qbind-node/src/{cli.rs:830-834, node_config.rs:2528, 2608-2609}`, §5 ratification object model, §6 genesis-bound initial authority, §7 per-environment policy, §8 persistence and anti-rollback, §9 emergency authority, §10 peer-driven apply dependency, §11 unsafe designs explicitly rejected, §12 operational lifecycle, §13 future implementation plan, §14 mapping to existing Runs, §15 documentation cross-check, §16 status). The evidence record is anchored at `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_100.md` (§1 investigation, §2 design decisions, §3 non-goals, §4 implementation plan, §5 contradictions found, §6 unresolved items, §7 files changed, §8 validation performed, §9 verdict). The runbook is anchored at `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md` (Run 100 row in §11 mapping + Run 100 prose note pointing to the spec). The cross-check against `docs/protocol/QBIND_PEER_TRUST_BUNDLE_PROPAGATION_SAFETY.md` §3 confirms the new spec §10 is the canonical extension of Run 087's "peers advisory only unless a future ratification mechanism exists" boundary; no Run 087 invariant is weakened.

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 100).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No new metric family is added; no `/metrics` surface changes. No new CLI flag is added. No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced, re-activated, or made reachable on any new code path. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority is introduced (the Run 050 trust-separation invariant is preserved and explicitly extended into §5.1 of the spec). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added — the spec §7.3 explicitly forbids it on MainNet. No Run 050 / 051 / 052 / 053 / 055 / 057 / 062 / 065 / 069 / 070 / 071 / 072 / 073 / 074 / 076 / 077 / 078 / 079 / 080 / 081 / 082 / 083 / 084 / 085 / 086 / 087 / 088 / 089 / 090 / 091 / 092 / 093 / 094 / 095 / 096 / 097 / 098 / 099 entry point is modified at the source or behavioural level — every one of those modules' public API signatures and existing test suites continues to pass bit-for-bit on the Run 100 tree state (no source change). The Run 050–099 §10 boundaries are preserved bit-for-bit. **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression** (Run 100 is documentation / evidence only — there is no behaviour change to regress), **no protocol behaviour change**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no transport-root reuse as bundle-signing authority**, **no classical signatures introduced** (spec §5.3 mandates PQC-only; classical signature suites are explicitly forbidden even on DevNet for the authority surface), **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, **no admin-API / network listener added**, **no peer/gossip subscription added**, **no peer/gossip publisher added**, **no peer-driven live apply path introduced**, and **no private-key material referenced by any Run 100 spec field, evidence statement, or runbook note** are introduced by Run 100.
#### C4 Run 101 update (2026-05-21) — genesis authority FIELDS, canonical genesis-hash helper, and boot-time refusal helper LANDED (partial implementation of Run 100 spec §6); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 101 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_101.md`) and the Run 101 update appended at §17 of `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` complete the **first implementation step** of Run 100's design, per `task/RUN_101_TASK.txt`. Run 101 lands the **additive genesis authority fields**, the **canonical domain-separated genesis-hash helper** with tag `b"QBIND:GENESIS:v1"`, and the **boot-time per-environment fail-closed verification helper** — without yet implementing the in-binary bundle-signing-key ratification verifier, without adding `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json`, without adding any new metric family, without adding any new CLI flag, without changing the trust-bundle or peer-candidate wire format, and without weakening any Run 050–099 invariant.

**What Run 101 narrows.** The C4 sub-piece "genesis-bound authority root surface and boot-time hash binding" — which Run 100 left as a fully-specified but **not-yet-implemented** design — is now **partial-positive**: (a) **additive genesis authority fields landed** as `GenesisConfig.authority: Option<GenesisAuthorityConfig>` (backward-compatible via `#[serde(default)]`), `GenesisAuthorityConfig { authority_policy_version, authority_sequence, authority_epoch, pqc_transport_roots, bundle_signing_authority_roots }`, and `GenesisAuthorityRoot { suite_id, key_fingerprint, label, not_before_epoch }` in `crates/qbind-ledger/src/genesis.rs`; (b) **canonical, domain-separated, deterministic genesis hash** `compute_canonical_genesis_hash(&GenesisConfig, env) -> [u8; 32]` landed with the project-style domain tag `b"QBIND:GENESIS:v1"`, length-prefixed framing of every field including the environment scope (`DEV`/`TST`/`MAIN`), `chain_id`, `genesis_time_unix_ms`, allocations, validators, council, monetary, and the full authority block (with discriminator bytes so `None` ≠ `Some(empty)` and the absence vs. emptiness of the authority block produce distinct hashes); (c) **boot-time verification helper** `verify_boot_time_genesis(env, &GenesisConfig, Option<&GenesisHash>)` landed with strict, fail-closed, per-environment refusal — MainNet refuses missing expected canonical hash (`ExpectedCanonicalHashMissing { env: Mainnet }`), refuses any mismatched hash (`CanonicalHashMismatch`), refuses missing authority before the hash compare (`AuthorityValidationFailed(Missing { env: Mainnet })`), refuses empty `bundle_signing_authority_roots` (`EmptyBundleSigningRoots`), refuses non-ML-DSA-44 suite (`UnsupportedSuite`), refuses short/non-hex/oversized/odd-length fingerprints (`MalformedFingerprint`), refuses empty labels (`EmptyLabel`), refuses empty fingerprints (`EmptyFingerprint`), refuses duplicate `(suite_id, key_fingerprint)` across the combined transport+bundle-signing set (`DuplicateAuthorityRoot`), refuses `authority_policy_version == 0` or `> 1` (`InvalidPolicyVersion`), and refuses chain_id not bound to the runtime environment (`ChainEnvironmentMismatch`); TestNet matches MainNet except that the expected-canonical-hash flag is not yet forced when absent (documented partial — Run 102 will force it alongside the ratification verifier); DevNet remains permissive for legacy local tests; (d) **24 new unit tests** in `crates/qbind-ledger/src/genesis.rs::tests` and **11 release-binary-facing integration tests** in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_101_genesis_authority_tests.rs` cover Scenarios 1–5 from the task (DevNet legacy passes; MainNet missing expected hash rejects; MainNet hash mismatch rejects; MainNet missing authority rejects with a precise error *before* any hash compare; MainNet valid genesis passes) plus duplicate/malformed/wrong-environment refusal coverage and a canonical-hash serde-json round-trip stability check; (e) the existing T232 `MainnetConfigError::GenesisMisconfigured` + T233 `MainnetConfigError::ExpectedGenesisHashMissing` MainNet CLI-layer fail-closed shields remain in place bit-for-bit, so MainNet operators still cannot accidentally start without a hash binding; (f) **no `Dummy*` primitive is referenced** by any Run 101 code path; **no transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority** is introduced (the Run 050 trust-separation invariant is preserved and is now structurally separated into `pqc_transport_roots` vs `bundle_signing_authority_roots`); **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added**; **no source-code static MainNet root anchor exists** (grep audit on `crates/**/src/**` confirms only the new Run 101 type declarations and re-exports appear).

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4/C5-open.** Run 101 is a **fields + hash + boot-helper** step only. It does **not** implement the in-binary bundle-signing-key ratification verifier (Run 102), does **not** add `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` (Run 103), does **not** wire `verify_boot_time_genesis` from the release-binary `async_runner` startup (the helper is exposed and exercised through the public API the release binary links against, but the single startup call site is deferred to Run 102 alongside the ratification verifier — the existing T233 file-bytes `MainnetConfigError::ExpectedGenesisHashMissing` shield continues to enforce MainNet fail-closed at the CLI layer in the meantime), does **not** introduce KMS/HSM custody (Run 105), does **not** implement governance, does **not** implement validator-set rotation, does **not** add peer-driven live apply (Run 106+, gated by Run 100 spec §10), does **not** change the trust-bundle wire format or peer-candidate wire format, does **not** change consensus or KEMTLS, does **not** change `activation_epoch` semantics, does **not** introduce production static root anchors as source-code constants, does **not** add fallback roots or fallback signing keys, does **not** add any new dependency, does **not** add any new metric family or CLI flag, and does **not** weaken any existing signed-bundle / chain_id / environment / sequence anti-rollback / activation-height / `activation_epoch` / Run 065 minimum-margin / revocation / reload-check non-mutation / reload-apply ordering check. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on: bundle-signing-key ratification **verifier** (Run 102), authority-state **persistence and anti-rollback** (Run 103), release-binary rotation/revocation **evidence** (Run 104), **KMS/HSM custody** (Run 105), **peer-driven live apply** (Run 106+, gated by spec §10), in-binary / on-chain signing-key ratification, production fast-sync / broader consensus-storage restore, per-environment production trust-anchor operation, MainNet governance authorization path, the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke, `activation_epoch` runtime source (narrowed but still open per Run 099), peer-driven apply / propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and selective per-peer session retention. **C5 remains OPEN / unchanged** — Run 101 does not touch KEMTLS, consensus message wire formats, signature/verification semantics outside the genesis-hash domain, or any C5-relevant code path. Run 101 does **not** claim full C4 closure and does **not** claim C5 closure.

**Anchoring (Run 101).** The implementation is anchored in `crates/qbind-ledger/src/genesis.rs` (Run 101 section: `GenesisAuthorityRoot`, `GenesisAuthorityConfig`, `NetworkEnvironmentPolicy`, `GenesisAuthorityValidationError`, `BootGenesisVerificationError`, `BootGenesisVerification`, `compute_canonical_genesis_hash`, `verify_boot_time_genesis`, `CANONICAL_GENESIS_HASH_DOMAIN_V1`, `GENESIS_AUTHORITY_SUITE_ML_DSA_44`, `GENESIS_AUTHORITY_POLICY_VERSION_RUN_101`, the additive `GenesisConfig.authority` field with `#[serde(default)]`, `GenesisConfig::validate_for_environment`, and the `GenesisValidationError::AuthorityValidationFailed(_)` variant) and re-exported from `crates/qbind-ledger/src/lib.rs`. #### C4 Run 102 update (2026-05-21) — release-binary boot-time genesis verification WIRED + canonical `--print-genesis-hash` LANDED (closes the Run 101 evidence note's two release-binary gaps); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 102 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_102.md`) and the Run 102 update appended at §18 of `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` complete the **release-binary wiring step** of Run 101's helper into the production `qbind-node` startup sequence, per `task/RUN_102_TASK.txt`. Run 102 lands (a) the boot-time call site that invokes `qbind_ledger::verify_boot_time_genesis` from `qbind-node`'s `main` after T185 MainNet invariants validation and **before** trust-bundle / B3 restore / Run 069 reload-check / P2P / consensus startup, and (b) the canonical `--print-genesis-hash` operator surface (parsed-genesis canonical Run 101 hash; no raw-file-byte fallback). The bundle-signing-key ratification verifier remains Run 103 scope per the task's explicit "no broad redesign in Run 102" rule.

**What Run 102 narrows.** The C4 sub-piece "wire `verify_boot_time_genesis` from the release-binary startup" — which Run 101 left explicitly deferred ("the single startup call site is deferred to Run 102 alongside the ratification verifier") — is now **partial-positive**: (a) a new module `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_boot_genesis.rs` exposes `run_boot_time_genesis_verification(&NodeConfig)`, `compute_print_genesis_hash(&Path, NetworkEnvironmentPolicy)`, `map_environment(NetworkEnvironment) → NetworkEnvironmentPolicy`, and the typed `BootGenesisError` / `BootGenesisOutcome` returned from those calls; (b) `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` invokes the verifier at the spec-defined ordering position (after T185, before all of `[restore]` / `[metrics]` / `[binary]` / `[binary-consensus]` / `[snapshot]` log families — proven by the Scenario 8 stderr capture in `docs/devnet/run_102_genesis_verification_evidence/scenario_8_mainnet_happy_path.stderr.log`) and exits non-zero with a typed reason on any failure; (c) the existing T233 `MainnetConfigError::ExpectedGenesisHashMissing` shield in `validate_mainnet_invariants` is **preserved bit-for-bit** and now **composes** with the Run 102 verifier (the shield refuses MainNet startup when the flag is absent; Run 102 refuses when the flag's value does not match the parsed canonical hash; Run 102 also adds a belt-and-braces refusal for callers that bypass `--profile mainnet` and so escape the shield); (d) `--print-genesis-hash` now computes the **canonical Run 101 hash over the parsed `GenesisConfig`** under the resolved env policy and exits — replacing the pre-Run-101 raw-file-byte semantics and the Run 101 release-binary no-op; the printed value is the same `0x`-prefixed 64-char hex pasteable verbatim into `--expect-genesis-hash`; (e) the release-binary smoke evidence proves authority-only-diff causes a different canonical hash (Scenario 1 hash `0xc0bf6b82…9872` vs Scenario 2 hash `0x623a3c49…d43c` over two genesis files that differ only in one byte of `authority.bundle_signing_authority_roots[0].key_fingerprint`); (f) DevNet/TestNet embedded-genesis path is preserved — when `genesis_source.use_external == false` the verifier returns `SkippedNoExternalGenesis` with a clear log line (Scenario 9); (g) MainNet without `--genesis-path` is independently refused by Run 102 (belt-and-braces fail-closed even though T185/T232 also reject it) via `BootGenesisError::GenesisPathMissing { env: Mainnet }`; (h) **8 new in-module unit tests** in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_boot_genesis.rs::tests` and **14 new integration tests** in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_102_boot_genesis_wiring_tests.rs` cover all MainNet refusal scenarios (missing/mismatched/malformed expected hash, missing/empty/malformed authority, env/chain_id mismatch, missing/malformed genesis file, missing genesis path), the happy path, the print→expect operator round-trip, and DevNet preservation; (i) the existing Run 101 (11), T232 (7), T233 (16), and T237 (24) tests **remain green bit-for-bit**.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4/C5-open.** Run 102 is the **release-binary wiring** step only. It does **not** implement the in-binary bundle-signing-key ratification verifier (Run 103 — deferred per the task's explicit "no broad redesign in Run 102" rule; see Evidence Run 102 §9 and `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` §18.3), does **not** add `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` (Run 103), does **not** introduce KMS/HSM custody (Run 105), does **not** implement governance, does **not** implement signing-key rotation, does **not** implement signing-key revocation, does **not** implement validator-set rotation, does **not** add peer-driven live apply (Run 106+, gated by Run 100 spec §10), does **not** change the trust-bundle wire format or peer-candidate wire format, does **not** change consensus or KEMTLS, does **not** change `activation_epoch` semantics, does **not** introduce production static root anchors as source-code constants, does **not** add fallback roots or fallback signing keys, does **not** add any new dependency, does **not** add any new metric family, does **not** add any new CLI flag (the existing T232/T233 `--genesis-path` / `--print-genesis-hash` / `--expect-genesis-hash` surface is unchanged in identifier and structure; only the doc-comment help text is updated to describe the new canonical semantics), does **not** add any admin-API endpoint, does **not** add any filesystem watcher, does **not** add any network listener or gossip subscription/publisher, and does **not** weaken any existing signed-bundle / chain_id / environment / sequence anti-rollback / activation-height / `activation_epoch` / Run 065 minimum-margin / revocation / reload-check non-mutation / reload-apply ordering check. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on: bundle-signing-key ratification **verifier** (Run 103), authority-state **persistence and anti-rollback** (Run 103), release-binary rotation/revocation **evidence** (Run 104), **KMS/HSM custody** (Run 105), **peer-driven live apply** (Run 106+, gated by spec §10), in-binary / on-chain signing-key ratification, production fast-sync / broader consensus-storage restore, per-environment production trust-anchor operation, MainNet governance authorization path, the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke, `activation_epoch` runtime source (narrowed but still open per Run 099), peer-driven apply / propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and selective per-peer session retention. **C5 remains OPEN / unchanged** — Run 102 does not touch KEMTLS, consensus message wire formats, signature/verification semantics outside the genesis-hash domain, or any C5-relevant code path. Run 102 does **not** claim full C4 closure and does **not** claim C5 closure.

**Anchoring (Run 102).** The implementation is anchored in `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_boot_genesis.rs` (Run 102 module: `map_environment`, `load_external_genesis`, `run_boot_time_genesis_verification`, `compute_print_genesis_hash`, `format_for_operator`, `BootGenesisOutcome`, `BootGenesisError`), `crates/qbind-node/src/main.rs` (two new startup blocks: `--print-genesis-hash` early-exit and the boot-time verification call positioned after T185 and before B3/Run 069/P2P/consensus), `crates/qbind-node/src/cli.rs` (updated `print_genesis_hash` / `expect_genesis_hash` doc comments), and `crates/qbind-node/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod pqc_boot_genesis`). The tests are anchored at `crates/qbind-node/src/pqc_boot_genesis.rs::tests` (8 new) and `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_102_boot_genesis_wiring_tests.rs` (14 new). The release-binary smoke logs are at `docs/devnet/run_102_genesis_verification_evidence/{scenario_0_*.txt, scenario_1_*..scenario_9_*}.log` plus the fixtures `genesis_a.json`, `genesis_b_authority_only_diff.json`, `genesis_no_authority.json`, `genesis_malformed.json`. The evidence record is anchored at `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_102.md` (§1 investigation, §2 what was implemented including file table, §3 what was proven including all 10 scenarios and test counts, §4 key security decisions, §5 evidence references, §6 contradictions found = none, §7 explicit non-claims, §8 residual risks, §9 Run 103 candidate work / explicit ratification-verifier deferral, §10 verdict = partial-positive). The spec is anchored at `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` §18 (Run 102 update appended).

**No-fallback / no-mutation proof (Run 102).** No new dependency is introduced (no `Cargo.toml` change). No new metric family is added; no `/metrics` surface changes. No new CLI flag is added (the existing T232/T233 surface is preserved; only help text doc-comments are updated). No `Dummy*` primitive is referenced, re-activated, or made reachable on any new code path. No transport-root reuse as a bundle-signing authority is introduced (the Run 050 trust-separation invariant is preserved bit-for-bit). No `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback path is added. No production static MainNet root anchor is introduced as a source-code constant. Run 102 reads the authority block **only** from the operator-supplied genesis file; the release binary contains no compiled-in production `pqc_transport_root` or `bundle_signing_authority_root`. No Run 050–101 entry point is modified at the source or behavioural level — every one of those modules' public API signatures and existing test suites continues to pass on the Run 102 tree state (verified by `cargo test -p qbind-node --test run_101_genesis_authority_tests` = 11 pass, `--test t232_genesis_mainnet_profile_tests` = 7 pass, `--test t233_genesis_cli_tests` = 16 pass, `--test t237_mainnet_launch_profile_tests` = 24 pass; the only behavioural change is the additive Run 102 verifier call site in `main.rs` whose refusal scenarios are all proven). **No fabricated metric**, **no silent regression**, **no protocol behaviour change beyond the additive boot-time verification call site and the canonical `--print-genesis-hash` semantics swap**, **no removed tests**, **no `DummySig` / `DummyKem` / `DummyAead` fallback path introduced or strengthened**, **no classical signatures introduced**, **no `--p2p-trusted-root` fallback when `--p2p-trust-bundle` is absent**, **no admin-API / network listener added**, **no peer/gossip subscription added**, **no peer/gossip publisher added**, **no peer-driven live apply path introduced**, **no filesystem watcher added**, **no KMS/HSM custody surface added**, and **no private-key material referenced by any Run 102 code path, evidence statement, or runbook note** are introduced by Run 102.
#### C4 Run 103 update (2026-05-21) — minimal bundle-signing-key ratification VERIFIER LANDED (library-level; consumption boundary deferred to Run 104); full C4 still OPEN

DevNet Evidence Run 103 (`docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_103.md`) and the Run 103 update appended at §19 of `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` add the minimal bundle-signing-key ratification verifier primitive that Run 102 explicitly deferred. Run 103 implements **only the verifier**: a versioned, domain-separated `BundleSigningRatification` schema (`b"QBIND:BUNDLE-SIGNING-RATIFICATION:v1"`), a deterministic length-prefixed canonical preimage, and a typed `verify_bundle_signing_key_ratification(...)` API that fail-closes with one of 12 precise `RatificationFailure` reasons (`UnsupportedVersion`, `ChainMismatch`, `EnvironmentMismatch`, `GenesisHashMismatch`, `UnsupportedSuite`, `BundleSigningKeyFingerprintMismatch`, `MalformedBundleSigningPublicKey`, `MalformedSignature`, `UnknownAuthorityRoot`, `TransportRootNotAllowed`, `AuthorityRootSuiteMismatch`, `AuthorityKeyMaterialUnavailable`, `BadSignature`, `MissingAuthorityBlock`). PQC signature verification is delegated to the existing production `MlDsa44SignatureSuite` adapter (FIPS 204 / ML-DSA-44, suite id 100); no parallel crypto stack, no classical signatures, no dummy verifier on the production path. Authority-root lookup is restricted to `authority.bundle_signing_authority_roots`; entries in `pqc_transport_roots` are queried **only** to produce the precise `TransportRootNotAllowed` diagnostic and can never authorise a bundle-signing key.

**What Run 103 narrows.** Run 101 left this gap explicit ("Not yet consumed by any live ratification verifier — that is Run 102+ scope") and Run 102 deferred the verifier itself ("the in-binary bundle-signing-key ratification verifier (Run 103 — deferred per the task's explicit 'no broad redesign in Run 102' rule)"). Run 103 closes the *verifier primitive* sub-piece: (a) a new module `crates/qbind-ledger/src/bundle_signing_ratification.rs` exposes the schema, the canonical preimage / digest helpers, the typed verifier API, the 12 typed accept/reject reasons, the `RatifiedBundleSigningKey` success type, the `classify_authority_root_kind` diagnostic helper, the `pqc_public_key_fingerprint` convenience helper, and a feature-gated `test_helpers::build_signed_ratification` mint helper for tests; (b) the verifier reads authority roots exclusively from the runtime's parsed `GenesisConfig.authority.bundle_signing_authority_roots` (no source-code constants, no fallback list); (c) the verifier requires `signature_suite_id == GENESIS_AUTHORITY_SUITE_ML_DSA_44 (= 100)` and verifies via `MlDsa44SignatureSuite` (no parallel crypto path); (d) the canonical preimage is binary, length-prefixed, big-endian, and domain-separated, so no JSON map-order or whitespace ambiguity can affect the signed digest; (e) transport roots are explicitly refused as bundle-signing authorities — proven by `transport_root_rejected_as_bundle_signing_authority` (unit) and `run_103_scenario_5_transport_root_rejected` (integration); (f) when the genesis-bound root stores only a 64-hex SHA3-256 fingerprint (Run 101 allows this for DevNet/TestNet relaxation) the verifier returns the documented `AuthorityKeyMaterialUnavailable` boundary rather than faking verification — proven by `authority_root_with_only_short_fingerprint_returns_unavailable` (unit) and `run_103_scenario_7_authority_key_material_unavailable` (integration); (g) **19 new in-module unit tests** in `crates/qbind-ledger/src/bundle_signing_ratification.rs::tests` and **8 new integration tests** in `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_103_bundle_signing_ratification_tests.rs` cover schema/preimage determinism, every field's preimage sensitivity, authority lookup, transport-root separation, environment/chain/genesis-hash binding, suite-id allow-list, bundle-signing-key fingerprint self-consistency, malformed PK / signature lengths, bad-signature and mutated-preimage refusal, JSON round-trip + re-verification, and the authority key-material partial boundary; (h) the existing Run 101 (11), Run 102 (14), T232 (7), T233 (16), T237 (24), qbind-ledger lib (196), qbind-node lib (1090), and qbind-crypto lib (68) tests **remain green bit-for-bit** — Run 103 changes no existing genesis / boot-verification / trust-bundle / consensus / KEMTLS code path.

**What is NOT narrowed and what remains C4/C5-open.** Run 103 is the **verifier primitive** only. It does **not** wire `verify_bundle_signing_key_ratification` into any existing trust-bundle acceptance surface (Run 104 — startup load, reload-check, reload-apply, SIGHUP, peer-candidate validation, propagation all still consume locally-configured signing keys directly), does **not** add `<data_dir>/pqc_authority_state.json` (still Run 104), does **not** add a `RatifiedSigningKeyRegistry` cache, does **not** add anti-rollback for ratification objects (no `authority_sequence` field, no on-disk highest-seen-sequence — explicitly deferred to Run 104 per the task's "Strict non-goals" list), does **not** add an authority-key-material registry that resolves short fingerprints to full PKs (Run 104), does **not** introduce KMS/HSM custody (Run 105), does **not** implement signing-key rotation (Run 105+), does **not** implement signing-key revocation (Run 105+), does **not** implement governance, does **not** implement validator-set rotation, does **not** add peer-driven live apply (Run 106+, gated by Run 100 spec §10), does **not** change the trust-bundle wire format, does **not** change the peer-candidate wire format, does **not** change consensus or KEMTLS, does **not** change `activation_epoch` semantics, does **not** introduce production static root anchors as source-code constants, does **not** add fallback roots / signing keys, does **not** add any new dependency, does **not** add any new metric family, does **not** add any new CLI flag, does **not** add any admin-API endpoint, does **not** add any filesystem watcher, does **not** add any network listener or gossip subscription / publisher, and does **not** weaken any existing signed-bundle / chain_id / environment / sequence anti-rollback / activation-height / `activation_epoch` / Run 065 minimum-margin / revocation / reload-check non-mutation / Run 070 reload-apply ordering check. **Full C4 remains OPEN** on: bundle-signing-key ratification **consumption** in trust-bundle acceptance surfaces (Run 104), authority-state **persistence and anti-rollback** (Run 104), authority-key material registry (Run 104), release-binary rotation/revocation evidence (Run 105), **KMS/HSM custody** (Run 105), **peer-driven live apply** (Run 106+, gated by spec §10), production fast-sync / broader consensus-storage restore, per-environment production trust-anchor operation, MainNet governance authorization path, the N-node MainNet release-binary peer-connection smoke, `activation_epoch` runtime source (narrowed but still open per Run 099), peer-driven apply / propagation, admin-API / filesystem-watcher triggers, and selective per-peer session retention. **C5 remains OPEN / unchanged** — Run 103 does not touch KEMTLS, consensus message wire formats, signature/verification semantics outside the new `QBIND:BUNDLE-SIGNING-RATIFICATION:v1` domain, or any C5-relevant code path. Run 103 does **not** claim full C4 closure and does **not** claim C5 closure.

**Anchoring (Run 103).** The implementation is anchored in `crates/qbind-ledger/src/bundle_signing_ratification.rs` (Run 103 module: `BundleSigningRatification`, `RatificationEnvironment`, `canonical_ratification_preimage`, `canonical_ratification_digest`, `verify_bundle_signing_key_ratification`, `RatificationVerifierInputs`, `RatifiedBundleSigningKey`, `RatificationFailure`, `classify_authority_root_kind`, `pqc_public_key_fingerprint`, `test_helpers::build_signed_ratification`, `BUNDLE_SIGNING_RATIFICATION_DOMAIN_V1`, `BUNDLE_SIGNING_RATIFICATION_VERSION_V1`), `crates/qbind-ledger/src/lib.rs` (new Run 103 re-export block), `crates/qbind-ledger/Cargo.toml` (`features.test-helpers = []` — dev-only gate for the mint helper), `crates/qbind-node/Cargo.toml` (dev-dep on `qbind-ledger` with `features = ["test-helpers"]`). The tests are anchored at `crates/qbind-ledger/src/bundle_signing_ratification.rs::tests` (19 new) and `crates/qbind-node/tests/run_103_bundle_signing_ratification_tests.rs` (8 new). No release-binary smoke logs are produced because Run 103 adds no operator surface — the integration tests in `crates/qbind-node/tests/` exercise the verifier through the same `qbind_ledger::verify_bundle_signing_key_ratification` re-export the `qbind-node` binary links against, which is the appropriate release-binary-facing evidence shape for a verifier-primitive run. The evidence record is anchored at `docs/devnet/QBIND_DEVNET_EVIDENCE_RUN_103.md` (§1 investigation, §2 what was implemented, §3 what was proven incl. test coverage map, §4 key security decisions, §5 contradictions found = none, §6 evidence references, §7 explicit non-claims, §8 residual risks + Run 104 candidate work, §9 verdict = positive). The spec is anchored at `docs/protocol/QBIND_TRUST_ANCHOR_AUTHORITY_MODEL.md` §19 (Run 103 update appended). The runbook update is appended to `docs/ops/QBIND_PQC_TRUST_LIFECYCLE_RUNBOOK.md`.
